[001,01]	om namaḥ buddhāya vidhūta kalpanā jāla gambhīra udāra mūrtaye namaḥ samantabhadrāya samanta spharaṇa tviṣe prāyas prākṛta saktiḥ apratibala prajñaḥ janaḥ kevalam na anarthī eva su bhāṣitaiḥ parigataḥ vidveṣṭi api īrṣyā amalaiḥ tena ayam na para upakāraḥ iti naḥ cintā api cetas ciram sūkta abhyāsa vivardhita vyasanam iti atra anubaddha spṛham 
[001,08_001,12^1]	artha anartha vivecanasya anumāna āśraya tvāt tad vipratipatteḥ tad vyavasthāpanāya āha pakṣa dharmaḥ tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ hetuḥ tridhā eva saḥ avinā abhāva niyamāt hetvābhāsāḥ tatas apare pakṣaḥ dharmī avayave samudāya upacārāt prayojana abhāvāt anupacāraḥ iti ced na sarva dharmi dharma pratiṣedha artha tvāt tad eka deśa tvāt tad upacāra yogya dharmi dharma pratipatti artham tathā ca cākṣuṣa tva ādi parihāraḥ dharma vacanena api dharmya āśraya siddhau dharmi grahaṇa sāmarthyāt pratyāsattyā sādhya dharmi siddhiḥ iti ced na dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇaḥ api pratyāsatteḥ tad aṃśa vyāptyā dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇi sattva siddheḥ dharmi vacanāt sādhya dharmi parigrahaḥ siddhe punar vacanam niyama artham āśaṅkyeta sajātīyaḥ eva sattvam iti siddhe api vijātīya vyatireke sādhya abhāve asattva vacana vat 
[001,12^2]	sāmarthyāt artha gatau pratipatti gaurava parihāra artham ca pakṣa vacanam pakṣasya dharma tve tad viśeṣaṇa apekṣasya anyatra ananuvṛtteḥ asādhāraṇa tā iti ced na ayoga vyavacchedena viśeṣaṇāt yathā caitraḥ dhanurdharaḥ na anya yoga vyavacchedena yathā pārthaḥ dhanurdharaḥ iti ākṣepsyāmaḥ tad aṃśaḥ tad dharmaḥ vaktuḥ abhiprāya vaśāt na tad eka deśaḥ pakṣa śabdena samudāyā vacanāt vyāptiḥ vyāpakasya tatra bhāvaḥ eva vyāpyasya vā tatra eva bhāvaḥ etena avayava vyatirekau yathāsvam pramāṇena niścitau uktau pakṣa dharmaḥ ca te ete kārya svabhāva anupalabdhi lakṣaṇāḥ trayaḥ hetavaḥ yathā agniḥ atra dhūmāt 
[001,12^3]	vṛkṣaḥ ayam śiṃśapā tvāt pradeśa viśeṣe kvacid na ghaṭaḥ upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdheḥ yadi syāt upalabdhi asattvaḥ eva syāt na anyathā tena upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta sattvasya iti uktam bhavati tatra dvau vastu sādhanau ekaḥ pratiṣedha hetuḥ svabhāva pratibandhe hi sati arthaḥ artham na vyabhicarati sa ca tad ātma tvāt tad ātma tve sādhya sādhana bheda abhāvaḥ iti ced na dharma bheda parikalpanāt iti vakṣyāmaḥ tathā ca āha sarve eva ayam anumāna anumeya vyavahāraḥ buddhi ārūḍhena dharma dharmi bhedena iti bhedaḥ dharma dharmitayā buddhi ākāra kṛtaḥ na arthaḥ api vikalpa bhedānām sva tantrāṇām anartha āśraya tvāt 
[001,12^4]	tad kalpita viṣayāt artha pratītau anartha pratilambhaḥ eva syāt kāryasya api svabhāva pratibandhaḥ tad svabhāvasya tad utpatteḥ iti etau dvau anumeya pratyayau sākṣāt anutpatteḥ atad pratibhāsi tve api tad utpatteḥ tat vyabhicāriṇau iti pramāṇam pratyakṣa vat pratyakṣasya api hi artha avyabhicāraḥ eva prāmāṇyam tad abhāve bhāvinaḥ tad vipralambhāt avyabhicāraḥ ca anyasya kaḥ anyaḥ tad utpatteḥ anāyatta rūpāṇām sahabhāva niyama abhāvāt yadi tad utpatteḥ kāryam gamakam sarvathā gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ sarvathā janya janaka bhāvāt na tad abhāve bhavataḥ tad utpatti niyama abhāvāt tasmāt 
[003,13_004,02]	kāryam svabhāvaiḥ yāvadbhiḥ avinābhāvi kāraṇe teṣām hetuḥ tad kāryatva niyamāt taiḥ eva dharmaiḥ ye taiḥ vinā na bhavati aṃśena janya janaka tva prasaṅgaḥ iti ced na tad janya viśeṣa grahaṇe abhimata tvāt liṅga viśeṣa upādhīnām ca sāmānyānām aviśiṣṭa sāmānya vivakṣāyām vyabhicārāt naḥ iṣyate svabhāve bhāvaḥ api bhāva mātra anurodhini hetuḥ iti vartate tādātmyam hi arthasya tanmātra anurodhini eva na anyāḥ āyatte tad bhāve abhūtasya paścāt bhāva niyama abhāvāt kāraṇānām kārya vyabhicārāt 
[004,05_004,13]	apravṛttiḥ pramāṇānām anupalabdhiḥ apravṛtti phalā asati sat jñāna śabda vyavahāra pratiṣedha phalā upalabdhi pūrvaka tvāt teṣām iti idam sat asat pratiṣedha vidhi hetvoḥ tulyam rūpam tathā hi sattvam upalabdhiḥ eva vastu yogya tā lakṣaṇā tad āśrayā vā jñāna pravṛttiḥ tatas sat jñāna śabda vyavahāra vṛtteḥ asatām ca asattvam anupalabdhiḥ asajjñānaphalā kācid hetu bheda vyapekṣayā 
[004,14^1]	hetuḥ anupalabdhiḥ bhedaḥ asyāḥ viśeṣaṇam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta sattvam atra anupalabdheḥ liṅgāt asattāyām upalabdheḥ abhāvaḥ api anyayā anupalabdhyā sādhyaḥ iti anavasthānāt apratipattiḥ syāt atha upalabdhi abhāvaḥ vinā anupalabdhyā syāt tathā sattā abhāvaḥ api syāt apārthikā anupalabdhiḥ atha anya upalabdhyā anupalabdhi siddhiḥ iti pratyakṣa siddhāḥ anupalabdhiḥ tathā anya sattayā asattā kim na sidhyati iti yadā punar evaṃvidhāḥ anupalabdhiḥ eva asatām asattā tadā siddhe api viṣaye mohāt viṣayiṇaḥ asat jñāna śabda vyavahārān apratipadyamānaḥ viṣaya pradarśanena samaye pravartyate 
[004,14^2]	yathā gauḥ ayam sāsnādi samudāya ātmaka tvāt iti tathā ca dṛṣṭānta asiddhi codanāḥ api prativyūḍhā viṣaya pratipattau api apratipanna viṣayīṇām darśanāt evam anayoḥ anupalabdhyoḥ sva viparyaya hetvabhāva bhāvābhyām sat vyavahāra pratiṣedha phala tvam tulyam ekatra saṃśayāt anyatra viparyayāt tatra ādyā sat vyavahāra niṣedha upayogāt pramāṇam uktā na tu vyatireka darśana ādau upayujyate saṃśayāt dvitīyā tu atra pramāṇam niścaya phala tvāt 
[005,06_005,09^1]	sā ca prayoga bhedāt viruddha kāryayoḥ siddhiḥ asiddhiḥ hetu bhāvayoḥ dṛśya ātmanoḥ abhāva artha anupalabdhiḥ caturvidhā yāvān kaścid pratiṣedhaḥ sa sarvaḥ anupalabdheḥ tathā hi sa dvidhā kriyeta kasyacid vidhinā niṣedhena vā vidhau viruddhaḥ vā vidhīyeta aviruddhaḥ vā aviruddhasya vidhau sahabhāva virodha abhāvāt apratiṣedhaḥ viruddhasya api anupalabdhi abhāvena virodha apratipattiḥ tathā hi aparyanta kāraṇasya bhavataḥ anya bhāve abhāvāt virodha gatiḥ sa ca anupalabdheḥ anyonya upalabdhi parihāra sthita lakṣaṇa tā vā virodhaḥ nitya anitya tva vat tatra api eka upalabdhyā anya anupalabdhiḥ eva ucyate anyathā aniṣiddha upalabdheḥ abhāva asiddheḥ ekasya niṣedhena anya abhāva sādhane siddhāḥ eva anupalabdhiḥ niṣedhasya anupalabdhi rūpa tvāt tatra api artha antara niṣedhe kārya kāraṇayoḥ anubhavasya vā tatra anubhavasya apratibandhāt tad abhāve anyena na bhavitavyam iti kutas etat kārya anupalabdhau api na avaśyam kāraṇāḥ api tadvanti bhavanti iti tad abhāvaḥ kutas 
[005,09^2]	tasmāt kāraṇa anupalabdhiḥ eva abhāvam gamayati iti svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ tu svayam asattā eva tatra kevalam viṣayī sādhyate asyām api yadā vyāpaka dharma anupalabdhyā vyāpya abhāvam āha tadā abhāvaḥ api iti iyam pratiṣedha viṣaya anupalabdhiḥ prayoga bhedena caturdhā bhavati viruddha siddhyā yathā na śīta sparśaḥ atra agneḥ etena vyāpaka viruddha siddhiḥ uktāḥ veditavyā yathā na tuṣāra sparśaḥ atra agneḥ viruddha kārya siddhyā yathā na śīta sparśaḥ atra dhūmāt hetu asiddhyā yathā na atra dhūmaḥ anagneḥ svabhāva asiddhyāḥ yathā na atra dhūmaḥ anupalabdheḥ etena vyāpaka svabhāvā siddheḥ uktāḥ yathā na atra śiṃśapā vṛkṣa abhāvāt sarvatra ca asyām abhāva sādhanyām anupalabdhau dṛśya ātmanām eva teṣām tad viruddhānām ca siddhiḥ asiddhiḥ ca veditavyā anyeṣām abhāva virodha asiddheḥ yadi viruddha kārya upalabdhyā api abhāva siddhiḥ tad kāraṇa upalabdhyā kim na sidhyati 
[006,11_006,13]	tad viruddha nimittasya yā upalabdhiḥ prayujyate nimittayoḥ viruddha tva abhāve sā vyabhicāriṇī yathā na śīta sparśaḥ atra kāṣṭhāt iti nimittayoḥ punar virodhe gamikāḥ eva yathā na asya romaharṣa ādi viśeṣāḥ santi saṃnihita dahana viśeṣa tvāt etena tat kāryāt api tad viruddha kārya abhāva gatiḥ uktāḥ veditavyā yathā na roma harṣa ādi viśeṣa yukta puruṣavān ayam pradeśaḥ dhūmāt iyam ca hetu asiddhyā eva tad viruddha siddhiḥ prāk eva nirdiṣṭāḥ iti iyam prayoga bhedāt aṣṭadhā anupalabdhiḥ tatra yā iyam viruddha kārya upalabdhiḥ uktā tatra
[006,20_006,24]	iṣṭam viruddha kārye api deśa kāla ādi apekṣaṇam anyathā vyabhicāri syāt bhasmāḥ iva aśīta sādhane yaḥ tarhi samagreṇa hetunā kārya utpādaḥ anumīyate sa katham trividhe hetau antarbhavati hetunā yaḥ samagreṇa kārya utpādaḥ anumīyate artha antara anapekṣa tvāt sa svabhāvaḥ anuvarṇitaḥ 
[006,26_007,03]	asau api yathā asaṃnihitāt na anyam apekṣate iti tanmātra anubandhī svabhāvaḥ bhāvasya tatra hi kevalam samagrāt kāraṇāt kārya utpatti sambhavaḥ anumīyate samagrāṇām kārya utpādana yogya tā anumānāt yogyatā ca sāmagrī mātra anubandhinī iti svabhāva bhūtāḥ eva anumīyate kim punar kāraṇam sāmagryāḥ kāryam eva na anumīyate sāmagrī phala śaktīnām pariṇāma anubandhini anaikāntika tā kārye pratibandhasya sambhavāt 
[007,05]	na hi samagrāṇi iti eva kāraṇa dravyāṇi sva kāryam janayanti sāmagrī janmanām śaktīnām pariṇāma apekṣa tvāt kārya utpādasya atra antare ca pratibandha sambhavān na kārya anumānam yogyatāyāḥ tu dravya antara anapekṣa tvāt na virudhyate anumānam uttarottara śakti pariṇāmena kārya utpādana samarthāḥ iyam kāraṇa sāmagrī śakti pariṇāma pratyayasya anyasya apekṣaṇīyasya abhāvāt iti pūrvasajāti mātra hetu tvāt śakti prasūteḥ sāmagryā yogyatā ananya apekṣiṇī iti ucyate yā tarhi akārya kāraṇa bhūtena anyena rasa ādinā rūpa ādi gatiḥ sā katham sā api
[007,14_007,20]	eka sāmagrī adhīnasya rūpa ādeḥ asataḥ gatiḥ hetu dharma anumānena dhūma indhana vikāra vat tatra hetuḥ eva tathābhūtaḥ anumīyate pravṛtta śakti rūpa upādāna kāraṇa sahakāri pratyayaḥ hi rasa hetuḥ rasam janayati indhana vikāra viśeṣa upādāna hetu sahakāri pratyaya agni dhūma janana vat tathā hi śakti pravṛttyā 
[007,21_008,06]	sva kāraṇasya phala utpādanam prati ābhi mukhyena na vinā rasaḥ saḥ eva anya kāraṇam rūpa upādāna hetūnām pravṛtti kāraṇam sā api rasa upādāna kāraṇa pravṛttiḥ rūpa upādāna kāraṇa pravṛtti sahakāriṇī tasmāt yathābhūtāt hetoḥ rasaḥ utpannaḥ tathābhūtam anumāpayan rūpam anumāpayati iti tatra api
[008,07_008,12]	 atīta ekaikālānām gati s na anāgatānām vyabhicārāt tat tasmāt iyam kārya liṅga jā tena na anyaḥ hetuḥ gamakaḥ asti apratibaddha svabhāvasya avinā abhāva niyama abhāvāt etena pipīlika utsaraṇa matsya vikāra ādeḥ varṣa ādi anumānam uktam tatra api bhūta pariṇāmaḥ eva varṣa hetuḥ pipīlikā ādi saṃkṣobha ādi hetuḥ iti 
[008,16_009,01]	hetunā tu asamagreṇa yat kāryam anumīyate śeṣavat tat asāmarthyāt dehāt rāga anumāna vat samagrāṇi eva hi kāraṇāni yogyatām api anumāpayanti asamagrasya ekānta asāmarthyāt yathā deha indriya buddhibhyaḥ rāga ādi anumānam ātma ātmīya abhiniveśa pūrvakāḥ hi rāga ādayaḥ ayoni śoma naskāra pūrvaka tvāt sarva doṣa utpatteḥ deha ādīnām hetu tve api na kevalānām sāmarthyam asti iti vipakṣa vṛtteḥ adṛṣṭau api śeṣavat anumānāt saṃśayaḥ tathā vipakṣe adṛṣṭi mātreṇa kārya sāmānya darśanāt hetu jñānam pramāṇa ābham vacanāt rāgita ādi vat 
[009,03^1]	na hi rāga ādīnām eva kāryam spandana vacana ādayaḥ vaktu kāma tā sāmānya hetutvāt saḥ eva rāgaḥ iti ced iṣṭa tvāt na kiṃcid bādhitam syāt nitya sukha ātma ātmīya darśana ākṣiptam sa āsrava dharma viṣayam cetasaḥ abhiṣvaṅgam rāgam āhuḥ na evam karuṇā ādayaḥ anyathā api sambhavāt iti nivedayiṣyāmaḥ atra yathā raktaḥ bravīti tathā viraktaḥ api iti vacana mātrāt apratipattiḥ na api viśeṣāt abhiprāyasya durbodha tvāt vyavahāra saṃkareṇa sarveṣām vyabhicārāt prayojana abhāvāt avyāhāraḥ iti ced na parārtha tvāt na yuktaḥ vīta rāga tvāt iti ced na karuṇāḥ api vṛtteḥ saḥ eva rāgaḥ iti ced iṣṭam aviparyāsa samudbhavān na doṣaḥ asatī api ātma grahe duḥkha viśeṣa darśana mātreṇa abhyāsa bala utpādinī bhavati eva karuṇā tathā hi sattva dharma ādi ālambanāḥ maitrī ādayaḥ iṣyante etāḥ ca sajātīya abhyāsa vṛttayaḥ na rāga apekṣiṇyaḥ na evam rāga ādayaḥ viparyāsa abhāve abhāvāt kāruṇikasya api niṣphalaḥ ārambhaḥ aviparyāsāt iti ced na para arthasya eva phala tvena iṣṭa tvāt 
[009,03^2]	icchā lakṣaṇa tvāt phalasya sarvathā abhūta asamāropāt nirdoṣaḥ tad anyena doṣavat tva sādhane na kiṃcid aniṣṭam vaktari ātmani rāga ādi darśanena anyatra tad anumāne ati prasaṅgaḥ vyabhicārāt ananya anumāne iha avyabhicāraḥ iti kaḥ niścayaḥ karaṇa guṇa vaktu kāmate hi vacanam anumāpayet rāga utpādana yogya tā ra hite vacana adarśanāt tad anumāne atiprasaṅgaḥ uktaḥ rāgasya anupayoge katham tat śaktiḥ upayujyate śakti upayoge hi saḥ eva upayuktaḥ syāt tat ca na asti iti uktam tasmāt na antarīyakam eva kāryam kāraṇam anumāpayati tad pratibandhāt na anyat vipakṣe adarśane api sarva darśinaḥ hi darśana vyāvṛttiḥ sarvatra abhāvam gamayet kvacid tathā dṛṣṭānām api deśa kāla saṃskāra bhedena anyathā adarśanāt yathā āmalakyaḥ kṣīra avasekena madhura phalāḥ bhavanti na ca evam bahulam dṛśyante tena evam syāt yuktam vaktum mādṛśaḥ vaktā rāgī iti rāga utpatti pratyaya viśeṣeṇa ātma darśana ayoni śoma naskāreṇa yogāt tadā api apārthakaḥ vacana udāhāraḥ tasmāt vipakṣe adṛṣṭiḥ ahetuḥ 
[010,13_010,15]	na ca adarśana mātreṇa vipakṣe avyabhicāritā sambhāvya vyabhicāra tvāt sthālī taṇḍula pāka vat na hi bahulam pakva darśane api sthālī antar gamana mātreṇa pākaḥ sidhyati vyabhicāra darśanāt evam tu syāt evam svabhāvāḥ etad samāna pāka hetavaḥ pakvāḥ iti anyathā tu śeṣavat etat anumānam vyabhicāri kim punar etat śeṣavat 
[010,19_010,21]	yasya adarśana mātreṇa vyatirekaḥ pradarśyate tasya saṃśaya hetu tvāt śeṣavat tat udāhṛtam sa tasya vyatirekaḥ na niścitaḥ iti vipakṣe vṛttiḥ āśaṅkyeta vyatireka sādhanasya adarśana mātrasya saṃśaya hetutvāt na sarva an upalabdhiḥ gamikā tasmāt eka nivṛttyā anya nivṛttim icchatā tayoḥ kaścid svabhāva pratibandhaḥ api eṣṭavyaḥ anyathā agamakaḥ hetuḥ syāt 
[010,26_010,28]	hetoḥ triṣu api rūpeṣu niścayaḥ tena varṇitaḥ asiddha viparīta artha vyabhicāri vipakṣataḥ na hi asati pratibandhe anvaya vyatireka niścayaḥ asti tena tam eva darśayan niścayam āha tatra anvayasya niścayena viruddha tat pakṣyāṇām nirāsaḥ vyatirekasya anaikāntikasya tad pakṣasya ca śeṣavat ādeḥ dvayoḥ iti eka siddha pratiṣedhaḥ prasiddha vacanena sandigdhayoḥ śeṣa vat asādhāraṇayoḥ sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ api 
[011,05_011,12]	anyathā hi asati pratibandhe adarśana mātreṇa vyatireke vyabhicāri vipakṣeṇa vaidharmya vacanam ca yat yat āha eṣa tāvat nyāyaḥ yat ubhayam vaktavyam viruddha anaikāntika pratipakṣeṇa iti vaidharmya vacanam anaikāntika pratipakṣeṇa yadi adṛṣṭi phalam tat ca yadi tena vipakṣe adarśanam khyāpyate tat anukte api gamyate 
[011,13_012,06]	na hi tasya prāk darśana bhrāntiḥ yā vacanena nivartyeta smṛtiḥ vācā darśane kriyate iti ced darśanam khalu apratīyamānam anaṅgam iti yuktam tatra smaraṇa ādhānam adarśanam tu darśana abhāvaḥ sa darśanena bādhyate tad abhāve tu siddhaḥ eva iti apārthakam tad siddhaye vacanam na vai anupalambhamānasya tāvatā na asti iti bhavati tad artham vacanam iti ced na ca na asti iti vacanāt tat na asti eva yathā yadi na asti sa khyāpyate nyāyaḥ tadā na asti iti gamyate 
[012,08_012,15]	yadi anupalabhamānaḥ na asti iti na pratyeti vacanāt api naḥ eva pratyeṣyati tat api hi anupalambham eva khyāpayati na ca eka anupalambhaḥ anya abhāvam sādhayati atiprasaṅgāt na ca tena na asti iti vacanāt tathā bhavati atiprasaṅgāt tat katham vaidharmya vacanena anaikāntika parihāraḥ tasmāt vyāvṛttim icchatā tatra nyāyaḥ vaktavyaḥ yatas asya vyāvṛttam iti bhavati nanu tad abhāve anupalambhāt siddhā vyāvṛttiḥ yadi adṛṣṭyā nivṛttiḥ syāt śeṣavat vyabhicāri kim 
[012,16_013,01]	yathā pakvāni etāni phalāni evaṃrasāni vā rūpa aviśeṣāt eka śākhā prabhava tvāt vā upayukta vat iti atra api vivakṣita aśeṣa pakṣīkaraṇe hetoḥ sādhya abhāve anupalambhaḥ asti iti katham vyabhicāraḥ pratyakṣa bādha āśaṅkā vyabhicāraḥ iti eke na pakṣīkṛta viṣaye abhāvāt kadācid bhavet iti ced tathā śaṅkāyām atiprasaṅgaḥ anyatra api abhāva niyama abhāvāt vṛttam pramāṇam bādhakam avṛtta bādhane sarvatra anāśvāsaḥ vyatirekaḥ tu siddhaḥ eva sādhanam iti tathā abhāva niścayam apekṣate anupalambhāt tu kvacid abhāva siddhau api apratibaddhasya tad abhāve sarvatra abhāva asiddheḥ saṃśayāt avyatirekaḥ vyabhicāraḥ śeṣavataḥ kim ca vyatireki api hetuḥ syāt 
[013,02]	na idam nirātmakam jīvat śarīram aprāṇa ādimattva prasaṅgāt iti nirātmakeṣu ghaṭa ādiṣu dṛṣṭeṣu prāṇa ādi adarśanāt tad nivṛtti ātma gatiḥ syāt adṛśya anupalambhāt abhāva asiddhau ghaṭa ādīnām nairātmya asiddheḥ prāṇa ādeḥ anivṛttiḥ abhyupagamāt siddham iti ced katham idānīm ātma siddhiḥ parasya api apramāṇikā katham nairātmya siddhiḥ abhyupagamena ca sa ātmakān ātmakau vibhajya tatra abhāvena gamaka tvam kathayatā āgamika tvam ātmani pratipannam syāt na anumeya tvam tasmāt adarśane api ātmanaḥ nivṛtti asiddheḥ tad nivṛttau kvacid nivṛttau api prāṇa ādīnām apratibandhāt sarvatra nivṛttya siddheḥ agamaka tvam yā api asiddhi yojanā tathā sa pakṣe san asan iti evamādiṣu api yathāyogam udāharyam iti evamādikā sā api
[013,14_013,15]	 na vācyāḥ asiddhi yojanā anupalambhaḥ eva saṃśayāt upalambhe tad abhāvāt anupalambhāt ca vyatirekaḥ iti saṃśayitaḥ anivāryaḥ syāt yathāyoga vacanāt anivāritaḥ eva iti ced na yaḥ eva tu ubhaya niścita vācī iti ādi vacanāt tena anupalambhe api saṃśayāt anivṛttim manyamānaḥ tat pratiṣedham āha kim ca 
[014,01_014,02]	viśeṣasya vyavaccheda hetu tā syāt adarśanāt śrāvaṇa tvasya api nitya anityayoḥ adarśanāt vyāvṛttiḥ iti tad vyavaccheda hetu tā syāt na hi tad vyāvṛtteḥ anyat vyavacchedanam avyavacchedaḥ tu kutaścid vyāvṛtteḥ eva aniścayāt yaḥ hi yatra na asti iti niścitaḥ sa bhavan tad abhāvam katham na gamayet 
[014,06_014,12]	pramāṇa antara bādhā ced atha api syāt ubhaya vyavacchede pramāṇa antaram bādhakam asti anyonya vyavaccheda rūpāṇām eka vyavacchedena anya vidhānāt apratiṣedhaḥ vidhi pratiṣedhayoḥ virodhāt na idānīm na astitāḥ adṛśaḥ na evam adarśanam pramāṇam bādhā sambhavāt tathā anyatra api sambhāvyam pramāṇa antara bādhanam 
[014,13_014,19]	lakṣaṇa yukte bādhā sambhave tad lakṣaṇam eva dūṣitam syāt iti sarvatra anāśvāsaḥ anumāna viṣaye api pratyakṣa anumāna virodha darśanāt anāśvāsa prasaṅgaḥ iti ced na yathā ukte asambhavāt sambhavinaḥ ca atad lakṣaṇa tvāt viruddha avi abhicārya vacanam iti ced anumāna viṣaye avacanāt iṣṭam viṣayam ca asya nivedayiṣyāmaḥ kim ca dṛṣṭā ayuktiḥ adṛṣṭeḥ ca syāt sparśasya avirodhinī 
[014,20_015,09]	yadi hi anupalambhena abhāvaḥ sidhyet yat āha yadi adarśana mātreṇa dṛṣṭebhyaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate na ca saḥ api yuktaḥ iti katham ayuktaḥ anupalambhāt abhāva siddheḥ nanu upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpteḥ sparśasya yuktaḥ eva pratiṣedhaḥ na yuktaḥ dṛśya tad svabhāva viṣaya mātrā pratiṣedhāt pṛthivī ādi sāmānyena gṛhītvā ayam pratiṣedham āha tatra ca tūla upala pallava ādiṣu tad bhāve api sparśa bheda darśanāt asya api kvacid viśeṣe sambhava āśaṅkayā bhavitavyam iti sarvatra adarśana mātreṇa ayuktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ iti evam ācāryīyaḥ kaścid anupalambhāt abhāvam bruvāṇaḥ upālabdhaḥ api ca deśa ādi bhedāt dṛśyante bhinnāḥ dravyeṣu śaktayaḥ tatra eka dṛṣṭyā na anyatra yuktaḥ tad bhāva niścayaḥ 
[015,11^1]	yadi kathaṃcid vipakṣe adarśana mātreṇa apratibaddhasya api tat avyabhicāraḥ kvacid deśe kānicid dravyāṇi kathaṃcid dṛṣṭāni punar anyathā anyatra dṛśyante yathā kāścid oṣadhayaḥ kṣetra viśeṣe viśiṣṭa rasa vīrya vipākāḥ bhavanti na anyatra tathā kāla saṃskāra bhedāt na ca tad deśaiḥ tathā dṛṣṭāḥ iti sarvāḥ tattvena tathābhūtāḥ sidhyanti guṇa antarāṇām kāraṇa antara apekṣa tvāt viśeṣa hetu abhāve tu syāt anumānam yathā adṛṣṭa kartṛkam api vākyam puruṣa saṃskāra pūrvakam iti vākyeṣu viśeṣa abhāvāt sarva prakārāṇām puruṣaiḥ karaṇasya darśanāt na evam asambhavat viśeṣa hetavaḥ puruṣāḥ yena vacana ādeḥ kiṃcid mātra sādharmyāt sarva ākāra sāmyam anumīyeta sarva guṇeṣu viśeṣa darśanāt 
[015,11^2]	saṃskāra bhedena viśeṣa pratipatteḥ tadvat anyasya api sambhavāt asambhava anumāne ca bādhaka hetu abhāvāt vairāgya adṛṣṭeḥ adṛṣṭena ca bādhya bādhaka bhāva asiddheḥ rāga ādi avyabhicāri kārya abhāvāt sambhave api viśeṣāṇām draṣṭum aśakya tvāt tādṛśām ca apratikṣepa artha tvāt na evam vākyāni dṛśya viśeṣa tvāt adṛśya tve api adṛṣṭa viśeṣāṇām vijātīyatva upagama virodhāt tad viśeṣāṇām anyatra api śakya kriya tvāt pratyakṣāṇām śabdānām apratyakṣa svabhāva abhāvāt bhrānti nimitta abhāvāt bādhaka abhāvāt bhrāntyasiddheḥ puruṣeṣu viśeṣa darśanasya bādhaka tvāt asamānam para bhāva bhūtasya ca vākya viśeṣasya atad viśeṣa tvāt tat abhinna svabhāvānām sarveṣām puruṣa kriyā na vā kasyacid kim ca 
[016,09_016,11^1]	ātma mṛd cetana ādīnām yaḥ abhāvasya aprasādhakaḥ saḥ eva anupalambhaḥ kim hetvabhāvasya sādhakaḥ anupalambham ca asya pramāṇayataḥ ātma vādaḥ nirālambaḥ syāt apratyakṣa tvāt ātmanaḥ tad kārya asiddheḥ indriya ādīnām tu vijñāna kāryasya kādācid ka tvāt sa apekṣya siddhyā prasiddhiḥ ucyate kim api asya kāraṇam asti iti ca tu evaṃbhūtam iti na evam sukha ādi kāryam prasādhitam kaṃcid artham puṣṇāti yena kenacid kāraṇavat tva abhyupagamāt tathā ca anupalambhaḥ eva ātmanaḥ syāt tam tena pratyācakṣāṇaḥ kim iti prativyūḍhaḥ anupalambhasya asādhana tvāt iti katham asādhanam vyatirekam sādhayet 
[016,11^2]	mṛdaḥ khalu api kaścid caitanyam anupalabhyamānam api icchan adarśanāt vacana ādeḥ vyāvṛttim āha dadhi ādikam ca aparaḥ kṣīra ādiṣu apara artheṣu saṃghāta tva adarśanāt vyatirekam kaḥ hi atra niyamaḥ saṃhataiḥ avaśyam para arthaiḥ bhavitavyam iti asti eva upalambhaḥ dadhi ādīnām kṣīra ādiṣu anumānam aśaktāt anutpatteḥ atha kā iyam śaktiḥ saḥ eva bhāvaḥ uta anyat eva kiṃcid saḥ eva ced tathā eva upalabhyeta viśeṣa abhāvāt anyat ced katham anya bhāve tat asti upacāra mātram tu syāt iti ayam eṣām paraspara vyāghātaḥ 
[016,28_017,04]	tasmāt tanmātra sambandhaḥ svabhāvaḥ bhāvam eva vā nivartayet yathā vṛkṣaḥ śiṃśapām śākhā ādimat viśeṣasya eva kasyacid tathā aprasiddheḥ sa tasya svabhāvaḥ svam ca svabhāvam parityajya katham bhāvaḥ bhavet svabhāvasya eva bhāva tvāt iti tasya svabhāva pratibandhāt avyabhicāraḥ kāraṇam vā kāryam avyabhicārataḥ 
[017,05_017,08]	kāraṇam nivartamānam kāryam nivartayati anyathā tat tasya kāryam eva na syāt siddhaḥ tu kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ svabhāvam niyamayati iti ubhayathā svabhāva pratibandhāt eva nivṛttiḥ anyathā eka nivṛttyā anya vinivṛttiḥ katham bhavet na aśvavān iti martyena na bhāvyam gamatā api kim saṃnidhānāt tathā ekasya katham anyasya saṃnidhiḥ gomān iti eva martyena bhāvyam aśvavatāḥ api kim 
[017,12_017,18]	tasmāt svabhāva pratibandhāt eva hetuḥ sādhyam gamayati sa ca tad bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ tad utpatti lakṣaṇaḥ vā saḥ eva avinā abhāvaḥ dṛṣṭāntābhyām pradarśyate tasmāt vaidharmya dṛṣṭānte na iṣṭaḥ avaśyam iha āśrayaḥ tad abhāve ca tat naḥ iti vacanāt api tad gateḥ yatas tad bhāva hetu bhāvau hi dṛṣṭānte tad avedinaḥ khyāpyete 
[017,20]	dṛṣṭānte hi sādhya dharmasya tad bhāvaḥ tanmātra anubandhena tad svabhāvatayā khyāpyate yaḥ kṛtakam svabhāvam janayati saḥ anitya svabhāvam santam janayati iti pramāṇam dṛṣṭāntena upadarśyate anyathā eka dharma sadbhāvāt tad anyena api bhavitavyam iti niyama abhāvāt sādhanasya sādhya vyabhicāra āśaṅkā syāt tena ca pramāṇena sādhya dharmasya tanmātra anubandhaḥ khyāpyate sva kāraṇāt eva kṛtakaḥ tathābhūtaḥ jātaḥ yaḥ naśvaraḥ kṣaṇa sthitaḥ dharmā anyatas tasya tad bhāva niṣedhāt hetu bhāvaḥ vā tasmin sati eva bhāvāt iti dṛṣṭāntena pradarśyate artha antarasya tathā prasiddhe tad bhāve hetu bhāve vā anitya tva abhāve kṛtaka tvam na bhavati dahana abhāve ca dhūmaḥ tathā hi sa tasya svabhāvaḥ hetuḥ vā katham svam svabhāvam hetum vā antareṇa bhavet iti āśrayam antareṇa api vaidharmya dṛṣṭānte prasidhyati vyatirekaḥ yeṣām punar prasiddhau eva tad bhāva hetu bhāvau teṣām
[018,09_018,15]	 viduṣām vācyaḥ hetuḥ eva hi kevalaḥ yad arthe dṛṣṭāntaḥ ucyate saḥ arthaḥ siddhaḥ iti kim tad vacanena tadā tad pradarśane api kim vaidharmya dṛṣṭānta āśrayeṇa iti manyamānaḥ āśrayam pratikṣipti sma tena eva jñāta sambandhe dvayoḥ anyatarā uktitaḥ arthāpattyā dvitīye api smṛtiḥ samupajāyate 
[018,17^1]	yat āha arthāpattyā vā anyatareṇa ubhaya pradarśanāt iti tatra api dṛṣṭāntena tad bhāva hetu bhāva pradarśanam manyamānaḥ artha āpattyai eka vacanena dvitīya siddhim āha tathā hi yat kṛtakam tat anityam iti ukte anartha antara bhāve vyaktam ayam asya svabhāvaḥ tanmātra anubandhī pramāṇa dṛṣṭaḥ tad bhāva niyamāt iti jñāta tad bhāvasya arthāpattyā anitya tva abhāve kṛtaka tvam na bhavati iti bhavati na hi svabhāvasya abhāve bhāvaḥ bhavati abhedāt anyathā tad bhāve bhavati iti eva na syāt tathā tad abhāve na bhavati iti ukte 
[018,17^2]	tatas eva tad bhāvatā vedinaḥ tathā hi ayam asya svabhāvaḥ yena tad abhāve na bhavati anyathā ayogāt iti tad tad svabhāvatā pratipattyā anvaya smṛtiḥ bhavati tathā yatra dhūmaḥ tatra agniḥ iti ukte kāryam dhūmaḥ dahanasya yena dhūme avaśyam agniḥ bhavati anyathā artha antarasya tad anubandha niyama abhāvāt svātantryam bhāvasya syāt atas tad abhāve api svabhāva avaikalyāt na abhāvaḥ kārye tu avaśyam kāraṇam bhavati idam eva hi kāraṇasya kāraṇa tvam yat artha antara bhāve svabhāva upadhānam kāryasya api tad bhāvaḥ eva bhāvaḥ tat ca asti dhūme 
[018,17^3]	tasmāt kāryam dhūmaḥ iti anvayena vidhita tat kārya tvasya dahana abhāve dhūmaḥ na bhavati iti arthāt vyatireka pratipattiḥ bhavati tathā asati agnau dhūmaḥ na asti iti ukte agniḥ dhūme bhavati avaśyam iti arthāt anvaya pratipattiḥ anyathā hi tad abhāve kim na bhavet iti nanu ca nitya anitya artha kārya tva abhāve api śravaṇa jñānam na bhavati tad abhāve na vai na bhavati tayoḥ eva tatas saṃśayāt anyathā abhāvena niścitāt katham tat bhāva parāmarśena saṃśayaḥ syāt kevalam tu bhāva niścaya abhāvāt na asti iti ucyate yadā punar dṛṣṭāntena na agni dhūmayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ pradarśyate 
[018,17^4]	tadā yatra dhūmaḥ tatra agniḥ iti eva na syāt pratibandha abhāvāt kutas agni abhāve dhūmaḥ na asti iti arthāt vyatireka siddhiḥ tathā vaidharmyeṇa abhāva asiddheḥ anvaya smṛtiḥ tasmāt dṛṣṭāntena ayam eva yathā ukta svabhāva pratibandhaḥ pradarśyate eka sadbhāve anyasya prasiddhi artham tad abhāve asambhavāt hetu svabhāva abhāvaḥ atas pratiṣedhe ca kasyacid hetuḥ tau eva hi nivartamānau sva pratibaddham nivartayate iti kasyacid arthasya pratiṣedham api sādhayitu kāmena hetoḥ vyāpakasya vā svabhāvasya nivṛttiḥ hetu tvena ākhyeyā apratibandhe hi katham
[020,02_020,07]	ekasya nivṛttiḥ anyasya nivṛttim sādhayet yukta upalabhasya tasya ca anupalambhanam pratiṣedha hetuḥ pratiṣedha viṣaya vyavahāra hetuḥ tad hetuḥ iti uktaḥ svayam tathābhūta anupalambhasya pratiṣedha rūpa tvāt hetu vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ ubhayasya api hetuḥ iti iyam trividhā api ukta anupalabdhiḥ anekadhā tat tad viruddha ādi agati gati bheda prayogataḥ 
[020,09_020,19]	trividhaḥ eva hi pratiṣedha hetuḥ upalabhya sattvasya hetoḥ tathā abhāva niścaye vyāpakasya sva ātmanaḥ ca anupalabdhiḥ iti sa prayoga vaśena tad tad viruddha ādi agati gati bheda prayogataḥ aneka prakāraḥ uktaḥ tasya agatyā tad viruddha gatyā viruddha kārya gatyā iti ādi bheda prayogaiḥ yathoktam prāk kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt vā svabhāvāt vā niyāmakāt avinā abhau a niyamaḥ adarśanāt na na darśanāt avaśyaṃbhāva niyamaḥ kaḥ parasya anyathā paraiḥ artha antara nimitte vā dharme vāsasi rāga vat iti antaraślokau api ca artha antara nimittaḥ hi dharmaḥ syāt anyaḥ eva saḥ 
[020,20^1]	na hi tasmin niṣpanne aniṣpannaḥ bhinna hetukaḥ vā tad svabhāvaḥ yuktaḥ ayam eva khalu bhedaḥ bheda hetuḥ vā bhāvānām viruddha dharma adhyāsaḥ kāraṇa bhedaḥ ca tau ced na bhedakau tadā na kasyacid kutaścid bhedaḥ iti ekam dravyam viśvam syāt tatas ca saha utpatti vināśau sarvasya ca sarvatra upayogaḥ syāt anyathā ekam iti eva na syāt nāma antaram vā artha bhedam abhyupagamya tathā abhidhānāt nanu anartha antara hetu tve api bhāva kāle anitya tā aniṣpatteḥ tulyā atatsvabhāva tā na vai kācid anyā anitya tā nāma yā paścāt niṣpadyeta saḥ eva hi bhāvaḥ kṣaṇa sthiti dharmā anitya tā vacana bhede api dharmi dharma tayā nimittam vakṣyāmaḥ tām punar asya kṣaṇa sthita udharma tām svabhāvam sva hetoḥ eva tathā utpatteḥ paśyan api manda buddhiḥ satta upalambhena sarvadā tad bhāva śaṅkā vipralabdhaḥ na vyavasyati sadṛśa apara utpatti vipralabdhaḥ vā 
[020,20^2]	antyakṣaṇa darśinām niścayāt paścāt asya anupalabdhyā asthita upratipatteḥ niścaya kālaḥ iti tadā anitya tā vyavasthāpyate kārya utpādana śakteḥ kāraṇa svabhāva tve api adṛṣṭa tad kāryasya kāraṇa darśane api apratipanna tadbhāvasya kārya darśanāt tad pratipatti vat anyathā artha antaram eva anitya tā syāt anya nimitta tve animitta tve vā tathā ca bhāvaḥ tadvān na syāt tad anupayogāt upayoge vā saḥ eva asya sva ātma bhūtaḥ anitya tā iti kim anyayā svabhāvena vā acalasya artha antara yoge api tad bhāva anutpatteḥ sa ca artha antarāt bhavan anitya tā anyaḥ vā dharmaḥ hetuḥ phalam vā syāt ahetu phalasya asambandhāt tatra bhāva anumānasya asambhavāt tatra 
[021,20_022,05]	paścāt bhāvān na hetu tvam phale api ekānta tā kutas sa hi niṣpanne bhāve artha antarataḥ paścāt bhavan katham tasya hetuḥ syāt phalasya api na avaśyam hetau bhāvaḥ iti tad bhāva hetoḥ anaikāntika tvam tat na artha antara nimittaḥ dharmaḥ bhāve avaśyam bhāvi iti ananumānam yadi tarhi darśana adarśane na anvaya vyatireka gateḥ āśrayaḥ katham dhūmaḥ agnim na vyabhicarati iti gamyate yasmāt kāryam dhūmaḥ hutabhujaḥ kārya dharma anuvṛttitaḥ yeṣām upalambhe tad lakṣaṇam anupalabdham yat upalabhyate tatra eka abhāve api naḥ upalabhyate tat tasya kāryam tat ca dhūme asti sa bhavan tad abhāve tu hetumat tām vilaṅghayet 
[022,06_022,20]	sakṛt api tathā adarśanāt kāryam siddhaḥ akārya tve akāraṇāt sakṛt api abhāvāt kāryasya ca sva kāraṇam antareṇa bhāve ahetumat tā eva syāt na hi yasya yam antareṇa bhāvaḥ sa tasya hetuḥ bhavati bhavati ca dhūmaḥ agnim antareṇa tat na tad hetuḥ anya hetuka tvāt na ahetuka tvam iti ced na tatra api tulya tvāt tad abhāve api agnau bhavati iti katham vā tatas anyatas vā atajjanana svabhāvāt bhavet svayam atad svabhāvasya ajananāt tasya ahetutā syāt na vai saḥ eva bhavati tādṛśasya bhāvāt anyādṛśāt bhavan katham tādṛśaḥ syāt tādṛśāt hi bhavan tādṛśaḥ syāt anyādṛśāt api tādṛśaḥ bhāve tad śakti niyama abhāvāt na hetu bhedaḥ bhedakaḥ iti akāraṇam viśvasya vaiśvarūpyam syāt sarvam vā sarvasmāt jāyeta tasmāt kāraṇa bheda abhedābhyām kārya bheda abhedau tat na dhūmaḥ arthāt dṛṣṭa ākāra vijātīyāt bhavati ahetuka tva prasaṅgāt tathā ca nityam sattvam asattvam vā ahetoḥ anya anapekṣaṇāt apekṣātaḥ hi bhāvānām kādācid ka tva sambhavaḥ 
[022,22]	sa hi dhūmaḥ ahetuḥ bhavat nirapekṣa tvāt na kadācid na bhavet tad bhāve vaikalya abhāvāt iṣṭa kāla vat tadā api vā na bhavet abhāva kāla aviśeṣāt apekṣayā hi bhāvāḥ kādācid kāḥ bhavanti bhāva abhāva kālayoḥ tad bhāva yogya tā ayogya tā yogāt tulya yogya tā yogyatayoḥ deśa kālayoḥ tadvat tā itarayoḥ niyama ayogāt sā ca yogyatā hetu bhāvāt kim anyat tasmāt eka deśa kāla parihāreṇa anya deśa kālayoḥ vartamānaḥ bhāvaḥ tad sāpekṣaḥ nāma bhavati tathā hi tathā vṛttiḥ eva apekṣā tad kṛta upakāra anapekṣasya tat niyama ayogāt tat niyata deśa kāla tvāt dhūmaḥ atra dṛṣṭaḥ sakṛt vaikalye ca punar na dṛṣṭaḥ tat janyaḥ asya svabhāvaḥ anyathā sakṛt api abhāvāt sa tad pratiniyataḥ anyatra katham bhavet bhavan vā na dhūmaḥ syāt tat janitaḥ hi svabhāva viśeṣaḥ dhūmaḥ iti tathā hetuḥ api tathābhūta kārya janana svabhāvaḥ tasya anyatas api bhāve na sa tasya svabhāvaḥ iti sakṛt api na janayet na vā sa dhūmaḥ adhūma janana svabhāvāt bhāvāt tad svabhāva tve ca saḥ eva agniḥ iti avyabhicāraḥ 
[023,14_023,18]	agni svabhāvaḥ śakrasya mūrddhā yadi agniḥ eva saḥ atha anagni svabhāvaḥ asau dhūmaḥ tatra katham bhavet dhūma hetu svabhāvaḥ hi vahniḥ tad śakti bhedavān adhūma hetoḥ dhūmasya bhāve sa syāt ahetukaḥ iti saṃgraha ślokau katham tarhi idānīm bhinnāt sahakāriṇaḥ kārya utpatteḥ yathā cakṣu ūrūpādeḥ vijñānasya na vai kiṃcid ekam janakam tad svabhāvam kim tu sāmagrī janikā tad svabhāvā saḥ eva anumīyate saḥ eva ca sāmagrī svabhāva sthiti āśrayaḥ kāryasya atas eva sahakāriṇām api aparyāyeṇa jananam yat api kiṃcid vijātīyāt bhavat dṛṣṭam gomaya ādeḥ śāluka ādi tatra api tathā abhidhāne api asti eva sva bīja prabhavāt svabhāva bhedaḥ hetu svabhāva bhedāt yathā kadalī bījakandodbhavā sphuṭam eva tādṛśam lokaḥ vivecayati ākāra bhedāt tasmāt na su vivecita ākāram kāryam kāraṇam vyabhicarati 
[024,01_024,03]	anvaya vyatirekāt yaḥ yasya dṛṣṭaḥ anuvartakaḥ svabhāvaḥ tasya tad hetuḥ atas bhinnāt na sambhavaḥ iti saṃgrahaślokaḥ tasmāt sakṛt api darśana adarśanābhyām kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddheḥ bhavati tatas tad pratipattiḥ na anyathā anvaya vyatirekayoḥ niḥśeṣa darśana adarśana āyattatvāt kvacid amūrta tve nitya tva darśane api anyatra anyathā adṛṣṭeḥ kvacid nitya tva abhāve api adṛṣṭasya punar dṛṣṭeḥ iti
[024,07_024,14]	bhavatu kāryasya kāraṇena avinābhāvaḥ tad utpatteḥ svabhāvaḥ idānīm katham avinābhāvaḥ svabhāve api avinābhāvaḥ bhāva mātra anurodhini yaḥ hi bhāva mātra anurodhī svabhāvaḥ tatra avinā abhāvaḥ bhāvasya iṣyate tad abhāve svayam bhāvasya abhāvaḥ syāt abhedataḥ yaḥ eva bhāvaḥ bhāva mātra anurodhī svabhāvaḥ iti ucyate saḥ eva svayam vastutas bhāvaḥ sa ca ātmānam parityajya katham bhavet yaḥ eva tarhi kṛtakaḥ saḥ eva anityaḥ bheda abhāvāt pratijñā artha eka deśaḥ hetuḥ syāt na eṣa doṣaḥ yasmāt 
[024,18]	sarve bhāvāḥ svabhāvena sva svabhāva vyavasthiteḥ svabhāva para bhāvābhyām yasmāt vyāvṛtti bhāginaḥ tasmāt yatas yatas arthānām vyāvṛttiḥ tad nibandhanāḥ jāti bhedāḥ prakalpyante tad viśeṣa avagāhinaḥ tasmāt yaḥ yena dharmeṇa viśeṣaḥ sampratīyate na sa śakyaḥ tatas anyena tena bhinnā vyavasthitiḥ 
[024,24^1]	sarve eva hi bhāvāḥ sva rūpa sthitayaḥ te naḥ ātmānam pareṇa miśrayanti tasya aparatva prasaṅgāt yat api eṣām abhinnam ātma bhūtam rūpam na tat teṣām tadānīm teṣām abhāvāt tat eva hi syāt abhinnasya bhāvāt tad vyatiriktasya bhinnasya ca abhāvāt tasya eva ca punar bheda virodhāt tat ca ātmani vyavasthitam amiśram eva artha antaram api aneka sambandhe api na tat teṣām sāmānyam atad rūpa tvāt dvi tva ādi saṃyoga kārya dravyeṣu api prasaṅgāt na hi sambandhinā api anyena anye samānā nāma tadvantaḥ nāma syuḥ bhūta vat kaṇṭheguṇena na abhinna pratyaya viṣayāḥ bhūta vat tadā ātmānam eva hi buddhiḥ saṃsṛjantī sāmānya viṣayā pratibhāsate na eka sambandhinau iti bhūta vat tad darśinyāḥ sā bhrāntiḥ iti ced tad darśinī iti kutas nirbīja bhrānti ayogāt iti ced te eva tad eka kāryā bījam saṃkhyā saṃyoga kārya dravya ādimatsu bhūtādiṣu abhāvāt ca tat na tathā sāmānya buddhau niveṣa abhāvāt sāmānyam anyat sati vā tasya api sva ātmani vyavasthānāt amiśraṇam anyena 
[024,24^2]	tasmāt ime bhāvāḥ sajātīya abhimatāt anyasmāt ca vyatiriktāḥ svabhāvena eka rūpa tvāt yatas yatas bhinnāḥ tad bheda pratyāyanāya kṛta saṃniveśaiḥ śabdaiḥ tatas tatas bhedam upādāya svabhāva abhede api aneka dharmāṇaḥ pratīyante te api śabdāḥ sarva bhedān ākṣepe api eka bheda codanāt tad sva lakṣaṇa niṣṭhāḥ eva bhavanti tat ekasmāt api tasya bhedaḥ asti iti tasmāt ekasya bhāvasya yāvanti para rūpāṇi tāvat yaḥ tad apekṣayā vyāvṛttayaḥ tad asambhavi kārya kāraṇasya tad bhedāt yāvat yaḥ ca vyāvṛttayaḥ tāvat yaḥ śrutayaḥ atad kārya kāraṇa parihāreṇa vyavahāra arthāḥ yathā prayatna anantarīyakaḥ śabdaḥ śrāvaṇaḥ iti atad kārya kāraṇa parihāra arthaḥ tasmāt svabhāva abhede api yena yena dharmeṇa nāmnā yaḥ viśeṣaḥ bhedaḥ pratīyate na sa śakyaḥ anyena pratyāyayitum iti naḥ eka arthāḥ sarva śabdāḥ tat na pratijñā artha eka deśaḥ hetuḥ iti katham punar etat gamyate vyavacchedaḥ śabda liṅgābhyām pratipādyate vidhinā na vastu rūpam eva iti pramāṇa antarasya śabda antarasya ca pravṛtteḥ tathā hi 
[026,02_026,12]	ekasya artha svabhāvasya pratyakṣasya sataḥ svayam kaḥ anyaḥ na dṛṣṭaḥ bhāgaḥ syāt yaḥ pramāṇaiḥ parīkṣyate ekaḥ hi artha ātmā sa pratyakṣaḥ asiddhe dharmiṇi sādhana asambhavāt yathā anitya tve sādhye śabdaḥ tasya pratyakṣeṇa eva siddheḥ sarva ākāra siddhiḥ tad anyasya asiddhasya abhāvāt bhāve vā atad svabhāva tvam na hi yaḥ yat eka yogakṣemaḥ na bhavati sa tad svabhāvaḥ yuktaḥ tanmātra nibandhana tvāt bheda vyavahārasya anyathā abhāva prasaṅgāt iti uktam tasmāt pratyakṣe dharmiṇi tad svabhāva sākalya paricchedāt tatra anavakāśā pramāṇa antara vṛttiḥ syāt no ced bhrānti nimittena saṃyojyeta guṇa antaram śuktau vā rajata ākāraḥ rūpa sādharmya darśanāt 
[026,14]	yadi dṛṣṭa sarva tattvasya api bhāvasya tathā niścaya pratirodhinā bhrānti nimittena guṇa antaram na saṃyojyate yathā śuktau rajata ākāraḥ na hi śuktau dve rūpe samānam viśiṣṭam ca tathā pratipatti prasaṅgāt apratipattau vā vivekena dvi tva vikalpā yogāt atiprasaṅgāt ca tasmāt paśyan śukti rūpam viśiṣṭam eva paśyati niścaya pratyaya vaikalyāt tu aniścinvan tad sāmānyam paśyāmi iti manyate tatas asya rajata samāropaḥ tathā sadṛśa apara apara utpattyā alakṣita nānā tvasya tad bhāva samāropāt sthitaḥ bhrāntiḥ yāvantaḥ asya para bhāvāḥ tāvantaḥ eva yathāsvam nimitta bhāvinaḥ samāropāḥ iti tad vyavacchedakāni bhavanti pramāṇāni sa phalāni syuḥ teṣām tu vyavaccheda phalānām na apratīta vastu aṃśa pratyāyane pravṛttiḥ tasya dṛṣṭa tvāt anaṃśasya ca eka deśena darśana ayogāt 
[027,03_027,07]	tasmāt dṛṣṭasya bhāvasya dṛṣṭaḥ eva akhilaḥ guṇaḥ bhrānteḥ niścīyate naḥ iti sādhanam sampravartate iti saṃgrahaślokaḥ tasmāt na adṛṣṭa grahaṇāya dṛṣṭe pramāṇa antara vṛttiḥ vastu grahe anumānāt ca dharmasya ekasya niścaye sarva dharma grahaḥ apohe na ayam doṣaḥ prasajyate 
[027,09]	na kevalam pratyakṣa dṛṣṭe pramāṇa antarāvṛttiḥ kvacid yadā anumānam api vastu vidhinā pratyāyayati na vyavaccheda kṛt tadā eka dharma niścaye tat avyatirekāt sarva dharma niścayaḥ iti pramāṇa antarāvṛttiḥ na hi tasmin niścite tad ātmā aniścitaḥ yuktaḥ yadā punar anumānena samāropa vyavacchedaḥ kriyate tadā naḥ eka samāra upa vyavacchedāt anya vyavacchedaḥ kṛtaḥ bhavati iti tad artham anyat pravartate nanu na avaśyam viparyāsa pūrvakaḥ eva apratīta niścayaḥ bhavati yathā akasmāt dhūmāt agni pratipattiḥ na hi tatra anagni samāropaḥ sambhāvyate tat na sarvatra vyavacchedaḥ kriyate uktam atra dharmi pratipattau abhedāt sarva pratipattiḥ bhede vā asambaddhasya tatra apratipattiḥ iti tasmāt tatra api tad darśinaḥ tad svabhāva aniścayaḥ kutas viparyāsāt sa ca tam pradeśam tad viviktena rūpeṇa niścinvan agni sattā bhāvanā vimuktayā buddhyā katham aviparyastaḥ nāma tad ākāra samāropa saṃśaya rahitaḥ ca tad pratipattau na liṅgam anusaret na ca tasya anvaya vyatirekayoḥ ādriyeta 
[028,03_028,08]	tasmāt apoha viṣayam iti liṅgam prakīrtitam anyathā dharmiṇaḥ siddhau asiddham kim atas param iti saṃgrahaślokaḥ kvacid dṛṣṭe api yat jñānam sāmānya artham vikalpakam asamāropitā anya aṃśe tad mātra apoha gocaram yat rūpa ādi darśana anantaram aliṅgam niścaya jñānam bhavati tat katham asati samārope bhavat vyavaccheda viṣayam bhavati samāropa viṣaye tasya abhāvāt yatra hi asya samāropaḥ yathā sthiraḥ sa ātmakaḥ iti vā na tatra bhede niścayaḥ bhavati 
[028,12_028,13]	niścaya āra upamanasoḥ bādhya bādhaka bhāvataḥ na hi sarvatas bhinnaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ api bhāvaḥ tathā eva pratyabhijñāyate kvacid bhede vyavadhāna sambhavāt yathā śukteḥ śukti tve yatra tu pratipattuḥ bhrānti nimittam na asti tatra eva asya tad darśana aviśeṣe api smārtaḥ niścayaḥ bhavati samāropa niścayayoḥ bādhya bādhaka bhāvāt niścayasya
[028,18_029,01]	samāropa viveke asya pravṛttiḥ iti gamyate tad vivekaḥ eva ca anya apohaḥ tasmāt tat api tad mātra apoha gocaram na vastu svabhāva niścaya ātmakam tathā hi kasyacid niścaye api anyasya apratipatti darśanāt tad svabhāva niścaye ca tasya ayogāt yāvantaḥ aṃśa samāropāḥ tad nirāse viniścayāḥ tāvantāḥ eva śabdāḥ ca tena te bhinna gocarāḥ anyathā ekena śabdena vyāptaḥ ekatra vastuni buddhyā vā na anya viṣayaḥ iti paryāyatā bhavet 
[029,05_029,10]	iti antaraślokaḥ yasya api nānā upādheḥ dhīḥ grāhikā arthasya bhedinaḥ yaḥ api manyate bhinnāḥ eva upādhayaḥ parasparam āśrayāt ca tad nibandhanāḥ śrutayaḥ tad ādhāreṣu vartante tatra eva vā tat ayam aprasaṅgaḥ iti tasya api nānā upādhi upakāra aṅga śakti abhinna ātmanaḥ grahe sarva ātmanā upakārasya kaḥ bhedakaḥ syāt aniścitaḥ 
[029,12_029,19]	yadi api upādhayaḥ bhinnāḥ eva śabda jñāna antarāṇām nimittam arthe sa tu taiḥ tadvān ekaḥ eva upalīyate tasya nānā upādhīnām upakāra āśraya śakti svabhāvasya sva ātmani abhedāt sarva ātmanā grahaṇe kaḥ eva upādhi bhedaḥ aniścitaḥ syāt sarva upādhi upakāraka tvena grahaṇāt na hi upakāraka tvam anyat eva tasya sva rūpeṇa gṛhyamāṇasya agṛhītam nāma atas yat eva asya svabhāvena grahaṇam tat eva upakāra tvena api iti tayoḥ ātmani sambandhāt eka jñāne dvaya grahaḥ 
[029,20_030,01]	ātma bhūtasya upādhi tadvatoḥ upakārya upakāraka bhāvasya grahaṇāt eka jñāne dvayoḥ api grahaṇam iti eka upādhi viśiṣṭe api tasmin gṛhyamāṇe sarva upādhīnām grahaṇam tad grahaṇana antarīyaka tvāt upādhimat grahaṇasya anyathā tathā api na gṛhyeta na hi anyaḥ eva anya upakārakaḥ yaḥ na gṛhītaḥ syāt na ca api upakārake tathā gṛhīte upakārya agrahaṇam tasya api agrahaṇa prasaṅgāt sva svāmi tva vat tasmāt artha antara upādhi vāde api samānaḥ prasaṅgaḥ atha api syāt bhinnāḥ eva śaktayaḥ śaktimataḥ yābhiḥ upādhīn upakaroti tatas na ayam prasaṅgaḥ iti dharma upakāra śaktīnām bhede tāḥ tasya kim yadi na upakāraḥ tatas tāsām tathā syāt anavasthitiḥ 
[030,03^1]	yadi pratyupādhi upakāraka tvāni tasya na sva ātma bhūtāni eva na api tatas upakāram anubhavanti kim tasya iti tāḥ ucyante upakāre vā sva ātma bhūtābhiḥ ayam ekaḥ śaktibhiḥ śaktīḥ upakurvan ekaḥ upādhinā api gṛhyamāṇaḥ sarva ātmanā gṛhyate eva tathā hi eka upādhi grahaṇe tad upakāriṇyāḥ śakteḥ grahaṇam tad grahaṇe tad upakārī bhāvaḥ sva ātma bhūta sakala śakti upakāraḥ gṛhītaḥ sarvāḥ śaktīḥ grāhayati tāḥ ca sva upādhīn iti tad avasthaḥ prasaṅgaḥ atha tāḥ api śakti upakāriṇyaḥ śaktayaḥ bhinnāḥ eva bhāvāt evam upādhīnām tad śaktīnām ca aparā parāsu eva śaktiṣu aparyavasānena ghaṭanāt saḥ ekaḥ tābhiḥ kadācid api agṛhītaḥ tad upakāra ātmā tadvat tvena na gṛhyate yadi punar kevalān eva upādhīn śabda jñānāni upalīyeran tadā tasya asamāveṣāt na bhavati tad pratipatti mukhena sarva pratipattiḥ 
[030,03^2_031,05]	tadā api tasya śabdaiḥ anākṣepāt na syāt tatra pravṛttiḥ iti vyarthaḥ śabda prayogaḥ syāt artha kriyā āśrayaḥ hi sarvaḥ vidhi pratiṣedhābhyām vyavahāraḥ upādhayaḥ ca tatra asamarthāḥ samarthaḥ ca naḥ eva ucyate iti kim śabda prayogaiḥ tatas ca upādhayaḥ naḥ upādhayaḥ syuḥ kvacid pravṛttau hi kasyacid pradhānasya aṅga bhāvāt tad apekṣayā tathā ucyate tasya śabdaiḥ anākṣepāt na te kasyacid aṅga bhūtāḥ iti kim upādhayaḥ lakṣita lakṣaṇāt adoṣaḥ iti ced samānaḥ prasaṅgaḥ sa tāvat taiḥ upādhibhiḥ na antarīyaka tayā upalakṣyamāṇaḥ ekena api upalakṣaṇe sarva ātmanā upalakṣitaḥ iti tad avasthaḥ prasaṅgaḥ kaḥ hi atra viśeṣaḥ śabdāḥ vai enam upalakṣayeyuḥ tad lakṣitāḥ vā upādhayaḥ sa tāvat tadānīm niścīyate sarva upakārakaḥ iti na kiṃcid etat tasmāt eka upakārake grāhye naḥ upakāraḥ tatas apare dṛṣṭe tasmin adṛṣṭāḥ ye tad grahe sakala grahaḥ iti saṃgrahaślokaḥ 
[031,06_031,16]	yadi bhrānti nivṛtti artham gṛhīte api anyat iṣyate syāt etat nirbhāgasya vastunaḥ grahaṇe kaḥ anyaḥ tadā na gṛhītaḥ nāma sa tu bhrāntyā na avadhāryate iti pramāṇa antaram pravartate yadi evam tat vyavaccheda viṣayam siddham tadvat tatas aparam asamāropa viṣaye vṛtteḥ tat tarhi bhrānti nivṛtti artham pravṛttam pramāṇam anya samāra upa vyavaccheda phalam iti siddham anya apoha viṣayam tadvat anyat api asamāropa viṣaye vṛtteḥ yatra asya samāropaḥ na tatrā niścayaḥ iti samāropa abhāve vartamānaḥ anya apoha viṣayaḥ siddhaḥ api ca niścayaiḥ yat na niścīyate rūpam tat teṣām viṣayaḥ katham 
[031,18]	iyam eva khalu niścayānām sva artha pratipattiḥ yat tat niścayanam tat ced ākāra antara vat aniścitam katham taiḥ gṛhītam katham idānīm aniścīyamānam pratyakṣeṇa api gṛhītam nāma na pratyakṣam kasyacid niścāyakam tat ayam api gṛhṇāti tat na niścayena kim tarhi tad pratibhāsena tat na niścaya aniścaya vaśāt pratyakṣasya grahaṇa agrahaṇe na evam niścayānām kiṃcid niścinvataḥ api anyatra aniścayena pravṛtti bhedāt grahaṇa agrahaṇam tasmāt tat eva asya grahaṇam yaḥ niścayaḥ anyathā eka ākāre api tat na syāt kim punar kāraṇam sarvatas bhinne vastu rūpe anubhava utpattau api tathā eva na smārtaḥ niścayaḥ bhavati saha kāri vaikalyāt tatas ca 
[032,01_032,03]	pratyakṣeṇa gṛhīte api viśeṣe aṃśa vivarjite yat viśeṣa avasāye asti pratyakṣaḥ sa pratīyate yadi api aṃśa rahitaḥ sarvatas bhinna svabhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ anubhūtaḥ tathā api na sarva bhedeṣu tāvatā niścayaḥ bhavati kāraṇa antara apekṣya tvāt anubhavaḥ hi yathā avikalpa abhyāsam niścaya pratyayān janayati yathā rūpa darśana aviśeṣe api kuṇapa kāminī bhakṣya vikalpāḥ tatra buddhi pāṭavam tad vāsanā abhyāsaḥ prakaraṇam iti ādayaḥ anubhavāt bheda niścaya utpatti sahakāriṇaḥ teṣām eva ca pratyāsatti tāratamya ādi bhedāt paurvāparyam yathā janakatvā adhyāpakatva aviśeṣe api pitaram āyāntam dṛṣṭvā pitā me āgacchati naḥ upādhyāyaḥ iti saḥ api bhavat niścayaḥ asati bhrānti kāraṇe bhavati tasmāt na abhūtaḥ iti eva sarva ākāra niścayaḥ 
[032,13_032,22]	tatra api ca anya vyāvṛttiḥ anya vyāvṛttaḥ iti api śabdāḥ ca niścayāḥ ca eva saṃketam anurundhate tatra api anya apohe na vyāvṛttiḥ anyā anyaḥ eva vyāvṛttaḥ tad vyāvṛtteḥ nivartamānasya tad bhāva prasaṅgāt tathā ca vyāvṛtteḥ abhāvaḥ tasmāt yā eva vyāvṛttiḥ saḥ eva vyāvṛttaḥ śabda pratipatti bhedaḥ tu saṃketa bhedāt na vācya bhedaḥ asti nanu ca vācya viśeṣa abhāvāt saṃketa bhedaḥ api ayuktaḥ dvayoḥ eka abhidhānāt tathā ca vyatirekiṇyā vibhakteḥ ayogaḥ tasyāḥ bheda āśraya tvāt dvayoḥ eka abhidhāne api vibhaktiḥ vyatirekiṇī bhinnam artham iva anveti vācye leśa viśeṣataḥ 
[032,24_033,07]	na vai śabdānām kācid viṣaya svabhāva āyattā vṛttiḥ icchātaḥ vṛtti abhāva prasaṅgāt te yathā vyatirikte avyatirikte vā prayoktum iṣyante tathā niyuktāḥ tam artham pratibandhena prakāśayanti tena gauḥ go tvam iti eka artha abhidhāne api kasyacid viśeṣasya pratyāyana artham kṛte saṃketa bhede vyatirikta arthā vibhaktiḥ artha antaram iva adarśayantī pratibhāti anartha antare api tathā prayoga darśana abhyāsāt na tāvatā sarvatra bhedaḥ anyatra api puruṣa icchā vaśāt pravṛttasya pratibandha abhāvāt yathā ekam kvacid eka vacanena khyāpyate tad aviśeṣe api gaurava ādi khyāpana artham bahuvacanena prayojana abhāvāt tu saṃketa bhedaḥ na syāt tat api asti eva tathā hi bheda antara pratikṣepa apratikṣepau tayoḥ dvayoḥ saṃketa bhedasya padam jñātṛ vāñca anurodhinaḥ 
[033,09]	yadā ayam pratipattā tad anya vyavaccheda bhāva anapekṣaḥ piṇḍa viśeṣe aśva vyavaccheda mātram jijñāsate tathā abhūta jñāpana artham tathā ākṛta saṃketena śabdena prabodhyata anaśva tvam asya asti iti yadā punar vyavaccheda antara anirākāṅkṣaḥ tam jñātum icchati tadā aparityakta vyavaccheda antare tatra eva aśva vyavacchede tathā aprakāśanāya prayuñjate anaśvaḥ ayam iti atas eva pūrvatra pratikṣipta bheda antara tvāt śabda vṛtteḥ na sāmānādhikaraṇyam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ vā go tvam asya śuklam iti tanmātra viśeṣeṇa buddheḥ tad āśraya bhūtāyāḥ ekatvena apratibhāsanāt nirākāṅkṣa tvāt ca dvitīye tu bhavati tathā saṃketa anusāreṇa saṃhṛta sakala vyavaccheda dharmaiḥ vibhāgavataḥ ekasya iva sandarśanena pratibhāsanāt vyavaccheda anta rasā kāṅkṣa tvāt ca 
[033,22_034,05]	bhedaḥ ayam eva sarvatra dravya bhāva abhidhāyinoḥ śabdayoḥ na tayoḥ vācye viśeṣaḥ tena kaścana tasmāt na sarvatra dharma dharmi vācinoḥ śabdayoḥ vācye arthe niścaya pratyaya viṣaya tvena kaścid viśeṣaḥ ekaḥ tam eva pratyāyayan pratikṣipta bheda antaraḥ pratyāyayati anyaḥ pratikṣepeṇa iti ayam viśeṣaḥ jijñāpayiṣuḥ artham tam tat hitena kṛtā api vā anyena vā yadi brūyāt bhedaḥ na asti tatas aparaḥ 
[034,07_034,17]	etāvantam eva ca bhedam darśayan tad hitena vā darśayet pācaka tvam iti kṛtā api vā pākaḥ iti anyena vā tathābhūta jñāpanāya svayam kṛtena samayena na punar tathā abhidhāna mātreṇa artha antaram eva tat bhavati tathābhūtasya eva jñāpanāya śabdasya kṛta saṃketa tvāt nanu ca pācaka tvam iti sambandhaḥ ucyate na pākaḥ eva na vai pākena anyaḥ eva kaścid pācakaḥ nāma abhidhīyate yādṛśaḥ varṇyate yat punar asya abhidheyam tat kathitam tat eva pācaka tvena api iti alam apratiṣṭhaiḥ mithyā vikalpaiḥ yathā ca na artha antara bhūtā kriyā asti tad samavāyaḥ vā tat pratyāyayiṣyāmaḥ tena anya apoha viṣaye tadvat pakṣa upavarṇanam pratyākhyātam pṛthaktve hi syāt doṣaḥ jāti tadvatoḥ 
[034,19^1]	yat āhuḥ anya apohe api śabda arthe tad viśiṣṭasya abhidhānāt tadvat pakṣa uditaḥ sarvaḥ prasaṅgaḥ samānaḥ iti tat api anena prativyūḍham tatra hi artha antaram upādāya anyatra vartamānaḥ dhvaniḥ asvātantrya ādi doṣaiḥ upadrūyate na ca artha antaram anyasmāt vyāvṛttiḥ vyāvṛttāt dvayoḥ eka abhidhānāt iti uktam katham idānīm ekasya vyāvṛttasya anyān anugamāt anya vyāvṛttiḥ sāmānyam tad buddhau tathā pratibhāsanāt na vai kiṃcid sāmānyam nāma asti śabda āśrayā buddhiḥ anādi vāsanā sāmarthyāt asaṃsṛṣṭān api dharmān saṃsṛjantī jāyate tasyāḥ pratibhāsa vaśena sāmānyam sāmānādhikaraṇyam ca vyavasthāpyate asat arthaḥ api arthānām saṃsarga bheda abhāvāt tasya sarvasya tad kārya kāraṇa tayā anyebhyaḥ bhidyamānāḥ arthāḥ samāśrayaḥ dhvaniḥ ca aniṣṭa parihāreṇa pravartayati iti anya apoha viṣayaḥ uktaḥ 
[034,19^2]	tatra anapekṣita bāhya tattvaḥ buddhi pratibhāsa vaśād ekaḥ aneka vyāvṛttaḥ śabdaiḥ viṣayīkriyate tad anubhava ahita vāsanā prabodha janmabhiḥ vikalpaiḥ adhyavasita tad bhāva arthaiḥ tatra eva ca ayam dharma dharmi vyavahāraḥ parasparam tattva anya tvābhyām avācyaḥ pratanyate na hi anyaḥ dharmaḥ dharmiṇaḥ anartha antara abhidhānāt na api saḥ eva tad vācinām iva dharma vācinām api vyavaccheda antarākṣepa prasaṅgāt tathā ca iṣṭa pratyāyanāt saṃketa bheda akaraṇam iti etat śabda arthe avācya tvam dharma dharmiṇoḥ vastuni tu sva lakṣaṇe sāmānya lakṣaṇam avācyam abhāvāt nanu ca dharma dharmiṇoḥ abhede bhede vā dṛṣṭāḥ ṣaṣṭhī ādi vibhaktayaḥ dharma bahu tvāt tatra dṛṣṭaḥ vacana bhedaḥ ca dharmiṇi na syāt uktam atra śabdānām svātantrya abhāvāt iti api ca 
[035,18_036,03]	yeṣām vastu vaśāḥ vācaḥ na vivakṣā para āśrayāḥ ṣaṣṭhī vacana bheda ādi codyam tān prati yuktimat yadi nāma ete śabdāḥ puruṣaiḥ kvacid praṇinīṣitāḥ api na śakyante praṇetum vastu pratibandhāt dhūma ādi vat tadā ayam upālambhaḥ syāt katham ṣaṣṭhī ādayaḥ iti yadā punar yat yathā vācaka tvena vaktṛbhiḥ viniyamyate anapekṣita bāhya artham tat tathā vācakam vacaḥ 
[036,05]	na hi vyatireke ṣaṣṭhī bāhulye jasā ādayaḥ iti etat api puruṣa abhiprāya nirapekṣam vastu saṃnidhi mātreṇa svayam pravṛttam te tu tatra tathā prayuñjate iti tatas tathā pratipattiḥ bhavati evam anyatra api kathaṃcid taiḥ prayuktāḥ tathā eva pratīti hetavaḥ bhavanti tatra vācyeṣu puruṣa āyatta vṛttīnām śabdānām avastu sandarśinām yathā abhyāsam vikalpa prabodha hetūnām pravṛtti cintā tad vaśāt vastu vyavasthāpanam ca kevalam jāḍya khyāpanam tathā akṛta vyavasthāḥ śabdāḥ dharma dharmyādiṣu na punar vyatireka vastu bhedāt iti kutas etat tathā vyavahāra ayogāt na hi dharma dharmiṇoḥ bhede tattva rūpa tve vā sāmānya tad sambandha sāmānā adhikaraṇya viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvāḥ yujyante śabdānām vā yathāvastu vṛttau iti vakṣyāmaḥ yaḥ ca ayam sarvatra vastu kṛtam eva śabda pravṛtti bhedam icchati tasya
[036,18_036,21^1]	dārāḥ ṣaṇṇagarī iti ādau bheda abheda vyavasthiteḥ khasya svabhāvaḥ kha tvam ca iti atra vā kim nibandhanam yadā ekā api strī dārāḥ ekam api sikatā dravyam sikatā iti vyavahāraḥ tatra kim bāhulyam yena evam bhavati śakti bhedaḥ iti ced sarvatra utsannam idānīm eka vacanam eka śakteḥ abhāvāt yatnaḥ ca vyarthaḥ vastu abhedāt anyatra eka vacanam iti ced iha api astu tat ayam nirvastukaḥ niyamaḥ kriyamāṇaḥ svātantryam icchāyāḥ śabda prayoge khyāpayati ṣaṇṇagarī iti ca katham bahuṣu ekavacanam na hi nagarāṇi eva kiṃcid kutas teṣām samāhāraḥ prāsāda puruṣa ādīnām vijātīyānām anārambhāt kutas tad samudāyaḥ dravyam asaṃyogāḥ ca na saṃyogaḥ prāsādasya svayam saṃyoga ātmakasya pareṇa asaṃyogāt ca tatas eva saṃkhyā bhāvaḥ tad saṃyoga puruṣa viśiṣṭā sattā nagaram iti ced 
[036,21^2]	kim asyāḥ niratiśayāyāḥ viśeṣaṇam sattāyāḥ ca eka tvāt nagara bahu tve api nagarāṇi iti bahuvacanam na syāt dvayasya paraspara sahita tā iti ced anupakārya upakārakaḥ kaḥ sahāyībhāvaḥ puruṣa saṃyoga sattānām ca bahu tvāt nagaram iti katham eka vacanam tathābhūtānām kvacid arthe abhinnā śaktiḥ asti sā nimittam iti ced na śakteḥ vastu rūpā vyatirekāt vyatireke vai anupakāryasya pāratantrya ayogāt upakāre vā śakti upakāriṇyāḥ api śakteḥ vyatirekaḥ iti anavasthiteḥ apratipattiḥ tat avyatireke vā ādyāyām api prasaṅgaḥ iti yat kiṃcid etat khasya svabhāvaḥ kha tvam iti vyatireka āśrayā ṣaṣṭhī na syāt na hi tatra sāmānyam asti na api vibhu tva ādayaḥ guṇāḥ tathā ucyante 
[036,21^3]	artha antarasya tad svabhāva tva ayogāt teṣām ca niḥsvabhāva tva prasaṅgāt tasya api artha antara svabhāva tve ati prasaṅgaḥ tathā ca apratipattiḥ evam ṣaṭpadārtha varga ādayaḥ api vācyāḥ na hi tatra sāmānyam saṃkhyā saṃyogaḥ vā sambhavati katham idānīm asati atiśaye khasya svabhāvaḥ iti na tu kham iti eva khasya artha antara sādhāraṇa rūpa aparāmarśena kha śabda pravṛtti nibandhanam rūpam tathā jijñāsāyām evam ucyate nanu sarvatas vyāvṛttasya rūpasya abhidhānam na sambhavati na vai tat eva rūpam buddhau samarpyate anatīndriya tva prasaṅgāt kevalam ayam tathābhūtam pratyāyayiṣyāmi iti śabdena śrotari asaṃsṛṣṭa tad svabhāvam vikalpa pratibimbam arpayati 
[036,21^4]	yat āha adṛṣṭa arthe artha vikalpa mātram iti na evam pratipādya pratipādakābhyām sva lakṣaṇam pratipannam pratipāditam vā bhavati svarga ādi śravaṇe api tad anubhāvinām iva pratibhāsā bheda prasaṅgāt tasmāt ayam apratipadyamānaḥ api bhāva svabhāvam tathābhūtaḥ eva vikalpa pratibimbe tat adhyavasāyī saṃtuṣyati tathābhūta tvāt eva śabda artha pratipatteḥ tena etat evam ucyate śabdaḥ sva rūpam āha iti na punar sva rūpa pratibhāsasyaḥ eva vijñānasya jananāt katham tarhi idānīm ekānta vyāvṛtta rūpeṣu bhāveṣu sāmānyam nāma teṣām asaṃsargāt anyasya ca abhāvāt uktam yādṛśam sāmānyam asaṃsṛṣṭānām eka asaṃsargaḥ tad vyatirekiṇām samāna tā iti api ca 
[038,11]	para rūpam svarūpeṇa yayā saṃvriyate dhiyā eka artha pratibhāsinyāḥ bhāvān āśritya bhedinaḥ tayā saṃvṛta nānā arthāḥ saṃvṛtyā bhedinaḥ svayam abhedinaḥ iva ābhānti bhāvāḥ rūpeṇa kenacid tasyāḥ abhiprāya vaśāt sāmānyam sat prakīrtitam tat asat parama arthena yathā saṃkalpitam tayā 
[038,17^1]	buddhiḥ khalu tad anya vyatirekiṇaḥ padārthān āśritya utpadyamānā vikalpikā sva vāsanā prakṛtim anuvidadhatī bhinnam eṣām rūpam tirodhāya pratibhāsam abhinnam ātmīyam adhyasya tān saṃsṛjantī sandarśayati sā ca eka sādhya sādhana tayā anya vivekinām bhāvānām tad vikalpa vāsanāyāḥ ca prakṛtiḥ yat evam eṣā pratibhāti tad udbhavā sā ca saṃvṛtiḥ saṃvriyate anayā svarūpeṇa para rūpam iti te ca tayā saṃvṛta bhedāḥ svayam bhedinaḥ api abhedinaḥ iva kenacid rūpeṇa pratibhānti tat eṣām buddhi pratibhāsam anurundhānaiḥ buddhi parivartinām eva bhāvānām ākāra viśeṣa parigrahāt bahis iva parisphuratām sāmānyam iti ucyate katham idānīm anya apohaḥ sāmānyam saḥ eva khalu anya apohas tam eva gṛhṇatī sā prakṛti vibhramāt vikalpānām vastu grāhiṇī iva pratibhāti sā hi tad anya vivekiṣu eva bhāveṣu bhavantī viveka viṣayāḥ iti gamyate 
[038,17^2_039,19]	nanu bāhyāḥ vivekinaḥ na ca teṣu vikalpa pravṛttiḥ iti katham teṣu bhavati vyākhyātāraḥ khalu evam vivecayanti na vyavahartāraḥ te tu sva ālambanam eva artha kriyā yogyam manyamānāḥ dṛśya vikalpyau arthau ekīkṛtya pravartante tad abhiprāya vaśāt evam ucyate tad kāritayā atad kāribhyaḥ bhinnān tathā śabdena pratipādayanti iti pratibhāsa bheda ādibhyaḥ tu tattva cintakāḥ na abhedam anumanyante yadi pratipattṛ abhiprāyaḥ anuvidhīyate anya apohaḥ api sāmānyam mā bhūt na hi evam pratipattiḥ iti na vai kevalam evam apratipattiḥ vyakti vyatirikta avyatirikta eka nitya vyāpita ādi ākāraiḥ api naḥ eva pratipattiḥ kevalam abhinna ākārā buddhiḥ utpadyate tasyāḥ kaḥ āśrayaḥ iti anya apohaḥ ucyate tasya vastuṣu bhāvāt avirodhāt vyavahārasya ca śabda āśrayasya tathā adarśanāt na punar vastu bhūtam kiṃcid sāmānyam nāma asti yathā iyam buddhiḥ pratibhāti yasmāt vyaktayaḥ na anuyanti anyat anuyāyi na bhāsate 
[039,20]	na hi imāḥ vyaktayaḥ parasparam anvāviśanti bheda abhāve na sāmānyasya eva abhāva prasaṅgāt anyat ca na tābhyaḥ vyatiriktam kiṃcid tathā buddhau pratibhāti apratibhāsamānam ca katham ātmanā anyam grāhayet vyapadeśayet vā na ca taiḥ sambaddham ekam iti eva sāmānyam bhavati atiprasaṅgāt iti uktam abhinna abhidhāna pratyaya nimittam ekam sāmānyam na sarvam iti ced katham anyatas anyatra pratyaya vṛttiḥ tad sambandhāt saṃkhyā kārya dravya ādiṣu api prasaṅgaḥ asāmānya ātmaka tvāt naḥ iti ced nanu saḥ eva ayam vicāryate kaḥ ayam sāmānya ātmā iti tatra sati sambandhe pratyaya vṛttiḥ tatas sāmānyam iti atra ucyate aneka sambandhebhyaḥ kārya dravya ādibhyaḥ nimitta sambhavāt pratyaya vṛttiḥ tatas ca sāmānya ātma tā anyathā anyatra api mā bhūt viśeṣa abhāvāt tathā ca dravya guṇa sāmānyānām rūpa saṃkaraḥ iti evam tarhi buddheḥ eva pratibhāsaḥ jñāna rūpa tvāt san eva sāmānyam tat na yasmāt 
[040,05_040,06]	jñānāt avyatiriktam ca katham artha antaram vrajet jñānasya rūpam katham arthānām sāmānyam tasya teṣu abhāvāt tad bhāva adhyavasāyāt tathā abhrāntyā vyavahāraḥ iti ced tatra tathā ajñāna utpatteḥ kim nibandhanam anāśrayasya ca utpattau sarvatra syāt athavā jñānāt avyatiriktam ekasmāt katham anyasya punar jñānasya rūpam syāt vyakti antara bhāvinaḥ te tas ca jñāna antaram vyakti antaram vā avyāpnuvat katham sāmānyam syāt 
[040,13_040,17]	tasmāt mithyā vikalpaḥ ayam artheṣu eka ātma tā grahaḥ na hi arthāḥ vyatiriktena avyatiriktena vā kenacid ātmanā samānāḥ tathā eṣām grahaṇam mithyā vikalpaḥ eva itaretara bhedaḥ asya bījam saṃjñā yad arthikā yasya pratyāyana artham saṃketaḥ kriyate abhinna sādhyān bhāvān atad sādhyebhyaḥ bhedena jñātvā tad parihāreṇa pravarteta iti saḥ ayam itaretara bhedaḥ tasya eka ātma tā pratibhāsinaḥ mithyā vikalpasya bījam tam eva gṛhṇan eṣa vikalpaḥ sva vāsanā prakṛteḥ evam pratibhāti katham punar bhinnānām abhinnam kāryam yena tad anyebhyaḥ bhedāt abhedaḥ iti ucyate prakṛtiḥ eṣā bhavānām yat 
[040,24_041,01]	eka pratyavamarśa artha jñāna ādi eka artha sādhane bhede api niyatāḥ kecid svabhāvena indriya ādi vat yathā indriya viṣaya āloka m anaskārāḥ ātmā indriya manaḥ artha tad saṃnikarṣāḥ vā asati api tat bhāva niyate sāmānye rūpa vijñānam ekam janayanti evam śiṃśapa ādayaḥ api bhedāḥ parasparān anvaye api prakṛtyāḥ eva ekam eka ākāram pratyabhijñānam janayanti anyām vā yathāpratyayam dahana gṛha ādikām kāṣṭha sādhyām artha kriyām na tu bheda aviśeṣe api jala ādayaḥ śrotra ādi vat rūpa ādi jñāne 
[041,07_041,09]	jvara ādi śamane kāścid saha pratyekam eva vā dṛṣṭāḥ yathā vai oṣadhayaḥ nānātve api na ca aparāḥ yathā vā guḍūcī vyakti ādayaḥ saha pratyekam vā jvara ādi śamana lakṣaṇam ekam kāryam kurvanti na ca tatra sāmānyam apekṣante bhede api tad prakṛti tvāt na tad aviśeṣe api dadhi trapusa ādayaḥ syāt etat sāmānyam eva kiṃcid tāsu tathābhūtāsu vidyate tatas eva tat ekam kāryam iti tat ayuktam 
[041,14_042,01]	aviśeṣān sāmānyasya na sāmānyam tad kārya kṛt tasya api aviśeṣa prasaṅgataḥ tāsām kṣetra ādi bhede api yadi hi sāmānyāt jvara ādi śamanam kāryam syāt tasya aviśeṣāt vyaktīnām kṣetra ādi bhede api cira śīghra praśamana ādayaḥ viśeṣāḥ guṇa tāratamyam ca na syāt viśeṣe vā sāmānyasya svabhāva bhedāt svarūpa hānam dhrauvyāt ca sāmānyasya anupakārataḥ 
[042,02^1]	yadi hi upakuryāt anādheya viśeṣasya ananya apekṣaṇāt sakṛt sarvam sva kāryam janayet na vā tad janana svabhāvam vyaktayaḥ tu kāla deśa saṃskāra vaśena viśiṣṭa utpattayaḥ viśeṣa vat kāryam kuryuḥ iti avirodhaḥ tadvat arthāḥ api kecid svabhāva bhede api eka pratyabhijñāna ādikām artha kriyām kurvantaḥ tad akāribhyaḥ bhedāt abhinnāḥ iti ucyante ekena vai anekaḥ janitaḥ atat janyebhyaḥ bhedāt kim punar anena bheda lakṣaṇena sāmānyena sva lakṣaṇam samānam iti pratyeyam atha anyat eva kim ca atas yadi sva lakṣaṇam katham vikalpasya viṣayaḥ anyatas vā katham artha kriyā sva lakṣaṇe ca anitya tva ādi pratīteḥ atādrūpyam teṣām ca avastu dharma tā 
[042,02^2]	na eṣa doṣaḥ jñāna pratibhāsinī arthe sāmānya sāmāna adhikaraṇya dharma dharmi vyavahārāḥ yat etat jñānam vastu svabhāva grāhiṇa anubhavena āhitām vāsanām āśritya vikalpakam utpadyate atad viṣayam api tad viṣayam iva tad anubhava ahita vāsanā prabhava prakṛteḥ adhyavasita tad bhāva svarūpam abhinna kārya padārtha prasūteḥ abhinna artha grāhī iva tad anya bheda parama artha samāna ākāram tatra yaḥ artha ākāraḥ pratibhāti bāhyaḥ iva ekaḥ iva anartha kriyā kārī api tad kārī iva vyavahāriṇām tathā adhyavasāya pravṛtteḥ anyathā pravṛtti ayogāt tat artha kriyā kāritayā pratibhāsanāt tad akāribhyaḥ bhinnam iva na ca tat tattvam parīkṣā anaṅga tvāt iti pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ 
[042,02^3]	te arthāḥ buddhi niveśinaḥ tena samānāḥ iti gṛhyante kutaścid vyāvṛttyā pratibhāsanāt na sva lakṣaṇam tatra apratibhāsanāt te eva ca kutaścid vyāvṛttāḥ punar anyatas api vyāvṛttimantaḥ abhinnāḥ ca pratibhānti iti svayam asatām api tathā buddhyā upadarśanāt mithyā arthaḥ eva sāmānya sāmāna adhikaraṇya vyavahāraḥ kriyate sarvaḥ ca ayam sva lakṣaṇānām eva darśana ahita vāsanā kṛtaḥ viplavaḥ iti tad pratibaddha janmanām vikalpānām atad pratibhāsi tve api vastuni avisaṃvādaḥ maṇiprabhāyām iva maṇi bhrānteḥ na anyeṣām tad bheda prabhave sati api yathā adṛṣṭa viśeṣa anusaraṇam parityajya kiṃcid sāmānya grahaṇena viśeṣa antara samāropāt dīpa prabhāyām iva maṇi buddheḥ tena na vikalpa viṣayeṣu artheṣu artha kriyā kāritvam na api sva lakṣaṇasya anitya tva ādi abhāvaḥ yasmāt na anitya tvam nāma kiṃcid anyat calāt vastunaḥ 
[042,02^4]	kṣaṇa pratyupasthāna dharma tayā tasya tathābhūtasya grahaṇāt etat evam bhavati anityaḥ ayam anitya tvam asya iti vā tad dharmatām eva avatarantaḥ vikalpāḥ nānā eka dharma vyatirekān sandarśayanti na ca te nirāśrayāḥ tad bheda darśana āśraya tvāt na avastu dharma tā tad svabhāvasya eva tathā khyāteḥ vastunaḥ tu nānā eka vyatireka grahaḥ vibhramaḥ syāt tasya eka aneka kārya kāriṇaḥ tathā abhāva jijñāsāsu tathā abhāva khyāpanāya tathā akṛta sthiti tvāt na vastu bhedāt tasya ekasya aneka tva ayogāt anekasya ca eka tva ayogāt vyatiriktasya ca niṣedhāt 
[042,02^5]	teṣām prakṛti bhedāt yathāvastu śabda artha abhyupagame sāmāna adhikaraṇya ayogāt tad upādheḥ ekasya dvābhyām abhidhānāt adoṣaḥ iti ced anupakāriṇi pāratantrya ayogāt anupādhiḥ pāratantrye ca janya janaka bhāvāt saha anavasthiteḥ dvayoḥ anabhidhānam ekasya buddhyā adhyāhāre na vastu viṣayaḥ śabdaḥ syāt buddhi pratibhāsa viṣaya tve ca sarvam tathā eva astu tathā bhinna upādhim atas ekasya grahaṇe apratibhāsanāt upakārya upakāriṇoḥ api upādhi tadvatoḥ saha avasthānāt adoṣaḥ iti ced na niṣpannasya pāratantrya abhāvāt anupādhi tvam 
[042,02^6]	na aniṣpannasya svarūpa asiddheḥ sarvathā asat pāratantryam iti kalpanā āropitam kṛtvā vyavahāre sarvathā saḥ eva kim na buddhiḥ anuvidhīyate eka śabda pramāṇena viṣayīkaraṇe vastu balāt aśeṣa ākṣepāt tad anya vaiyarthyam ca na syāt buddhi pratibhāsasya nirvastuka tvāt vastu sāmarthya abhāvinām doṣāṇām aprasaṅgaḥ tat abhinnam eka ākāra viṣayīkaraṇe api aniścitāni ākāram ākāra anta rasā kāṅkṣa buddhi grāhyam bhinna śabda artha upasaṃhāre api abhinnam buddhau pratibhāti iti sāmānya viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva sāmāna adhikaraṇyāni yathāprati iti na virudhyante dharma dharmi bhedaḥ api asya 
[042,02^7]	aneka artha bheda sambhave tad eka artha bheda vidhi pratiṣedha jijñāsāyām tat eva vastu pratikṣipta bheda antareṇa dharma śabdena saṃcodya buddheḥ tathā pratibhāsanāt vyatiriktam dharmam iva aviśeṣeṇa aparam asya svabhāvam dharmi tayā vyavasthāpya pradarśyate tāvatā ca aṃśena dharma dharmiṇoḥ bhedāt bhedavatī iva buddhiḥ pratibhāti na vastu bhedāt yathā ukta doṣāt tathābhūta bheda bāhulya codanayā vacana bhedaḥ sādhya sādhana bhedaḥ ca tad svabhāva samāśrayaiḥ dharma pratibhāsa bhedaiḥ tad svabhāva pratipattaye kriyate iti 
[044,15^1]	tad svabhāva grahaṇāt yā dhīḥ tad arthāḥ iva api anarthikā vikalpikā atad kārya artha bheda niṣṭhā prajāyate tasyām yat rūpam ābhāti bāhyam ekam iva anyatas vyāvṛttam iva nistattvam parīkṣā anaṅga bhāvataḥ arthāḥ jñāna niviṣṭāḥ te yatas vyāvṛtti rūpiṇaḥ tena abhinnāḥ iva ābhānti vyāvṛttāḥ punar anyatas te eva teṣām sāmānya samāna ādhāra gocaraiḥ jñāna abhidhānaiḥ mithyā arthaḥ vyavahāraḥ pratanyate sa ca sarvaḥ padārthānām anyonya abhāva saṃśrayaḥ tena anya apoha viṣayaḥ vastu lābhasya ca āśrayaḥ yatra asti vastu sambandhaḥ yathā ukta anumitau yathā na anyatra bhrānti sāmye api dīpa tejaḥ maṇau yathā tatra eka kāryaḥ anekaḥ api tad akārya anyata āśrayaiḥ eka tvena abhidhā jñānaiḥ vyavahāram pratāryate tathā aneka kṛt ekaḥ api tad bhāva paridīpane atad kārya artha bhedena nānā dharma pratīyate 
[044,15^2]	yathā pratīti kathitaḥ śabda arthaḥ asau asan api sāmānādhikaraṇyam ca vastuni asya na sambhavaḥ dharma dharmi vyavasthānam bhedaḥ abhedaḥ ca yādṛśaḥ asamīkṣita tattva arthaḥ yathā loke pratīyate tam tathā eva samāśritya sādhya sādhana saṃsthitiḥ parama artha avatārāya vidvadbhiḥ avakalpyate saṃsṛjyante na bhidyate svatas arthāḥ pāramārthikāḥ rūpam ekam anekam ca teṣu buddheḥ upaplavaḥ bhedaḥ tatas ayam bauddhe arthe sāmānyam bhedaḥ iti api tasya eva ca anya vyāvṛttyā dharma bhedaḥ prakalpyate sādhya sādhana saṃkalpe vastu darśana hānitaḥ bhedaḥ sāmānya saṃsṛṣṭaḥ grāhyaḥ na atra sva lakṣaṇam samāna bhinna ādi ākāraiḥ na tat grāhyam kathaṃcana bhedānām bahu bhedānām tatra ekasmin ayogataḥ tad rūpam sarvatas bhinnam tathā tad pratipādikā na śrutiḥ kalpanā vā asti sāmānyena eva vṛttitaḥ 
[045,20_045,24]	iti saṃgraha ślokāḥ kim punar kāraṇam sva lakṣaṇe śabdāḥ na prayujyante yasmāt śabdāḥ saṃketitam prāhuḥ vyavahārāya sa smṛtaḥ tadā sva lakṣaṇam na asti saṃketaḥ tena tatra na na hi śabdāḥ asaṃketitam artham prakāśayanti saṃketaḥ ca vyavahāra artham kriyate api nāma itas śabdāt kṛta saṃketāt uttarakālam imam artham pratipadyeta iti na ca prāk kṛta sambandhasya ekatra sva lakṣaṇe śabdasya paścāt prayogaḥ yuktaḥ tasya deśa kāla vyakti bhedān āskandhanāt tasmāt na sva lakṣaṇe samayaḥ sāmānyam tarhi vyatiriktam avyatiriktam vā vyāpi śabdaiḥ abhidhīyate tat na vyavahāra kāla abhāva doṣaḥ na etat asti yasmāt 
[045,32_046,10]	api pravarteta pumān vijñāya artha kriyā kṣamān tat sādhanāya iti artheṣu saṃyojyante abhidhāyakāḥ na khalu vai vyasanam eva etat lokasya yat ayam asaṃketayan aprayuñjānaḥ vā śabdān duḥkham āsīta kim tarhi sarve eva asya avadheyaḥ ārambhaḥ phala arthaḥ niṣphala ārambhasya upekṣanīya tvāt tat ayam śabdān api kvacid niyuñjānaḥ phalam eva kiṃcid īhitum yuktaḥ tat ca sarvam tyāga āpti lakṣaṇam iṣṭa aniṣṭayoḥ tena ayam iṣṭa aniṣṭayoḥ sādhanam asādhanam ca jñātvā tatra pravṛtti nivṛttī kuryām kārayeyam vā iti śabdāt niyuñjīta niyoge vā ādriyeta anyathā apekṣaṇīya tvāt tatra anartha kriyā yogyā jātiḥ 
[046,11^1]	na hi jātiḥ kvacid vāha doha upatiṣṭhate na ca tādṛśam prakaraṇam antareṇa loke śabda prayogaḥ vyavahāreṣu vyakteḥ aśakya codana tvāt lakṣita lakṣaṇa artham jāti codanāḥ iti ced aśabda codite sati api sambandhe katham pravarteta na hi kaścid daṇḍam chindhi iti ukte daṇḍinam chinatti na api asambhavāt vyaktau pravṛttiḥ evam hi asambaddha pralāpī syāt na tatas anyatra pravṛttiḥ balīvarda doha codanā vat na ca artha antara codanena artha antarasya lakṣaṇam na hi sambandhe sati api daṇḍa śabdāt daṇḍini pratipattiḥ aniyata sambandha tvāt tatra naḥ iti ced tat tulyam jātau api vyaktīnām apāye kevalāyāḥ jāteḥ avasthānāt 
[046,11^2]	bhrātṛ ādi śabdāḥ tu sambandhi śabda tvāt ākṣipeyuḥ param na tathā go tva ādi śrutayaḥ sambandhi vācinyaḥ apeta vyaktīnām api jātīnām tat śrutibhyaḥ nityam anugamana prasaṅgāt sarvadā tad sambandha yogya tā pratīteḥ iṣṭam eva iti ced sarvadā tarhi go śabdāt apravṛttiḥ sahita asahita avasthayoḥ viśeṣeṇa anākṣepāt vyakti sambandhinyāḥ jāteḥ codanāt adoṣaḥ iti ced sarvadā tarhi tad viśeṣaṇa tvena avasthitā vyaktiḥ ākṣiptāḥ eva iti tadvān abhidheyaḥ syāt na ca jāti vyaktyoḥ kaścid sambandhaḥ anyonyam ajanya janaka tvena anupakārāt tatas lakṣaṇam api ayuktam tasmāt na jātau śabda niveśanam phala abhāvāt evam tarhi 
[046,31_047,06]	 tadvān alam artha kriyāsu iti tatra śabdaḥ niyojyate sa ca sākṣāt na yojyate kasmāt yadi vyaktau śabda niveśanam phalavat sa ca śabdaḥ kasmāt sākṣāt vyaktiṣu eva na niyujyate kim tatra anyena vyavadhinā ānantyāt ced idam samam 
[047,07_047,18]	syāt etat ānantyāt vyaktīnām aśakyaḥ śabdena sambandhaḥ kartum evam sati idam ānantyam tadvatī api samānam jātyāḥ api hi vyaktasya eva vaktavyāḥ iti akṛta sambandhasya anabhidhānāt avaśyam tatra sambandhaḥ karaṇīyaḥ sa ca na śakyate tad sambandhini karaṇāt tatra api kṛtaḥ eva iti ced uktam atra sambandhe api ekatra kṛtāt anyatra apratītiḥ na ca sambandhaḥ asti iti api ca tad kāriṇām atatkāri bheda sāmye na kim kṛtaḥ yām artha kriyām adhikṛtya ayam artheṣu śabdāt niyuṅkte tad kāriṇām arthānām anyebhyaḥ bhedāt tatra eva ca eṣām abhede kim na śabdaḥ prayujyate tadvat doṣasya sāmyāt ced astu jātiḥ alam parā 
[047,19]	syāt etat anya vyāvṛtte api śabda arthe vyāvṛtti viśiṣṭasya tadvataḥ abhidhānāt na tadvat pakṣāt viśeṣaḥ kaḥ hi atra viśeṣaḥ vyāvṛttiḥ jātiḥ vyāvṛttimān jātimān iti astu nāma tadvat doṣaḥ jātiḥ anyā mā bhūt jātim api hi abhyupagacchatā avaśyam bhāvānām bhedaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ tad abhāve tasyāḥ api abhāva prasaṅgāt sa ca ekasmāt bhedaḥ tad anyeṣām abhedaḥ tad viśiṣṭeṣu artheṣu pratipattiḥ astu sarvathā doṣa parihārasya kartum aśakya tvāt artha antara abhyupagame prayojana abhāvāt tad arthasya anyena sādhanāt tad abhyupagamasya ca avaśyam bhāvi tvāt api ca 
[048,09_048,11]	tad anya parihāreṇa pravarteta iti ca dhvaniḥ ucyate tena tebhyaḥ asya avyavacchede katham ca saḥ śabdam hi eṣa prayuñjānaḥ artheṣu aniṣṭa parihāreṇa pravarteta iti ca prayuṅkte tatra anyatra ca pravṛtti anujñāyām tad nāma grahaṇa vaiyarthyāt pravṛtti nivṛtti anujñāyām ca eka codanāḥ anādarāt avacanam eva syāt anya vyāvṛtti anabhidhāne tasmāt avaśyam śabdena vyavacchedaḥ codanīyaḥ sa ca abhinnaḥ tad anyeṣu iti jāti dharmaḥ api asti tat niyata abhyupagamam niyata codanam jāti artha prasādhanam ca parityajya artha antara kalpanam kevalam anartha nirbandhaḥ eva yathākalpanam asya ayogāt na vai vyavacchedaḥ na kriyate pravṛtti viṣayam tu kathayadbhiḥ jātiḥ uktā 
[048,20_048,22^1]	vyavacchedaḥ asti ced asya nanu etāvat prayojanam śabdānām iti kim tatra sāmānyena apareṇa vaḥ nanu uktam pravṛtti viṣayaḥ pradarśyate iti uktam idam ayuktam tu uktam tathā hi na sā pravṛtti yogyāḥ iti niveditam etat tad dvāreṇa acodite pravṛttiḥ api pratyuktā tadvat codane ca vyavadhānam jāti tadvatoḥ pravṛtti viṣaya tve vyāvṛtti ta dvantau kim naḥ iṣyete vyāvṛtteḥ avastu tvena asādhana tvāt ced tat tulyam jāteḥ tadvataḥ sādhanāt adoṣaḥ iti ced tulyam tat vyāvṛttimataḥ avastu grāhī ca vyāvṛtti vādinām śābdaḥ pratyayaḥ sa vibhrama vaśāt akārake api kāraka adhyavasāyī pravartayati vastu saṃvādaḥ tu vastu utpattyā tad pratibandhe sati bhavati anyathā naḥ eva asti vastu utpatteḥ abhrāntiḥ iti ced na atad pratibhāsinaḥ tad adhyavasāyāt 
[048,22^2_049,16]	maṇi prabhāyām maṇi bhrānti darśanena vyabhicārāt ca bhrānteḥ avastu saṃvādaḥ iti ced na yathā uktena eva vyabhicārāt vitatha pratibhāsaḥ hi bhrānti lakṣaṇam tat na antarīyaka tayā tu saṃvādaḥ na pratibhāsā apekṣī vastuni tu yathābhāvam arpita cetasaḥ pravṛttau grāhyasya sāmānyasya anartha kriyā yogya tvāt apravṛttiḥ anyatra ca pravṛttau atiprasaṅgaḥ tadvat grahaṇe ca sāmānya vaiyarthya ādayaḥ proktāḥ jāti grahaṇe api sambandhāt śliṣṭa ābhāsā buddhiḥ pravartayati iti ced tadā na jātiḥ na tadvān ekasya api svabhāva sthiteḥ agrahaṇāt iti para vādaḥ eva āśritaḥ syāt evam tarhi anvayinaḥ kasyacid arthasya abhāvāt prakṛti bhinneṣu artheṣu tat eva idam iti pratyabhijñānam na syāt na eṣa doṣaḥ yasmāt jñāna ādi artha kriyām tām tām dṛṣṭvā bhede api kurvataḥ arthān tad anya viśleṣa viṣayaiḥ dhvanibhiḥ saha saṃyojya pratyabhijñānam kuryāt api anya darśane 
[049,19^1]	uktam etat bhede api bhāvāḥ tulya artha kriyā kāriṇaḥ cakṣuḥ ādi vat iti tām ekām jñāna ādikām artha kriyām teṣu paśyataḥ vastu dharma tayā eva anyebhyaḥ bhidyamānāḥ bhāvāḥ tad vyāvṛtti viṣaya dhvani saṃsṛṣṭam tat eva idam iti sva anubhava vāsanā prabodhena saṃsṛṣṭa bhedam mithyā pratyayam janayanti anyathā na bheda saṃsargavatī buddhiḥ syāt yathā daṇḍiṣu na hi tatra eka daṇḍa yoge api anyatra saḥ eva ayam iti bhavati kim tarhi tat iha iti na ca evam pratyabhijñānam kim tarhi tat eva idam iti tat na tat ekam anekatra paśyataḥ api bheda saṃsarga vat yuktam vibhrama balāt tu tathā jñāne na virodhaḥ nimitta abhāvāt vibhramaḥ ayuktaḥ iti ced te eva bhāvaḥ tad eka artha kāriṇaḥ anubhavadvāreṇa prakṛtyā vibhrama phalāyāḥ vikalpa vāsanāyāḥ hetu tvāt nimittam 
[049,19^2]	marīcika ādiṣu api hi jala ādi bhrānteḥ tau eka abhinna ākāra parāmarśa pratyaya nimitta anubhava jananau bhāvau kāraṇam bhinnau api na hi tatra anyat eva kiṃcid sāmānyam asti yat tathā pratīyeta sattve vā sat artha grāhiṇī buddhiḥ bhrāntiḥ na syāt abhūta ākāra samāropāt bhrāntiḥ iti ced na tarhi sā tad sāmānya grāhiṇī yam eva khalu ākāram iyam āropayati saḥ eva asyāḥ viṣayaḥ iti aviṣayīkṛtasya aśakya samāropāt ākāra antara vat sa ca tatra na asti iti asāmānyam sati sāmānya grahaṇe tad āropaḥ na anyathā atiprasaṅgāt iti ced sati eka kārya kāri grahaṇaḥ iti kim naḥ iṣyate avaśyam ca icchatā api sāmānyam vyaktīnām eka kārya janana śaktiḥ eṣṭavyā 
[049,19^3]	tatas te eva anyebhyaḥ bhidyamānāḥ tādṛśam pratyayam janayanti iti kim atra sāmānyena yathābhāvam eva asaṃsṛṣṭa bhedam kim na pratyeti iti ced aśaktiḥ eṣā vikalpānām avidyā prabhavāt na vai bāhya apekṣāḥ eva bhrāntayaḥ bhavanti kim tu viplavāt āntarāt api keśa ādi vibhrama vat avidyā udbhavāt viplava tve cakṣuḥ vijñāna ādiṣu api prasaṅgaḥ na tasyāḥ vikalpa lakṣaṇa tvāt vikalpaḥ eva hi avidyā sā svabhāvena eva viparyasyati na evam indriya jñānāni vikalpakāni na vā teṣu api eṣa doṣaḥ advayānām dvaya nirbhāsāt iti vakṣyāmaḥ sarveṣām viplave api pramāṇa tad ābhāsa vyavasthā ā āśraya parāvṛtteḥ artha kriyā yogya abhimata saṃvādanāt mithyātve api praśama anukūla tvāt mātṛ saṃjñā ādi vat 
[049,19^4]	marīcikāyām jala jñānasya anyasya ca bhinna bhāva utpatteḥ vibhramasya ca aviśeṣe api abhimata artha kriyā yogya ayogya utpatteḥ artha saṃvādāḥ itarau ayogyāt katham utpattiḥ iti ced vikalpānām artha pratibandha niyama abhāvāt na hi vikalpāḥ yathārtham eva jāyante sati marīcikā darśane jala bhrāntiḥ iti tad udbhavāḥ iti ucyate na tu yathā svabhāvam ajala vivekinā arthena svabhāva anukāra pratyarpaṇena jananāt sā tu viśeṣa lakṣaṇa apāṭavāt pratyaya apekṣiṇā sva vāsanā prabodhena janyate tasmāt bhinna bhāva janmanaḥ vikalpa vibhramāt tat eva idam iti pratyabhijñānam na vyatiriktasya sāmānyasya darśanāt na avyatiriktasya vyakti vat ananvayāt api ca 
[051,17_051,23]	parasya api na sā buddhiḥ sāmānyāt eva kevalāt na hi paraḥ api enām buddhim kevala sāmānya bhāvinīm vaktum arhati nityam tanmātra vijñāne vyakti ajñāna prasaṅgataḥ yadi hi nityam anayā buddhyā sāmānyam eva gṛhyeta apratītāḥ eva vyaktiḥ syāt anena jñānena tadā kadācid sambaddhasya agṛhītasya tadvataḥ 
[051,24_052,03]	tadvat tā aniścayaḥ na syāt vyavahāraḥ tatas katham yadā sāmānya grāhiṇaḥ vijñānasya na bhedaḥ ālambana bhāvena upayujyate tadā na tau kadācid api śliṣṭau gṛhītau iti idam asya sāmānyam ayam vā tadvān iti na syāt tathā ca tad pratipattyā tadvati pratipattiḥ na syāt artha antara vat eka vastu sahāyāḥ ced vyaktayaḥ jñāna kāraṇam 
[052,05_052,10]	syāt etat bhavanti vyaktayaḥ tasya ālambana bhāvena kāraṇam na tu kevalāḥ yadā punar āsām ekam sahakārī asti tadā tad sahitāḥ gṛhyante iti tat ekam vastu kim tāsām nānātvam samapohati nānā tvāt ca eka vijñāna hetu tā tāsu naḥ iṣyate kim vai teṣām bhedānām tena ekena nānātvam nirākriyate nānātvam hi teṣu eka vijñāna akāraṇa tve kāraṇam ucyate 
[052,12_052,16]	anekam api yadi ekam apekṣya abhinna buddhi kṛt na brūmaḥ anekam ekam pratyayam na janayati bhedāt iti na bhedaḥ janana virodhī kim tarhi kaivalyam tena ekena sahitāḥ janayanti eva evam tarhi tābhiḥ vinā api pratyekam kriyamāṇām dhiyam prati tena ekena api sāmarthyam tāsām naḥ iti agrahaḥ dhiyā 
[052,18]	katham idānīm vyaktīnām tatra jñāne sāmarthya gatiḥ pratyekam tāsām abhāve api tad bhāvāt asati sāmānye abhāvāt itarathā ca bhāvāt na eṣa doṣaḥ yathā nīla ādiṣu eka apāye api cakṣuḥ vijñānam bhavati iti na samūhe api teṣām asāmarthyam tathā iha api pratyekam eka apāye api bhavati iti na sarvadā sāmarthyam viṣamaḥ upanyāsaḥ tathā hi 
[053,01_053,03]	nīla ādeḥ netra vijñāne pṛthak sāmarthya darśanāt śakti siddhiḥ samūhe api na evam vyakteḥ kathaṃcana nīla ādīnām hi cakṣuḥ vijñāne pratyekam api sāmarthyam dṛṣṭam iti samūhe api śaktiḥ aviruddhā tathā na kadācid vyaktayaḥ sāmānya nirapekṣāḥ anvayi vijñānam janayanti tasmāt asamarthāḥ eva vyaktayaḥ tatra iti na tena gṛhyeran 
[053,07_053,08]	tāsām anyatama apekṣam tat ced śaktam na kevalam atha api syāt na vema rahitaḥ kuvindaḥ paṭam karoti prati ekam vema abhāve api kuvindaḥ karoti iti na tatas eva paṭa utpattiḥ tathā na kevalam ekaika vyakti apāye vijñāna utpattau api sāmānyam tad hetuḥ kim tarhi vyaktīnām ekām kāṃcid apekṣya vijñānam utpādayati evam sati 
[053,13_053,20]	tat ekam upakuryuḥ tāḥ katham ekām dhiyam ca na bhinnānām hi arthānām eka artha upakriyā virodhinī iti sarvaḥ ayam ārambhaḥ tāḥ ced vyaktayaḥ bhinnāḥ api ekam sāmānyam upakurvanti kaḥ punar āsām vijñānena aparādhaḥ kṛtaḥ yat tat naḥ upakurvanti kim antar gaḍunā sāmānyena yathā asambhinnānām api eka sāmānya upakaraṇa śaktiḥ evam tat eva ekam vijñānam kurvantu kim ca kāryaḥ ca tāsām prāptaḥ asau jananam yat upakriyā 
[053,21^1]	na hi anatiśayam ātmānam asya pūrvavat bibhrataḥ kaścid upakārakaḥ nāma atiprasaṅgāt artha antara janane api tasya kim tena tasya tad āśraya tve anupakāriṇaḥ kaḥ ayam āśraya āśrayi bhāvaḥ atiprasaṅgaḥ vā upakāre api tatra eva tad pratibandhaḥ iti kim anyaḥ tad karaṇāt tad upakārī tad apekṣasya āśrayasya tad upayoge anupakārya tve kā iyam apekṣā nāma tad utpatti dharmā dharmāḥ bhāvaḥ svabhāva pratibandhāt apekṣate nāma anādheya atiśaya ātmā paraiḥ apekṣate ca iti vyāhatam etat tasmāt yaḥ kaścid kasyacid kvacid pratibandhaḥ sa sarvaḥ janyatāyām eva antarbhavati para bhāva utpādane tad anupakārāt akiṃcitkarasya ca anupakārāt tasmāt vyakti upakṛtasya sāmānyasya vijñāna janane janane vyaktam asya tad kāryatā anuyujyate 
[053,21^2]	kevalasya sāmarthye api vyaktīnām kvacid api atra sāmarthya asiddheḥ agrāhya tvam samarthāḥ vyaktayaḥ vijñāne pratibhāsanāt iti ced katham asiddha upakārāṇām pratibhāsaḥ iti saḥ eva sāmānya abhyupagame cintyate yasmāt na anupakārakaḥ viṣayaḥ ati prasaṅgāt na aviṣayasya vijñāne pratibhāsaḥ anupakārakasya aviṣaya tve atīta anāgata ādīnām aviṣaya tvam asatām upakāra asāmarthyāt iti ced bhavantu nāma tad viṣayāṇi nirviṣayāṇi nirviṣaya tve api tad anukārī pratibhāsaḥ tad rūpa anubhava ahita vāsanā utpatteḥ ātma bhūtaḥ eva vijñānasya bhāva abhāva anuvidhānāt ca sāmarthyam na pratibhāsanāt apratibhāsinaḥ api vyakti vyatirekeṇa sāmānyasya bhāvāt pratibhāsinām api keśa ādi viplavānām abhāvāt 
[054,17_054,18^1]	abhinna pratibhāsā dhīḥ na bhinneṣu iti ced matam na brūmaḥ anekam eka kārya kṛt na bhavati iti kim tarhi na bhinneṣu artheṣu arpita tad ākārā buddhiḥ abhinna pratibhāsinī syāt na vai sāmānya grāhiṇīṣu sva lakṣaṇa pratibhāsaḥ tad abhāve api tāsām bhāvāt ākāra antareṇa ca sva jñāne pratibhāsanāt aneka ākāra ayogāt ekasya atiprasaṅgāt ca tasmāt naḥ iyam bhinna artha grāhiṇī abhinnā pratibhāti tad udbhavā atad pratibhāsinī api adhyavasāya vibhramāt vyavahārayati lokam sa tu tasyām pratibhāsamānaḥ ākāraḥ na artheṣu asti anyatra bhedāt abhedinaḥ sa ca arūpaḥ 
[054,18^2]	tam eva eṣā gṛhṇatī tathā viplavataḥ iti uktam prāk api ca vastu sāmānya vādinaḥ api hi bhinnāḥ eva vyaktayaḥ katham tāsu abhinna ākārā buddhiḥ iti tulyam codyam na tulyam tatra abhinnasya sāmānyasya sadbhāvāt nanu tatra tasya ābhāsaḥ sataḥ api na lakṣyate sā hi varṇa saṃsthāna pratibhāsavatī vibhāvyate na ca īdṛśam sāmānyam na ca tatas vyatiriktaḥ kaścid abhinnaḥ ākāraḥ asti ākṛti sāmānya vādinaḥ api viśeṣa vat tasya avyatirekāt artha antare avṛttiḥ iti bhedāt na abhinna pratibhāsaḥ yujyate athavā astu
[055,14_055,15]	pratibhāsaḥ dhiyam bhinnaḥ samānāḥ iti tad grahāt na eva tāsu abhinnaḥ pratibhāsaḥ asti samānāḥ iti grahāt na hi ekasmin pratibhāse samānāḥ iti yuktam kim tarhi tat eva iti dvayasya grahaṇāt adoṣaḥ iti ced tathā api tat iha iti syāt na samānaḥ iti tat eva tāsām sāmyam iti ced katham anyonyasya sāmyam tad sambandhāt iti ced na pratibaddhasya sambandha ayogāt atiprasaṅgāt ca 
[055,21_056,06]	katham tāḥ bhinna dhī grāhyāḥ samāḥ ced nanu samānāḥ iti grahaṇāt eva āsu abhinna pratibhāsaḥ na vai tad darśane bhinna abhinnayoḥ pratibhāsanāt samānāḥ iti pratītiḥ kim tarhi eka kārya tā sādṛśyam na hi vayam artha jñāne dvau ākārau paśyāmaḥ apaśyantaḥ ca katham artha dvaya kalpanena ātmānam eva vipralabhāmahe eka kāryāḥ tu vyaktayaḥ kalpanā viṣaya tām upayāntyaḥ tathā anayā vibhramāt miśrīkriyante iti anavadyam etat 
[056,10_056,16]	 nanu dhīḥ kāryam tāsām sā ca vibhidyate pratibhāvam tadvat tad pratibhāsinaḥ vijñānasya api bhedāt katham eka kāryāḥ tat hi tāsām kāryam tat ca bhidyate yat api udaka āharaṇa ādikam ekam ghaṭa ādi kāryam tat api pratidravyam bhedāt bhidyate eva iti naḥ ekam bhedānām kāryam asti na eṣa doṣaḥ yasmāt eka pratyavamarśasya hetu tvāt dhīḥ abhedinī ekadhī hetu bhāvena vyaktīnām api abhinnatā 
[056,18]	niveditam etat yathā na bhāvānām svabhāva saṃsargaḥ asti iti tatra saṃsṛṣṭa ākārā buddhiḥ bhrāntiḥ eva tām tu bhedinaḥ padārthāḥ krameṇa vikalpa hetavaḥ bhavantaḥ janayanti svabhāvataḥ iti ca sa tu eṣām abhinnaḥ bhedaḥ iti ucyate jñāna ādeḥ kasyacid ekasya karaṇāt atatkāri svabhāva vivekaḥ tat api pratidravyam bhidyamānam api prakṛtyāḥ eka pratyavamarśasya abheda avaskandinaḥ hetuḥ bhavat abhinnam khyāti tathābhūta pratyavamarśa hetoḥ abheda avabhāsinaḥ jñāna ādeḥ arthasya hetu tvāt vyaktayaḥ api saṃsṛṣṭa ākāram svabhāva bheda parama artham svabhāvataḥ ekam pratyayam janayanti iti asakṛt uktam etat tasmāt eka kārya tā eva bhāvānām abhedaḥ
