[057,08_057,16]	sā ca atad kārya viśleṣaḥ eva tad anyasya anuvartinaḥ vastunaḥ adṛṣṭeḥ pratiṣedhāt ca na hi dṛśyam vibhāgena apratibhāsamānam asti iti uktam etat sati vā kvacid anāśritam katham jñāna hetuḥ iti pratiṣedhasya ca vidhānāt tad kalpanāḥ ayuktāḥ iti tasmāt saṃketas 
[057,17_058,01]	api tad vidarthikaḥ eva yuktaḥ yaḥ ayam anyonyam vivekaḥ bhāvānām tad pratītayaḥ eva saṃketaḥ api kriyamāṇaḥ śobheta atatkāri vivekena pravṛtti artha tayā yadi hi na tat prati iti arthaḥ saṃketaḥ tasya vyavahāra kāle api asaṃsparśāt na anya parihāreṇa pravarteta na hi sa teṣām tebhyaḥ vivekaḥ śabdena coditaḥ iti sā ca śrutiḥ akārya kṛti tad kāri tulya rūpa avabhāsinīm dhiyam vastu pṛthak bhāva mātra bījām anarthikām janayanti api atatkāri parihāra aṅga bhāvataḥ vastu bheda āśrayāt ca arthe na visaṃvādikā matā tatas anya apoha viṣayā tad kartṛ āśrita bhāvataḥ 
[058,06]	eka svabhāva rahiteṣu artheṣu tam adhyāropya utpadyamānām mithyā pratibhāsi tvāt akārya kāriṇam api tad kārya kāriṇam iva adhyavasyantīm vastu pṛthak bhāva mātra bījām samāna adhyavasāyām mithyā buddhim śrutiḥ janayanti api tad anya parihāra aṅga abhāvāt paramārthataḥ tad vyatirekiṣu padārtheṣu na visaṃvādikāḥ iti ucyate tathā hi sa teṣu vyatirekaḥ bhūtaḥ sarvathā avyatikramaṇīya tvāt na ekaḥ vyatiriktaḥ avyatiriktaḥ vā sarvathā ayogāt tasya samāveśane vastuni dūra utsṛṣṭam eva vastu syāt śabda jñānābhyām tad viṣaya abhimatasya tasya abhāvāt anyasya ca vastu dharmasya kasyacid asaṃsparśāt tatas eva ca sā śrutiḥ anya apoha viṣayayā iti ucyate anya vyāvṛtteṣu artheṣu vyāvṛtti bhedam upādāya aviśeṣeṇa niveśanāt vyavahāre api anya parihāreṇa pravartanāt 
[058,19_058,22]	avṛkṣa vyatirekeṇa vṛkṣa artha grahaṇe dvayam anyonya āśrayam iti eka graha abhāve dvayāgrahaḥ saṃketā sambhavaḥ tasmāt iti kecid pracakṣate yadi avṛkṣebhyaḥ bhedaḥ vṛkṣaḥ tasya avṛkṣa grahaṇam antareṇa tathā grahītum aśakya tvāt avijñāta vṛkṣeṇa avṛkṣasya api tad vyavaccheda rūpasya aparijñānāt buddhau anārūḍhe arthe na saṃketaḥ śakyate iti eke 
[059,01_059,07]	teṣām avṛkṣāḥ saṃkete vyavacchinnā na vā yaḥ evam ekam vastu sāmānyam abhyupagamya itaretara āśrayam anya vyavacchedena saṃkete codayanti teṣām tatra api saṃketa karaṇe avṛkṣāḥ vyavacchinnāḥ na vā yadi vyavacchinnāḥ katham jñātāḥ prāk vṛkṣa grahaṇāt ṛte na hi tadā pratipattā vṛkṣam vetti na avṛkṣam tat jñānāya eva tad arthitayā upagamāt saḥ ajānānaḥ katham avṛkṣa vyavacchedam pratipadyeta saṃkete apratipattau ca aparihṛta tad anya niveśinaḥ śabdāt 
[059,11_059,15]	anirākaraṇe teṣām saṃkete vyavahāriṇām na syāt tad parihāreṇa pravṛttiḥ vṛkṣa bheda vat na hi saṃkete para avyavacchedena niveśitāt śabdāt vyavahāre tad parihāreṇa pravṛttiḥ yuktā śiṃśapā ādi bheda vat atha api syāt avidhāya niṣidhya anyat pradarśya ekam puras sthitam vṛkṣaḥ ayam iti saṃketaḥ kriyate tat prapadyate vyavahāre api tena ayam adoṣaḥ iti ced 
[059,18_060,02]	na vai vastu sat sāmānya vādinā kasyacid vyavacchedena kiṃcid vidhīyate kim tarhi ekam agratas vyavasthitam vastu sandarśya vṛkṣaḥ ayam iti saṃketaḥ kriyate saṃketa kāle tathā adṛṣṭam eva ayam artham tad sambandhinam vā vyavahāre api pratipadyate iti na samānaḥ prasaṅgaḥ na samānaḥ yasmāt tatra api taruḥ ayam api ayam eva iti prasaṅgaḥ na nivartate 
[060,04]	ekam pradarśya ayam vṛkṣaḥ iti api bruvāṇaḥ ayam api ayam eva iti ubhayīm gatim na ativartate tayoḥ ca saḥ eva doṣaḥ na doṣaḥ dṛṣṭa viparītasya su jñāna tvāt ekam hi kiṃcid paśyataḥ anyatra tad ākāra vivekinīm buddhim anubhavataḥ tatas anyat iti yathā anubhavam tad vivecanaḥ vaidharmya niścayaḥ utpadyate sa hi ayam eva vṛkṣaḥ iti pradarśya vyutpāditaḥ yatra eva tam na paśyati tam eva avṛkṣam svayam eva pratipadyate na idam vyavaccheda vādinaḥ sambhavati ekatra dṛṣṭasya rūpasya kvacid ananvayāt darśanena pratipattau vyakti antare api na syāt tathā pratītiḥ evam tarhi tatra api tulyam etat yasmāt 
[060,14_060,19]	eka pratyavamarśa ākhye jñānaḥ ekatra hi sthitaḥ prapattā tat atad hetūn arthān vibhajate svayam niveditam etat prāk yathā ete bhāvāḥ prakṛti bhedinaḥ api jñāna ādikam ekam kāryam kecid kurvanti na anyaḥ iti tān ayam tatra svayam eva tad hetūn atad hetūn ca vibhajya pratyeti tasya tad buddhi vartinaḥ bhāvān bhātaḥ hetu tayā dhiyaḥ ahetu rūpa vikalān eka rūpān iva svayam bhedena pratipadyeta iti uktiḥ bhede niyujyate tam tasyāḥ pratiyatī dhīḥ bhrāntyā ekam vastu iva īkṣyate 
[060,23^1]	teṣām prakṛtyāḥ eva pratyaya vaśāt tathābhūta vikalpa kāraṇānām anvayāt tat draṣṭuḥ buddhau viparivartamānān tad jñāna hetu tayā tad anya vyāvṛttyā ca atathābhūtān api tathā adhyavasitān avibhakta bāhya ādhyātmika bhedān pratipattā pratipattim anusṛtya ete vṛkṣāḥ iti sva para vikalpeṣu eka pratibhāsān ādarśya vikalpa vijñāne vyavasthitaḥ tad vijñāna hetūn bhedena pratipadyeta iti uktim atad dhetubhyaḥ bhede niyuṅkte tam tasyāḥ pratipadyamānā buddhiḥ vikalpikā bhrānti vaśāt eva eka vastu grahiṇī iva pratibhāti 
[060,23^2_061,12]	na punar ekam vastu tatra dṛśyam asti yasya darśana adarśanābhyām bhinna darśane api eṣa vṛkṣāvṛkṣa vibhāgam kurvīta tasya śākhā ādi pratibhāsa vibhāgena daṇḍa vat daṇḍinī agrahaṇāt agṛhītasya ca apara pravibhāgena anupalakṣaṇāt ākṛteḥ api ekatra dṛṣṭāyāḥ anyatra draṣṭum aśakya tvāt tat atadvatoḥ vṛkṣāvṛkṣa tve vyaktiḥ ekaḥ eva vṛkṣaḥ syāt bhavatu nāma ghaṭa ādi śabdeṣu artha antara vyavacchedaḥ atha jñeya ādi padeṣu katham na hi ajñeyam kiṃcid asti yatas bhedaḥ syāt tatas bhedena viṣayīkaraṇaḥ eva tasya jñeya tvāt na eṣa doṣaḥ yasmāt kvacid niveśanāya arthe vinivartya kutaścana buddheḥ prayujyate śabdaḥ tad arthasya avadhāraṇāt vyarthaḥ anyathā prayogaḥ syāt tat jñeya ādi padeṣu api vyavahāra upanīteṣu vyavacchedyaḥ asti kaścana 
[061,16^1]	śabdam hi prayuñjānaḥ sarvaḥ anvaya vyatirekau na ativartate tasya pravṛtti nivṛtti artha tvāt yadi hi ayam na kasyacid kutaścid nivartayet pravartayet vā buddhim yathābhūta anujñānāt sarva vyavahāreṣu na kiṃcid vyāharet vyāhārasya avadhāraṇana āntarīyaka tvāt yathā ghaṭena udakam ānaya iti yadi ghaṭena añjalinā vā udaka ānayanam yathā kathaṃcid abhimatam syāt udakam ānaya iti eva vaktavyam syāt na ghaṭena iti tathā paṃśunā vā anena vā yena kenacid ānītena arthaḥ ānaya iti eva syāt anākṣipta karaṇa karmakam evam ānayanam anyat vā yat kiṃcid anuṣṭhānam vai abhimatam tadā ānaya iti api na brūyāt vyartha tvāt vacanasya tathā vyavahāra upanītānām jñeya ādi padānām api kenacid vyavacchedyena bhavitavyam ananyāśaṅkāyām prayoga ayogāt tatra hi yat eva mūḍha mateḥ āśaṅkā sthānam tat eva nivartyam 
[061,16^2]	anāśaṅkamānaḥ vā kim parasmāt upadeśam apekṣate aśrotṛ saṃskāram ca bruvāṇaḥ katham naḥ unmattaḥ tad saṃskārāya eva śabdānām kṛta saṃketa tvāt avyavahāra upanītaḥ ca naḥ eva kaścid jñeya ādi śabdaḥ asti vākya gatasya padasya artha cintanāt kva punar ete śabdāḥ prayujyante iti prayoga viṣaya cintāyām anya apohaḥ ucyate anirdiṣṭa prayogam tu jñeya śabdasya kaḥ arthaḥ iti praśne na kaścid arthaḥ tatas kvacid apratipatteḥ tathā ghaṭa ādi śabdānām api yāḥ api kvacid prakaraṇe kevala śabda śravaṇāt pratipattiḥ dṛṣṭa prayoga anusāreṇa sa ākāṅkṣa tvāt sā aparisamāpta tad viplavaḥ eva ghaṭa ādi śabdeṣu tādṛśaḥ jñeya ādi śabdeṣu api yathādarśanam asti eva tasmāt sarve eva śabda prayogaḥ kutaścid buddhim nivartya kvacid niveśana arthaḥ tat sāphalyāt 
[062,16]	niveśanam ca yaḥ yasmāt bhidyate vinivartya tam tad bhede bhidyamānānām samāna ākāra bhāsini sa ca ayam anya vyāvṛttyā gamyate tasya vastunaḥ kaścid bhāgaḥ iti proktaḥ rūpam na asya api kiṃcana tad gatau eva śabdebhyaḥ gamyate anya nivartanam na tatra gamyate kaścid viśiṣṭaḥ kenacid paraḥ na ca api śabdaḥ dvaya kṛt anyonya abhāvaḥ iti asan arūpaḥ rūpavat tvena darśanam buddhi viplavaḥ 
[062,24^1]	niveśyamānaḥ api eṣa śabdaḥ yasmāt bhidyate tam vinivartya bhidyamānānām bhede samāna rūpa pratibhāsinī ākṣipta tad anya vyāvṛttiḥ niveśyate iti saḥ eva ayam artha antara vyāvṛttyā tasya vastunaḥ kaścid bhāgaḥ gamyate śabdaḥ artha antara nivṛtti viśiṣṭān eva bhāvān āha iti ādinā nirdiṣṭaḥ sa hi tam bhedam kathayan artha antara vyavacchedam ākṣipan eva vartate eka gata bheda codanāyāḥ tad anya vyāvṛtti ākṣepana āntarīyaka tvāt saḥ eva bhedaḥ tad vyāvṛttyā gataḥ bhāgaḥ tad gateḥ tad upādhi tvāt tad viśiṣṭaḥ gataḥ iti ucyate na punar artha antara nivṛttiḥ viśeṣaṇa bhūtā keṣāṃcid arthānām yayā viśiṣṭāḥ śabdaiḥ codyante daṇḍi vat 
[062,24^2_064,01]	dvayoḥ hi bhidyamānayoḥ bhedasya ubhaya gata tvāt eka bheda abhidhāne api na antarīyakaḥ tad anyākṣepaḥ bhavati iti tayoḥ na viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ eka bheda abhidhāne api anya vyāvṛtti gateḥ anvaya vyatireka codanayā vyavahāra aṅgatām śabdānām darśayan tad vyāvṛttyā gamyate tad viśiṣṭaḥ vā iti āha atas eva ca śabdasya na dvau vyāpārau tad anya vyāvartanam sva artha abhidhānam ca sva artha abhidhānāt eva tad anyavyāvṛtti gateḥ sva arthasya bheda rūpa tvāt na hi anvayaḥ avyatirekaḥ ananvayaḥ vā vyatirekaḥ eka anvayasya parihārya abhāve niṣphala codana tvāt tathā eka parihārasya kvacid sthiti abhāve sa ca ayam bhedaḥ arūpaḥ rūpavat tvena tu asya darśanam kevalam buddhi viplavaḥ eva tena eva aparama arthaḥ asau anyathā na hi vastunaḥ vyāvṛttiḥ vastu bhavati bhedaḥ asya asmāt iti īraṇāt 
[064,03]	rūpam hi parama arthaḥ bhedaḥ ced rūpam syāt tad rūpam vā syāt atad rūpam vā tādrūpye tat eva iti na anyaḥ tatas bhidyeta na hi tasya rūpam anyasya syāt na tat eva bhedasya rūpam rūpam ca anyat eva syāt tatas ca bhāvaḥ tasmāt vyāvarteta tatas asmāt tasya bhedaḥ iti na syāt yat khalu yat bhedāt vyāvartate tat eva tat bhavati iti saḥ asya bhedaḥ iti ca na syāt na hi anyonyasya bhedaḥ bhavati sambandha abhāvāt sati vā sa kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ iti rūpam tat janitam bhedaḥ iti aviśeṣāt sarva kāryāṇi sva kāraṇānām vyāvṛttayaḥ syuḥ rūpa antara tve ca bhedasya tatas api asya bhedaḥ iti bheda upādhi tvāt dravya antara vat na bhedaḥ syāt na hi bheda upādhiḥ eva bhedaḥ ayam atas iti viśeṣa nirdeśāt tatas ca upādhi abhāve bhedasya eva abhāvaḥ syāt tasmāt na vyatiriktaḥ tad anyagati abhāvāt ca vastunaḥ na parama arthaḥ katham tarhi abhinnasya vastunaḥ śabdena codane tasya eva anyatas api bhedāt anaṃśaya eka bheda codane sarva bheda gateḥ tatra śabda pramāṇa antarāṇi vyarthāni na syuḥ yasmāt 
[064,19_064,23]	eka artha śleṣa vicchedaḥ ekaḥ vyāpriyate dhvaniḥ liṅgam vā tatra vicchinnam vācyam vastu na kiṃcana yasya abhidhānataḥ vastu sāmarthyāt akhile gatiḥ bhavet nānā phalaḥ śabdaḥ eka ādhāraḥ bhavati atas uktam prāk yathā saṃsṛṣṭa bāhya ādhyātmika bhedā buddhiḥ svam eva ābhāsam vyavahāra viṣayam artha kriyā yogyam adhyavasāya śabda artham upanayati iti tatra eva ca te śabdāḥ taiḥ taiḥ bhrānti kāraṇaiḥ saṃsṛṣṭa rūpaḥ iva ābhāti yathā saṃketam vicchedāya vyāpriyante na ca eka sādhyam vyavacchedam anyaḥ karoti saṃketa pratiniyamāt na ca vicchinnam kiṃcid vastu ākṣipyate yasya abhidhānāt vastu balena akhile gatiḥ syāt śabdānām buddhi viplava viṣaya tvāt tatra ca avastuni vastu sāmarthya abhāvāt tathābhūta artha darśana dvāreṇa ayam nānā eka dharma bheda abheda pratibhāsa viplava anusārī vyavahāraḥ iti tasya tad pratibandhe sati tat avyabhicāraḥ tatas vitathāt api ante tathābhūtaḥ eva vastuni jñāna saṃvādāt na punar bhinna ākāra grāhiṇām jñāna śabdānām eka vastu viṣaya tvāt nānā phalaḥ śabdaḥ eka ādhāraḥ vyāghātāt yathā varṇite tu buddhi pratibhāsā āśraye na doṣaḥ iti 
[065,10]	vicchedam sūcayan ekam apratikṣipya vartate yadā anyam tena sa vyāptaḥ eka tvena ca bhāsate sāmānādhikaraṇyam syāt tadā buddhi anurodhataḥ vastu dharmasya saṃsparśaḥ viccheda karaṇe dhvaneḥ syāt satyam sa hi tatra iti naḥ eka vastu abhidhāyini buddhau abhāsamānasya dṛśyasya abhāva niścayāt 
[065,16_065,23]	iti antaraślokāḥ tena anya apoha viṣayāḥ proktāḥ sāmānya gocarāḥ śabdāḥ ca buddhayaḥ ca eva vastuni eṣām asambhavāt yadi hi vidhi rūpeṇa vastu eva śabdaiḥ vikalpaiḥ vā api viṣayīkriyeta saḥ ayam sarva artha sarva ākāra pratīti prasaṅgaḥ asāmānādhikaraṇya ādayaḥ ca iti manyamānaḥ praṇetāḥ nyāya śāstrasya anya apoha viṣayau etau prāha tathā hi eka tvāt vastu rūpasya bhinna rūpā matiḥ kutas anvaya vyatirekau vā na ekasya eka artha gocarau 
[065,25]	tat ekam anaṃśam vastu katham bhinna ākārābhiḥ buddhibhiḥ viṣayīkriyate ākāra bheda āśraya tvāt bhedasya tasya ca abhedāt tad ā ātmanaḥ api sāmānyasya tad eka yogakṣema tvāt tat ayam anyonya artha parihāreṇa eka viṣayayoḥ vṛtti abhāvāt sāmānādhikaraṇya ādiḥ na ca vastu ātmanaḥ ekasya tatra eva vṛttiḥ avṛttiḥ ca yuktā vyāghātāt na ca anyatra avartamānam sāmānyam syāt sāmānyasya vṛttiḥ na viśeṣasya iti ced na bheda abhāvāt tat hi eka rūpam sāmānyam vā bhavet viśeṣaḥ vā na hi asati rūpa bhede ayam pravibhāgaḥ yuktaḥ sati vai avyatirekaḥ na syāt iti uktam tat ayam avibhāgaḥ anviyāt vā na vā na punar ananvayaḥ anvayī ca yaḥ api bhinnam eva sāmānyam āha tasya api abheda vyavahārāḥ ca bhede syuḥ anibandhanāḥ yathāsvam śabdāḥ bhinnam artham abhidadhānāḥ katham eka artha buddhi āśrayāḥ syuḥ artha antara abhidhāyinaḥ ca anākṣepakāḥ
[066,11_066,15]	nirākāṅkṣa tvāt katham viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva āśrayāḥ sarvatra bhāvāt vyāvṛtteḥ na ete doṣāḥ prasaṅginaḥ yathā hi ekaḥ tasmāt bhinnaḥ tathā anyaḥ api iti bhedasya asāmānya doṣaḥ api na asti pariśiṣṭa abhāvaḥ tu prāk eva uktaḥ api ca eka kāryeṣu bhedeṣu tad kārya paricodane gaurava aśakti vaiphalyāt bheda ākhyāyāḥ samā śrutiḥ kṛtā vṛddhaiḥ atad kārya vyāvṛtti vinibandhanā na bhāve sarva bhāvānām svabhāvasya vyavasthiteḥ yat rūpam śābaleyasya bāhuleyasya na asti tat atad kārya parāvṛttiḥ dvayoḥ api ca vidyate artha abhedena ca vinā śabda abhedaḥ na yujyate tasmāt tad kāryatā api iṣṭā atad kāryāt eva bhinna tā cakṣuḥ ādau yathā rūpa vijñāna eka phale kvacid aviśeṣeṇa tad kārya codanā sambhave sati sakṛt sarva prati iti artham kaścid sāṃketikīm śrutim kuryāt ṛte api tad rūpa sāmānyāt vyatirekiṇaḥ 
[067,01^1]	yaḥ api manyate katham abhinnam artham antareṇa bahuṣu ekā śrutiḥ teṣām asāmyāt eka vṛtteḥ anyatra pratyaya ajananāt apratyāsattike ca pratyaya utpāde ati prasaṅgāt teṣu ca eka śabda niveśana vaiphalyāt eka artha niyoga abhāvāt bhinna svabhāvānām pṛthak niyoge ca tathā coditānām vibhāga aparijñānāt iti tasya api ekam asti iti eva lokena śabdaḥ niveśanīyaḥ tat vai ekam enām śrutim vastu śaktyā eva dhvanayati iti na asti etat kim tarhi kenacid prayojanena kecid śabdāḥ kvacid niveśyante tatra yadi anekam ekatra upayujyeta tat avaśyam tatra codanīyam tasya pṛthak pṛthak codane ati gauravam syāt na ca asya ananya sādhāraṇam rūpam śakyam codayitum na api asya āyāsa asya kiṃcid sāphalyam kevalam anena tatra yogyāḥ te arthāḥ codanīyāḥ te ekena vā śabdena ca udyeran bahubhiḥ vā iti svātantryam atra vaktuḥ tat iyam ekā śrutiḥ bahuṣu vaktrabhiprāya vaśāt pravartamānā na upālambham arhati 
[067,01^2]	na ca iyam aśakya pravartanā icchā adhīna tvāt yadi hi na prayoktuḥ icchā katham iyam ekatra api pravarteta icchāyām vā kaḥ enām bahuṣu api pratibandhum samarthaḥ prayojana abhāvāt eva apravartanam iti ced uktam prayojanam bhinneṣu ekasmāt pratītiḥ atad prayojana bhedena iti uktam na punar svabhāvasya eka tvāt yathāsvam vyavasthita svabhāvānām anyonya rūpa āśleṣāt katham eka svabhāva nimittaḥ śabdaḥ bhinneṣu bhavet iti uktam prāk atad prayojana vyāvṛttiḥ tu bhinnānām aviruddhāḥ iti saḥ eva artha abhedaḥ śabda abhedasya kāraṇam bhavatu tena ime tad prayojanāḥ iti atad prayojanebhyaḥ bhinnāḥ eva uktāḥ na punar eṣām anyā tad kāryatā anyatra anyatas bhedāt yathā cakṣu ūru upāloka manaskāresu ātma indriya manaḥ artha tad saṃnikarṣeṣu vā rūpa vijñāna eka kāryeṣu tad kārya sāmānya codanā sambhave kutas rūpa vijñānam iti vyavahāra lāghava artham kaścid sāṃketikīm śrutim niveśayet yaraḥ rūpa vijñāna hetuḥ śasaḥ vā iti 
[067,01^3]	api nāma sarveṣām tad hetūnām sakṛt pratītiḥ yathā syāt iti na ca atra anugāmi kiṃcid rūpam asti kevalam tad artha tayā te bhāvāḥ atad arthebhyaḥ bhinnāḥ iti bhedaḥ eva eṣām abhedaḥ evaṃjātīyāḥ ca sarve samūha santāna avasthā viśeṣa śabdāḥ ye samastāḥ kiṃcid ekam kāryam kurvanti teṣām tatra viśeṣa abhāvāt apārthikāḥ viśeṣa codanāḥ iti sakṛt sarveṣām niyojana artham ekam ayam lokaḥ śabdam teṣu niyuṅkte ghaṭaḥ iti te api sajātīyāt anyatas ca bheda aviśeṣe api tad prayojana aṅga tayā tad anyebhyaḥ bhidyante iti abhedāt tatas aviśeṣeṇa pratīyante tatra ghaṭasya rūpa ādayaḥ iti api ghaṭa svabhāvāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ udaka dhāraṇa viśeṣa ādi kārya samarthāḥ iti yāvat sāmānya kārya sādhana prasiddhena ātmanā rūpa ādi śabdaiḥ prasiddhāḥ viśiṣṭa kārya sādhana ākhyena viśeṣeṇa viśiṣṭāḥ te evam ucyante na punar atra anyat kiṃcid yathāvarṇita lakṣaṇam dravyam asti tasya tādṛśasya anupalambhāt eka vacanam api tad eka śakti sūcana artham saṃketa paratantram vā 
[067,01^4]	tathā ye hetu phala viśeṣa bhūtāḥ kiṃcid ekam sādhayanti sādhyante vā te api sakṛt pratyaya artham vrīhi ādi śabdaiḥ kṛta saṃketāḥ kathyante iti pūrvavat vācyam ye api pṛthak samastāḥ vā kvacid upayujyante te avasthā viśeṣa vācibhiḥ sakṛt eva śabdaiḥ pratyaya artham khyāpyante sa nidarśanāḥ sa pratighāḥ vā iti tad anyebhyaḥ bheda sāmānyena yathā eka kāryāḥ tad kārya codanāyām tad anya bhedena ghaṭa ādi śabdaiḥ kṛta samayāḥ tathā kāraṇa apekṣayā api anekaḥ ekena vyavahāra artham eva yathā śābaleyaḥ bāhuleyaḥ prayatna anantarīyakaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtakaḥ vā iti tathā tad kārya pratiṣedhena api acākṣuṣaḥ śabdaḥ anityaḥ anātmaḥ iti tad kāraṇa pratiṣedhena api asvāmikaḥ śūnyaḥ iti evam yathāyogam anyat api vācyam śūnyān ityādi śabdeṣu yathākalpanam samīhita ākāram buddhau āropya tad vyavacchedena vyapadeśaḥ kriyate buddhi samīhā sandarśita vibhāga tvāt sarvasya śabda arthasya apratipakṣa doṣa upakṣepa ādayaḥ durmati vispanditāni iti upekṣanīyāḥ atha
[069,10_069,20]	eka vṛtteḥ anekaḥ api yadi eka śrutimān bhavet na kevalam eka kāryāḥ tad anya bheda aviśeṣāt eka śabdena ucyante api tu eka vṛttyā api anekaḥ eka śabdena ucyeta kaḥ virodhaḥ syāt uktam atra tasya upalabhya abhimatasya anupalabdheḥ abhāvāt anupalabhyatāyām vā tad darśana āśrayāḥ vyapadeśa pratyabhijñāna ādayaḥ na bhaveyuḥ iti ādi api ca vṛttiḥ ādheya tā vyaktiḥ iti tasmin na yujyate yat etat ekam anekatra vartamānam ekām śrutim vartayati tasya kā iyam vṛttiḥ ādheya tā vā syāt yathā kuṇḍe badarāṇi vartante iti vyaktiḥ vā taiḥ abhivyakteḥ yadi ādheya tā nityasya anupakārya tvāt naḥ ādhāraḥ 
[069,21_070,14]	nityam hi sāmānyam iṣyate anitya tve apara apara utpatteḥ anekatvāt bheda vat eka pratyaya ayogāt nityasya ca kim kurvāṇaḥ ādhāraḥ syāt tasya tatra samavāyāt ādhāraḥ iti ced kaḥ ayam samavāyaḥ nāma apṛthak siddhānām āśraya āśrayi bhāvaḥ tat eva idam anupakārakasya āśraya tvam na sambhāvayāmaḥ atiprasaṅga bhayāt tasmāt samavāya saṃyogau eka artha samavāya ādayaḥ api vastu sambandhāḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt na vyatiricyante parasparam anyatas vā anupakāriṇām apratibandhāt apratibaddhasya ca asambandhāt yadi api eka artha samavāyinām parasparam anupakāraḥ tatas ekasmāt upakāreṇa bhāvyam abhāve yathā ukta doṣa prasaṅgāt atas sva upakāra dvāreṇa eva param api buddhyā saṃghaṭayya khyāpyate tasmāt tatra api kārya kāraṇa bhāva kṛtaḥ eva pratibandhaḥ tat ayam āśrayaḥ sāmānyasya sva ātmani anupakurvāṇaḥ anapekṣasya ādhāraḥ iti yācitaka maṇḍanam etat katham tarhi idānīm ajanakam kuṇḍam badarāṇām ādhāraḥ pravisarpataḥ śaktiḥ tad deśa jananam kuṇḍa ādeḥ badara ādiṣu 
[070,16]	prakṛtyāḥ eva guruṇaḥ dravyasya asamāna deśa kārya utpādana dharmaṇaḥ samāna deśa kārya utpādana bhāvaḥ ādhāra kṛtaḥ tasmāt tad pūrvakṣaṇa sahakāri kuṇḍam tatra eva badara kāryam janayat ādhāraḥ iti ucyate anyathā iha kuṇḍe badarāṇi iti api na syāt na vai tad upakāra kṛtaḥ ayam vyapadeśaḥ kim tarhi saṃyoga kṛtaḥ kim punar sa tayoḥ eva saṃyogaḥ tābhyām jananāt samavāyāt vā sa kim ekatra eva na samavaiti janyate vā tasya asāmarthyāt tat asamartham pṛthak tat sahitam api tādṛśam eva iti anupakāraka tvāt na saṃyogena tadvat syāt sahitasya tad anya upakārāt viśeṣa utpatteḥ sāmarthyam kaḥ ayam ajanya janaka bhūtānām upakāraḥ svarūpasya siddheḥ akārya tvāt para rūpa kriyāyām api tatra anupakārāt ubhayathā kārakasya akiṃcitkara tvena anupakāraka tvāt iti ukta prāyam tasmāt sarve eva vastu sambandhāḥ janakasya eva upayoga viśeṣa vaśāt pravibhāgena kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt vyavasthāpyante tat ayam kuṇḍa ādīnām api ādhāra bhāvaḥ badara ādiṣu janana śaktiḥ eva
[071,06_071,11^1]	na sambhavati sā api atra na hi ayam janana viśeṣa lakṣaṇaḥ ādhāra bhāvaḥ sāmānye sāmānya āśrayasya sambhavati tasya ajanya tvāt tad abhāve api avasthiteḥ na sthitiḥ atha api syāt sthāpakaḥ āśrayaḥ sāmānyasya tatas sthiti hetu tvāt ādhāraḥ na jananāt iti tat ayuktam tasya tad abhāve api sthānāt patana dharmāṇām hi bhāvānām pāta pratibandhāt ajanakaḥ api sthāpakaḥ bhavet atra api yadi kaścid pratibandham na paryanuyuñjīta sa hi pāta pratibandhaḥ na artha antaram eva yaḥ sthāpayitrā kriyeta artha antara tve tatra eva asya upayogaḥ iti kaḥ patataḥ pratibandhaḥ pratibandhāt apāte api tulyaḥ paryanuyogaḥ anavasthā vā tasmāt pāta abhāvaḥ pāta pratibandhaḥ sa katham kenacid kriyate abhāvam karoti iti hi na abhāvaḥ nāma kaścid kāryaḥ 
[071,11^2_071,30]	tasya kathaṃcid kārya rūpa tve abhāva ayogāt tasmāt bhāva kriyā pratiṣedha nirdeśaḥ eṣa bhāvam na karoti iti yāvat tathā ca ayam na kiṃcid karoti iti akiṃcitkaraḥ ca kaḥ kasya sthāpakaḥ nāma tena ayam kenacid apratibaddhaḥ iti na kadācid tiṣṭhet tasmāt pāta pratibandhaḥ iti api kṣaṇikānām bhāvānām upādānasamāna deśa utpādanam ucyate astu nāma ajananam pātinām tad pratibaddhaḥ tad karaṇāt gatimatas dravyasya kaścid sthāpakaḥ api astu sāmānyasya akriyasya kiṃlakṣaṇām sthitim kurvāṇaḥ sthāpakaḥ syāt sthitiḥ hi tasya svarūpa apracyutiḥ eva sā ca naḥ āśraya āyattā nitya tvāt sā api ayuktāḥ eva bheda abheda vivecane 
[072,01_072,14]	astu nāma āśraya hetukā sthitiḥ sāmānyasya sā sāmānyāt anyā vā syāt ananyā vā sā anyā ced tām eva saḥ āśrayaḥ karoti sā ca apratibaddhā sāmānyaḥ iti kim sāmānyasya āśrayeṇa pratibaddhe vā kaḥ pratibandhaḥ iti vācyam sthiti karaṇam ced tatra api tulyaḥ prasaṅgaḥ anavasthā ca tatas upakārān avadhāraṇāt asya iyam sthitiḥ iti apratītiḥ jananam ced kim āśrayeṇa apekṣitena anupakāriṇā apekṣāḥ iti hi tad pratibandhaḥ sa ca anādheya viśeṣasya sāmānyasya ayuktaḥ iti kevalam janayet iti na asti anyaḥ sthiti hetuḥ abhede vā sthiteḥ sāmānyāt svarūpam eva tat tasya tat ca nityam asti iti na sthitiḥ asya kenacid kriyate tasmāt na sāmānyasya ādhāraḥ asti tat naḥ ādheya tā asya vṛttiḥ atha punar sataḥ api sāmānyasya avyaktasya vyaktyā jñāna kāraṇa tvāt tad vyaktiḥ tatra vṛttiḥ syāt na yuktam evam bhavitum yasmāt vijñāna utpatti yogya tvāya ātmani anya anurodhi yat tat vyaṅgyam yogyatāyāḥ ca kāraṇam kārakam matam prāk eva asya ca yogya tve tad apekṣā na yujyate sāmānyasya avikāryasya tat sāmānyavataḥ kutas 
[072,19^1]	na khalu vai kārakāt vyañjakasya kaścid bhedaḥ sva viṣaya vijñāna utpādana samartham aparam sajātīya upādāna apekṣam anapekṣam vā janayan bhāvam eva vyañjakaḥ ucyate paratra tu jñāna janana śaktiḥ anākṣiptāḥ janyasya iti janana mātreṇa kāraka tvam yaḥ hi yatas vijñāna utpādana yogya tām pratilabhate sa ced na tasya janyaḥ syāt sā asya svabhāva bhūtā yogyatā prāk eva asti iti na vijñāna janane tam apekṣeta para bhūtāyām ca asyām saḥ eva tatas bhavati iti sthiti vat prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt vyañjakaḥ na tam karoti na api anyam iti akiṃcitkaraḥ ca apekṣyate iti vyāhatam etat nanu ajanakāḥ api kāryatvāt dhūma ādayaḥ vyañjakāḥ satyam vyañjakāḥ na tu dhūmam apekṣya agniḥ ātmani jñānam janayati tathābhūtasya agneḥ sākṣāt ajanaka tvāt kevalam upādāna balena eva tatra jñānam utpadyate na viṣaya balena asati api tasmin bhāvāt paraṃparayā liṅga anusāreṇa 
[072,19^2]	na api sāmānya lakṣaṇa avabhāsinām pratyayānām saṃnihita viṣaya tā viṣaya balena utpattiḥ vā iti niveditam etat nivedayiṣyate ca tasmāt ye viṣayāḥ sākṣāt upayogena vijñānam janayantaḥ tatra param apekṣante te avaśyam tatas ātmānam pratilabhante na ca ayam ātma pratilambhaḥ sāmānyasya nityasya kutaścid sambhavati tasmāt na tat kenacid vyaṅgyam na vai yogya tā pratilambham sāmānyasya vyaktim brūmaḥ kim tarhi sva āśraya samavāyam sva āśraya samavetam hi tat ātmani anyatra vā vijñāna hetuḥ iti uktam atra ajanya janakayoḥ kaḥ ayam āśraya āśrayi bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ samavāyaḥ iti sva āśraya samavāya apekṣaḥ vijñāna hetuḥ tena janyaḥ eva syāt tad hetoḥ svabhāvasya prāc abhāvāt paścāt ca tatas bhāvāt nityam tad svabhāva sadbhāve prāk api samavāyāt vijñāna udaya prasaṅgāt na vai vyaktiḥ sāmānyasya saṃskārāt vyañjikā kim tarhi tad grāhiṇaḥ indriyasya saḥ api 
[073,20_073,22^1]	añjana ādeḥ iva vyakteḥ saṃskāraḥ naḥ indriyasya ca pratipatteḥ abhinna tvāt tad bhāva abhāva kālayoḥ saṃskṛtam añjana ādibhiḥ indriyam pratipattau kiṃcid atiśayam āsādayati spaṣṭa aspaṣṭa bhedāt atatkāriṇaḥ ca atad saṃskāraka tvāt na evam vyakteḥ indriyasya kaścid saṃskāraḥ tad bhāva abhāva kālayoḥ pratipattim prati aviśeṣāt viṣaya saṃskāraḥ tu indriya aviśeṣe api tad viśeṣa ādhānāt upakārī syāt na indriya saṃskāraḥ prāk adṛśye darśana śakti ādhānāt upakārakaḥ iti ced saḥ atīndriyam artham darśayan katham na pratipatteḥ bhedakaḥ eka pratiniyame ca sāmānya antarasya darśakaḥ na syāt vyaktyā ca indriya saṃskārāt tad darśane tad vyaṅgyeṣu sāmānyeṣu kadācid aniścayaḥ na syāt eka niścayaḥ vā tasyāḥ avibhāgāyāḥ teṣu viśeṣa abhāvāt 
[073,22^2_074,20]	vyakteḥ yadi indriya saṃskāraḥ yadi naḥ indriya saṃskāraḥ sāmānyasya vijñāna janana svabhāvaḥ iti svabhāvāt apracyuteḥ anapekṣya eva indriya saṃskāram vijñānam janayet saṃskṛta indriya sahakāri tvāt kevalam asamartham iti ced kaḥ ayam anādheya atiśayasya sahakāra arthaḥ anityāḥ hi bhāvāḥ sahakāriṇaḥ viśiṣṭa ātma lābhāt tam apekṣeran yaḥ hi eṣām janakaḥ ātmā sa tadā eva tatas bhavati iti janyatā eva eṣām parasparataḥ apekṣā sāmānyam punar anāsādya param nityam tad svabhāvam kim iti indriyam apekṣate hi tasya kevalasya yaḥ na tad svabhāvaḥ sa punar kathaṃcid bhāvī vyakteḥ indriya saṃskāraḥ tad sahakāri sāmānyam vijñāna hetuḥ iti api pāraṃparyeṇa vyakteḥ kāryam eva sāmānyam uktam syāt api ca vyañjakasya ca jātīnām jāti mattā yadi iṣyate prāptaḥ go tva ādinā tadvān pradīpa ādiḥ prakāśakaḥ 
[074,22]	yaḥ hi yat viṣaya vijñāna hetuḥ sa tasya vyañjakaḥ vijñāna hetu tvam go tva ādiṣu pradīpa ādeḥ api asti tejaḥ saṃskāra apekṣiṇaḥ cakṣuṣaḥ artha pratipatteḥ tatas pradīpa ādayaḥ go tva ādinā tadvantaḥ syuḥ na hi vyakteḥ api jñāna hetu tām muktvā anyā kācid asti abhivyaktiḥ sāmānyasya svabhāva atiśayasya ādhātum aśakya tvāt samavāyaḥ abhivyaktiḥ iti ced uktāḥ uttaram etat tasya samavāya ayogāt iti samavāya mātram hi vyaktyā saha asya jātam na anyaḥ kaścid viśeṣaḥ iti pūrvavat paścāt api na jñāna hetuḥ syāt samavāyāt eva jñāna hetu tve sva āśraya samavāyinām anyeṣām api dṛśyatā āpattiḥ tasmāt jñāna hetu tā eva vyañjaka tvam tat ca tulyam pradīpa ādau iti saḥ eva prasaṅgaḥ tat naḥ ādheya tā na vyaktiḥ vṛttiḥ sāmānyasya iti avṛtteḥ na anekatra jñāna hetuḥ atas eva 
[075,10_075,19]	vyakteḥ anyā athavā ananyā yeṣām jātiḥ tu vidyate teṣām vyaktiṣu apūrvāsu katham sāmānya buddhayaḥ vidyate eva iti avadhāraṇa arthaḥ tuśabdaḥ vidyamānaḥ hi padārthaḥ sva sāmarthyena anyatra buddhim janayan sva rūpa anukāriṇīm tad sambandham apekṣate anyathā atiprasaṅgāt sa ca sāmānyasya sataḥ tattva anyat tva pakṣayoḥ na sambhavati ekatra dṛṣṭasya anyatra darśana asambhavāt sā hi buddhiḥ eka bhāvinī vyakti antaram evam āskandet bhūta grāhiṇī yadi tatra dṛṣṭam kiṃcid anyatra paśyet tat ca sataḥ ananya tve anvaya abhāvāt anya tve api anapāśrayāt 
[075,21^1]	na sambhavati svabhāvaḥ hi svabhāvāt na tattvam anya tvam vā laṅghayati rūpasya atadbhūtasya anya tva avyatikramāt idam eva khalu rūpasya anya tvam yat na tat ākāra antara vat aviśeṣāt tat ced sāmānyasya rūpam ananyat tat eva tat bhavati atattve vastu antara vat anya tva prasaṅgāt na ca eka vyakti ātmanaḥ vyakti antara anvāveśaḥ avyakti antara tva prasaṅgāt tatas na avyatirekiṇaḥ sāmānyāt anvayinī buddhiḥ syāt na api vyatirekiṇaḥ tasya kvacid anāśrayāt anyasya api vyaṅgya vyañjaka bhāva ādeḥ sambandhasya kenacid anupakāryasya apratibandhena abhāvāt asambandhāt ca jñāna utpattau api prasaṅgāt 
[075,21^2]	tat ayam eka vastu darśanena eka vṛtteḥ pratyayasya anyatra vṛttim icchan tattva anyat tve na atikrāmati iti ayuktam etat tasmāt iyam artheṣu eka rūpā pratītiḥ vikalpa vāsanā samutthitā bhrāntiḥ eva bhāva bhedaḥ vāsanā prakṛtiḥ ca tasya āśrayaḥ iti nirloṭhitam etat katham tarhi idānīm pradhāna īśvara ādi kārya śabdāḥ bhāveṣu atadbhūta bhedeṣu abhedena vartante te api yathā saṃketa ahita vāsanā upaskṛta tvāt vijñāna santateḥ sarva artha darśaneṣu anapekṣya api tad bhedam tathā adhyavasāyāt atathābhūta kalpita vyavacchedena vikalpa vijñāna pratibhāsini arthaḥ upādāna bala prabhava vikalpa samutthitāḥ pravartante 
[075,21^3]	na hi teṣu atathābhūteṣu kiṃcid vyatiriktam avyatiriktam vā sāmānyam asti tathā abhāva kalpanayā tu tad anya bhedaḥ pratipattṛ abhiprāya vaśāt syāt tad abhiprāyāt eva sāmānyam kim naḥ iti ced tena avaśyam hi tatra bhedaḥ na antarīyaka tvāt eṣṭavyaḥ saḥ eva sāmānya kārye paryāptaḥ iti niḥ prayojanā sāmānya kalpanā yadi satsu asatsu vā bhāveṣu sāmānya buddhiḥ na iyam arthavatī kevalam viplavaḥ eva iti na asmākam asyāḥ viṣaya nirūpaṇam prati kaścid ādaraḥ kvacid avisaṃvādaḥ asyāḥ vastuni kārya kāraṇa bhāva pratibandhāt na tathābhūta grāhya samāveśāt pratyakṣa vat atatha abhāve api bhāvāt iti nivedayiṣyāmaḥ niveditam ca 
[075,21^4]	bheda viṣaya tvam punar asyāḥ bahulam bhinna padārtha darśana balena teṣu bhāva adhyavasāyāt tathā bhāva kalpanāyām eva aparatra bhāvāt api ca ayam sāmānyam artha antaram kalpayan sva āśraya mātra gatam vā kalpayet sarva gatam vā ākāśa ādi vat tatra yadi sva āśraya mātra gatam ghaṭa tva ādi śūnyeṣu pradeśeṣu ghaṭa ādi utpattau katham teṣu bhinna deśa dravya vartinaḥ sāmānyasya sambhavaḥ yasmāt tat pūrva dravyāt utpitsu dravyam
[077,05_077,15]	na yāti niṣkriya tva upagamāt na hi anya dravya vṛtteḥ bhāvasya tatas avicalataḥ bhinna deśena bhāvena tad ubhaya antarālā vyāpinaḥ yogaḥ yuktaḥ prāk sa na ca tatra āsīt asti paścān na ca tatra utpannaḥ na kutaścid āyātaḥ iti kaḥ imam vyāghāta bhāram udvoḍhum samarthaḥ anyatra jāḍyāt api ca na ca aṃśa vat jahāti pūrvam naḥ ādhāram utpitsu deśāt bhinna deśam tayoḥ ca vartate iti aho vyasana santatiḥ 
[077,16]	bhinna deśayoḥ hi bhāvayoḥ sambandhaḥ dvidhā bhavet nānā avayava ātma tayā anyonyābhyām avayavābhyām tad sambandhāt āloka rajju vaṃśa daṇḍa ādi vat na hi sa avayava tvam antareṇa bhinna deśābhyām yugapad kasyacid yogaḥ yuktaḥ tasya dvitīya ātma abhāvāt eka ātmanaḥ ca tad pradeśa varti sambandhi rūpa tvāt anyathā tad sambandha ayogāt ekasya ādheyasya tatra sthānam tadā eva tatra tena eva ātmanā asthānam iti tad sthita asthita ātmanoḥ ekasya virodhāt ayuktam etat sarvatra sarvadā sarva ākāra sthita ātmā iti ced tad svabhāva darśana āśrayaḥ pratyayaḥ sarvatra sarva ākāraḥ syāt tathā ca gām api aśvaḥ iti pratīyāt aśva sthita ātmanā dravya tvena sambandhāt tad svabhāva pratipattyā ca tathā niścayāt tasya ca ekasya adṛṣṭa ākāra antara abhāvāt tasmāt na anavayavam aneka deśe yugapad ādhīyate pūrva ādhāra tyāge tu bhinna deśe api varteta sa ca na abhimataḥ 
[078,08_078,13]	anyatra vartamānasya tatas anya sthāna janmani svasmāt acalataḥ sthānāt vṛttiḥ iti ati yuktimat yatra asau vartate bhāvaḥ tena sambadhyate api na tad deśinam ca vyāpnoti kim api etat mahā adbhutam iti antaraślokau yasya tu sarva gatam sāmānyam tasya api vyaktāḥ eva ekatra sā vyaktyai abhedāt sarvatragāḥ yadi jātiḥ dṛśyeta sarvatra 
[078,15_078,22]	na jāteḥ nityāyāḥ kācid vyaktiḥ iti niṣiddham etat tasmāt nityam anapekṣita para upaskārā dṛśyeta vā na vā kadācid tasmin svabhāve vyavasthānāt svabhāva antarasya kutaścid anutpatteḥ abhyupagamya api vyaktim vyāpini ekatra vyaktyai bheda abhāvāt vyaktāḥ eva sarvatra iti vyakti śūnyeṣu api pradeśeṣu dṛśyeta na ca sā vyakti apekṣiṇī yadi hi vyakti apekṣiṇī syāt vyañjaka apratipattau hi na vyaṅgyam sampratīyate viparyayaḥ punar kasmāt iṣṭaḥ sāmānya tadvatoḥ 
[078,24]	yaḥ api hi sva āśraya indriya saṃyoga apekṣa pratipattikam sāmānyam āśraya śūnyeṣu pradeśeṣu na dṛśyate iti pratisamādadhīta tasya api asti eva āśraya indriya saṃyogaḥ upakārakaḥ iti tatas tad darśī yathā sthitām paśyet na hi tasyām dṛśyamānāyām adṛṣṭam tadīyam yuktam vyakti vyaṅgya tvāt sāmānyasya vyañjaka rahiteṣu pradeśeṣu adarśanam iti api mithyā tathābhūtasya vyaṅgya vyañjaka bhāvasya tatra abhāvāt sva pratipattyā apara pratipatti hetuḥ hi vyañjakaḥ pradīpa ādiḥ svarūpa śūnye deśe su a vyaṅgyam na darśayat na evam vyaktiḥ viparyayāt katham hi sā vyañjikā ca syāt sāmānyasya tad pratipatti dvāreṇa ca dṛśyā syāt vyaṅgyā ca sā eva prasajyate pradīpa ghaṭa vat kathaṃcid tad pratipattim antareṇa adṛśya rūpa tvāt api ca anena kim asambhavat abhisamīkṣya evam bahu āyāsaḥ sāmānya vādaḥ āśritaḥ para sparataḥ bhedāt vyatirekiṇīṣu vyaktiṣu anvayinaḥ pratyayasya ayogāt katham idānīm
[079,12_079,13]	pācaka ādiṣu abhinnena vinā api arthena vācakaḥ pācaka pāṭhaka ādiṣu anyonyam ananvayiṣu api śabda pratyaya anuvṛttiḥ asti pācakaḥ pāṭhakaḥ iti na hi teṣu anyat ekam abhinnam asti yena bhinnāḥ tathā pratīyeran karma asti ced vyaktibhyaḥ eva tarhi sa pratyayaḥ astu kim idānīm karmaṇā anyena vā bhinnam abhinna pratyaya hetuḥ na bhavati iti ekam sāmānyam iṣṭam tat yadi bhinnam api karma abhinnam pratyayam janayet vyaktibhiḥ kaḥ aparādhaḥ kṛtaḥ yena tāḥ tathā naḥ iṣyante tāsām eka rūpa tvāt asya idam iti vyatireka pratītiḥ atadākāra viśeṣavatī ca na syāt iti ced uktam atra yathā vyatirekaḥ viśeṣa pratyayāḥ ca yathāsvam artha antara vivekāt iti tasmāt vyakti vat 
[079,23_080,01]	bhedāt na hetuḥ karma asya pācaka ādi abheda pratyayasya tat karma jātiḥ abhedāt hetuḥ iti ced na jātiḥ karma saṃśrayāt na hi artha antara sambandhinī jātiḥ artha antare pratyaya hetuḥ go tvam iva karka ādiṣu pācaka karmasu ca karma jātiḥ na ca tāni karmāṇi pācaka śabdena abhidhīyante kim tarhi tad karma āśrayaḥ dravyam tasya karma sāmānyasya
[080,05_080,09]	śruti antara nimitta tvāt ca pākaḥ pākaḥ iti hi tatas syāt na punar pācakaḥ iti tasya karma nimitta tve proktam kim ca sthiti abhāvāt ca karmaṇaḥ na hi anityam karma sarvadā asti tasya ca pratyayasya karma nimitta tve niruddhe karmaṇi na pācakaḥ iti ucyeta pacataḥ eva karma sadbhāvāt tatas eva
[080,12_080,20]	asambandhāt na sāmānyam na ayuktam śabda kāraṇam atiprasaṅgāt vinaṣṭe hi karmaṇi tat sāmānyam na karmaṇi na kartari iti sambaddha sambandhe api asya na asti iti asambandhāt na śabda jñāna hetuḥ anyathā hi atiprasaṅgaḥ syāt atītam anāgatam vā nimittīkṛtya tayoḥ pravṛttiḥ iti ced karma api na asat jñāna abhidhānayoḥ nimittam tayoḥ anaimittika tā āpatteḥ 
[080,21_081,06]	asat hi nirupākhyam katham nimittam syāt kārya karaṇa lakṣaṇa tvāt vastu tvasya tat pracyutā samprāpta rūpam atīta anāgatam karma nimittam anyat ca vyakti ādikam naḥ iṣṭam iti animitte te syātām tathā ca na jāti siddhiḥ tasyāḥ jñāna abhidhānayoḥ nimitta tve naḥ iṣṭa tvāt śaktiḥ pācaka ādi śabda nimittam na karma na sāmānyam iti ced na ca śaktiḥ ananvayāt 
[081,07]	na hi śaktiḥ nāma kiṃcid anyat eva pācaka ādīnām tasyāḥ eva pācaka ādi artha kriyā upayogena dravyasya anupayogi tva prasaṅgāt tasyām tasya upayogaḥ iti ced kim idānīm śaktyā śakti upayogāya śakti antarasya vyatirekiṇaḥ abhyupagame ati prasaṅgāt dravyam eva upayujyate iti vācyam tasya upayoge śaktau artha kriyāyām eva upayujyate iti kim naḥ iṣyate iti kim antarāle anarthikayā śaktyā tasmāt śaktiḥ iti dravyam eva tat kāryam tat ca na anveti iti tatas anvayī śabdaḥ na syāt 
[081,15_081,24]	sāmānyam pācaka tva ādi yadi prāk eva tat bhavet vyaktam sattā ādi vat no ced na paścāt aviśeṣatas atha api pācaka tvam iti sāmānyam eva kiṃcid bhavet sati arthe tad samavāyasya akādācitka tvāt sattā ādi vat prāk eva vyaktam syāt yāvanti hi sāmānyāni arthe samavāya dharmāṇi tāni saha utpādena asya samavayanti iti samayaḥ tad vyatikrame tasya paścāt api aviśeṣāt na tad samavāyaḥ syāt tad sambandhi svabhāva vaiguṇyāt hi sa tasya prāk naḥ āsīt tatra eva ca asya svabhāve sthitasya paścāt bhavati iti duranvayam etat kriyā upakāra apekṣasya vyañjaka tve avikāriṇaḥ na apekṣā atiśaye api asya kṣaṇika tvāt kriyā kutas 
[081,26^1]	karma upakāram apekṣya pācaka tvam dravyeṇa vyajyate iti ced sthira svabhāvasya anatiśayāt aviśeṣa ādhāyini kā apekṣā atiśaye vā kṣaṇika tvāt karmaṇaḥ pratikṣaṇam svabhāva bhūtasya anyāni asya atiśayasya utpatteḥ tat api kṣaṇikam syāt tatas sva utpatti sthāna vināśinaḥ kriyā kutas yat apekṣam vyañjakam syāt katham tarhi idānīm asti abhinne vastuni jñāna śabdayoḥ anvayinoḥ vṛttiḥ yathā pācaka ādiṣu nanu tat eva idam cintyate katham teṣu api iti cintitam etat yathā na teṣu sambhavati tat kim idānīm animitte te syātām na animitte kim tarhi na bāhya tattva nimitte yathāsvam vāsanā prabodhāt vikalpa utpattiḥ tatas śabdāḥ na punar vikalpa abhidhānayoḥ vastu sattā samāśrayaḥ iti ukta prāyam etat 
[081,26^2]	yathāsvam samaya vāsanā vaśāt virodhi rūpa samāveśena apara apara darśane api anvayinoḥ tayoḥ darśanāt na ca tatra tad nibandhanaḥ kaścid svabhāvaḥ asti paraspara virodhinoḥ yugapad ekatra samāveśa ayogāt aniyamena tarhi syāt na hi animittam bhavat kvacid bhavati kvacid na bhavati iti niyamam arhati na khalu vai tat animittam vāsanā viśeṣa nimitta tvāt bāhyam tu tathābhūtam dṛśyam na asti iti brūmaḥ na ca asati tasmin na bhavitavyam supta taimirika upalabdheṣu artheṣu abhāveṣu samaya vāsana āropita rūpa viśeṣeṣu ca tathā vikalpa utpatteḥ na ca te asatsu utpadyante iti sarvatra sarva ākāraḥ vibhāge naḥ eva tathā upalabdhānām vikalpanāt uktam ca atra kiṃcid asmābhiḥ prakṛtyāḥ api kecid eka jñāna kāryāḥ svabhāva bhedāt iti api ca 
[082,23_082,28]	tulye bhede yayā jātiḥ pratyāsattyā prasarpati kvacid na anyatra saḥ eva astu śabda jñāna nibandhanam iti antaraślokaḥ na nivṛttim vihāya asti yadi bhāva anvayaḥ aparaḥ ekasya kāryam anyasya na syāt atyanta bhedataḥ yadi ete bhāvāḥ vyāvṛttim muktvā svabhāvena kenacid anvayinā śūnyāḥ na eṣām bahūnām ekam kāryam syāt yaḥ hi tasya svabhāvaḥ janakaḥ na hi saḥ anyasya asti yaḥ asti sa na janakaḥ vyatirekaḥ yaḥ niḥsvabhāva tvāt yat janakam tat eva vastu tad janakam ca aparatra na asti iti na aparam janayet sa hi tasya svabhāvaḥ yaḥ janakaḥ saḥ anyasya api yadi syāt sa tena svabhāvena tatas abhinnaḥ syāt iti asti svabhāva anvayaḥ 
[083,07_083,12]	yadi eka ātma tayā anekaḥ kāryasya ekasya kārakaḥ ātmā ekatra api saḥ asti iti vyarthāḥ syuḥ sahakāriṇaḥ yadi eka svabhāva tvāt anekaḥ ekasya kārakaḥ sa teṣām abhinnaḥ svabhāvaḥ eka saṃnidhāne api asti iti avaikalyāt kāraṇasya ekaḥ api janakaḥ syāt yasmāt na apaiti abhinnam tad rūpam viśeṣāḥ khalu apāyinaḥ 
[083,13_083,19]	na hi tasya abhinna svabhāvasya artha antare viśeṣaḥ asti viśeṣaḥ abheda hāneḥ sa ca tatra api asti iti naḥ eka sthitau api tasya apāyaḥ asti ye viśeṣāḥ teṣām saha sthiti niyama abhāvāt syāt apāyaḥ na ca te janakāḥ iṣṭāḥ sahakāriṇām eka svabhāva tayā janakatvā abhyupagamāt tatas janakasya sthānāt asthāyinaḥ ca ajanaka tvāt eka sthitau api kārya utpattiḥ syāt na ca bhavati atas eka apāye phala abhāvāt viśeṣebhyaḥ tad udbhavaḥ 
[083,20]	tad kāryam aneka sahakāri sādhāraṇam eka viśeṣa apāye api na bhavati punar api avikaleṣu sarveṣu viśeṣeṣu bhavati na tu avikale api abhinne rūpe kāryam hi kutaścid bhāva dharmi yat na bhavati tat tasya eva vaikalyāt na ca abhinnasya rūpasya eka sthitau api vaikalyam asti avikale api tasmin abhavat tasya ajanaka ātma tām sūcayati yat sākalya vaikalyābhyām ca kāryam bhāva abhāva vat tatas eva utpattiḥ tasmin sati niyamena bhavataḥ tad anyasmāt utpatti kalpanāyām atiprasaṅgāt tasmāt viśeṣāḥ eva janakāḥ na sāmānyam tatas te eva vastu yasmāt 
[084,04_084,14]	sa pāramārthikaḥ bhāvaḥ yaḥ eva artha kriyā kṣamaḥ idam eva hi vastu avastunoḥ lakṣaṇam yat artha kriyā yogya tā ayogya tā ca iti vakṣyāmaḥ sa ca artha kriyā yogyaḥ arthaḥ na anveti yaḥ anveti na tasmāt kārya sambhavaḥ tasmāt sarvam sāmānyam anartha kriyā yogya tvāt avastu vastu tu viśeṣaḥ eva tatas eva tat niṣpatteḥ svabhāvān anvayāt tarhi ekasya janakam rūpam anyasya na asti iti ajanakaḥ syāt janaka tve vā bheda aviśeṣāt sarvaḥ janakaḥ syāt na etat asti yasmāt tena ātmanā hi bhede api hetuḥ kaścid na ca aparaḥ svabhāvaḥ ayam 
[084,16]	ekasya janakāt ātmanaḥ bhidyamānāḥ sarve samam janakāḥ na vā aviśeṣe kaścid iti syāt etat yadi eṣām na viśeṣaḥ sambhavet tatas bheda api kutaścid ātmā atiśayāt kaścid janakaḥ na aparaḥ sa hi tasya svabhāvaḥ na aparasya na hi svabhāvāḥ bhāvānām paryanuyogam arhanti kim agniḥ dahati uṣṇaḥ vā naḥ udakam iti etāvat tu syāt kutas ayam svabhāvaḥ iti nirhetuka tve anapekṣiṇaḥ niyama abhāvena atiprasaṅgāt tasmāt svabhāvaḥ asya sva hetoḥ iti ucyate tasya api tad janana ātma tā tad anyasmāt iti anādiḥ hetu paraṃparāḥ bhinnānām hi kaścid hetuḥ na anyaḥ svabhāvāt iti atra na kiṃcid bādhakam 
[085,03_085,08]	 abhede tu syātām nāśa udbhavau sakṛt abhedāt svabhāvena eva viśvasya sva ātma vat vibhāga utpatti sthiti nirodha ādayaḥ na syuḥ tathā upalakṣaṇāt abhedasya idam eva hi bheda abheda lakṣaṇam eka ākārasya api vyatirekaḥ avyatirekaḥ ca virodhinoḥ eka ātmani asambhavāt bhedaḥ api tena naḥ evam ced 
[085,09_085,13]	na vai sarva ākāra avyatirekam brūmaḥ yena evam syāt kaścid asya ātmā bhinnaḥ na anyaḥ iti bhedāt na saha utpatti ādayaḥ evam tarhi yaḥ ekasmin vinaśyati tiṣṭhati ātmā na tasya bhedaḥ sthāna āsthānayoḥ eka ātma āśraya tve kaḥ anyaḥ dharmaḥ bhedakaḥ iti nānātvam eva kvacid na syāt sarva ākāra viveka avivekinoḥ vā arthayoḥ abhyupagamāt nāma kevalam naḥ iṣṭam syāt na vastu iti uktam tat ime na eka yogakṣemāḥ bhāvāḥ bhinnāḥ eva
[085,17_085,22]	 atas na syāt sāmānya bheda dhīḥ tat idam artha antaram anāyattam ajanya tvāt asya idam sāmānyam bhedaḥ vā iti vyapadeśam na arhati anya apohe api eṣa tulyaḥ prasaṅgaḥ iti ced na tulyaḥ yatas nivṛtteḥ niḥsvabhāva tvāt na sthāna āsthāna kalpanā na hi anyāpohaḥ nāma kiṃcid tasya ca svabhāva anuṣaṅgiṇyaḥ svabhāva sthiti pracyuti kalpanāḥ na kalpante 
[085,24_086,04]	upaplavaḥ ca sāmānya dhiyaḥ tena api adūṣaṇā nirviṣayam eva khalu idam mithyājñānam yat anekatra eka ākāram iti na tad viṣayasya abhāvāt sthitiḥ asthitiḥ vā yat punar etat uktam tad janakaḥ hi sa tasya svabhāvaḥ yat tasya janakam rūpam tatas anyaḥ janakaḥ katham tatra na brūmaḥ anyasya tad janakam rūpam na asti iti kim tarhi yat ekasya tad janakam tat anyasya naḥ iti anyaḥ api sva rūpeṇa eva janakaḥ na para rūpeṇa atattvāt te yathāsvam bhinnāḥ ca tad janakāḥ ca svabhāvena iti kaḥ atra virodhaḥ eka rūpa vikalaḥ tad rūpaḥ na syāt na atad kāryaḥ tena eva ca tat kāryam kartavyam iti kaḥ atra nyāyaḥ api ca 
[086,10_086,20]	bhinnā viśeṣā janakā iti uktam na ca te viśeṣāḥ tena ātmanā parasparam anuyanti yat ekasya janakam rūpam anyasya tat na asti na ca tāvatā ajanakāḥ api abhedaḥ api teṣu ced syāt etat satyam viśeṣāḥ janakāḥ na punar teṣām viśiṣṭam eva rūpam kim tu abhinnam api tad eka śakti yogāt janakāḥ tena te ajanakāḥ proktāḥ sati api sāmānye rūpe na tena te janakāḥ tasya anapāyāt eka sthitau api kārya utpatti prasaṅgāt iti uktam prāk kim ca pratibhāsaḥ api bhedakaḥ ananya bhāj 
[086,22]	utpatti sthiti vināśa ādi bhedaḥ naḥ iti api śabdāt yaḥ ayam abhinnān sarva arthāt manyate tasya ayam artheṣu buddhi pratibhāsa bhedaḥ viruddha dharma adhyāsaḥ ca na syāt sati vā tasmin abhede api na kaścid bhedaḥ syāt tathā ca ayam pravibhāgaḥ na syāt eka ātma vat tasmāt ayam bhinna pratibhāsa ādiḥ viśeṣaḥ eva na ca atra aparam abhinnam pratibhāsam paśyāmaḥ yat balena abheda pratītiḥ syāt atas viśeṣaḥ eva 
[087,01_087,04]	 saḥ eva arthaḥ tasya vyāvṛttayaḥ apare tat kāryam kāraṇam ca uktam tat sva lakṣaṇam iṣyate tad tyāga āpti phalāḥ sarvāḥ puruṣāṇām pravṛttayaḥ yat artha kriyā kāri tat eva vastu iti uktam sa ca viśeṣaḥ eva yat punar etat sāmānyam nāma tat tasya eva aparasmāt bhedaḥ na hi tasya artha tve dṛśyasya rūpa anupalakṣaṇam yuktam tad upalakṣaṇa kṛta tvāt bhedeṣu abhinna pratyayasya api ca 
[087,08_087,10]	yathā abheda aviśeṣe api na sarvam sarva sādhanam tathā bheda aviśeṣe api na sarvam sarva sādhanam yat uktam katham tad janaka svabhāvāt bhinnaḥ asya janakaḥ syāt janaka tve vā aviśeṣāt sarvaḥ janakaḥ syāt iti uktam atra yadi aviśeṣaḥ syāt syāt etat iti yathā ca asya svayam abheda vādinaḥ abheda aviśeṣe api na sarvaḥ sarvasya janakaḥ iti tathā bheda aviśeṣe api bhaviṣyati athavā 
[087,15_087,17]	bhede hi kārakam kiṃcid vastu dharma tayā bhavet abhede tu virudhyete tasya ekasya kriyā kriye bheda mātrā viśeṣe api sva hetu pratyaya niyamita svabhāva tvāt kecid eva kārakāḥ syuḥ na anye atad svabhāva tvāt iti atra naḥ eva kiṃcid viruddham asti ekatve tu tasya tatra eva tathā kāraka tvam akāraka tvam ca iti vyāhatam etat 
[087,21_087,26]	bhedaḥ api asti akriyātaḥ ced na kuryuḥ sahakāriṇaḥ na vai sarva ākāra avivekam brūmaḥ bhedasya api bhāvāt tasmāt kaścid akārakaḥ api iti tathā api kathaṃcid bhedāt sahakāriṇaḥ akārakāḥ syuḥ paryāyeṇa atha kartṛ tvam sa kim tasya eva vastunaḥ atha api syāt naḥ eva kaścid akārakaḥ asti sarveṣām sarvatra paryāyeṇa upayogāt śakteḥ vā vipariṇatāyāḥ tad niveśinyā rūpa antareṇa upayogāt saḥ eva khalu ayam paryāyaḥ bheda āśrayaḥ ekasya katham pariṇāmaḥ vai avyatirekiṇyāḥ viśeṣe vā kathaṃcid eka tva hāniḥ iti yat kiṃcid etat kim ca 
[088,03_088,05]	atyanta bheda abhedau ca syātām tadvati vastuni anyonyam vā tayoḥ bhedaḥ sadṛśā sadṛśa ātmanoḥ bhāvāḥ ced abhinnena ātmanā sva ātma bhūtena bhedinaḥ tadvantaḥ syuḥ tad abhinna svabhāva ātma tvāt bhedasya api kutas parasparam bhedaḥ atha na sa tasya samānaḥ ātmā tathā sati tad ātmanā tena api na yuktam tathā bhavitum tathā abhāve hi ataddharmā syāt na hi ayam pravṛtti nivṛttimān svabhāvaḥ ekaḥ yuktaḥ na sarva ātmanā abhedaḥ eva 
[088,11_088,17]	tayoḥ api bhavet bhedaḥ yadi na hi kvacid asya ekāntikaḥ bhedaḥ abhedaḥ vā vivekena vyavasthāpanāt sāmānyam viśeṣaḥ iti yena ātmanā tayoḥ bhedaḥ sāmānyam iti etat yadi bhedaḥ tad ātmanā bhedaḥ eva yadi sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ yam ātmānam āśritya sāmānyam viśeṣaḥ iti sthitiḥ tena ātmanā bhedaḥ tadā bhedaḥ eva yasmāt tau hi tayoḥ sva ātmānau tau ced vyatirekiṇau vyatirekaḥ eva sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ svabhāva bhedāt svabhāvaḥ hi bhāvaḥ iti 
[088,21_088,26]	 tathā ca syāt niḥsāmānya viśeṣa tā bheda sāmānyayoḥ yadvat ghaṭa ādīnām parasparam vyatireke ca bheda sāmānyayoḥ na bhedaḥ sāmānyāt na sāmānyam bheda vat sambandha abhāvāt parasparam ghaṭa ādi vat iti uktam api ca yam ātmānam puraskṛtya puruṣaḥ ayam pravartate tad sādhya phala vān chāvān bheda abhedau tad āśrayau cintyete sva ātmanā bhedaḥ vyāvṛttyā ca samāna tā asti eva vastu na anveti pravṛtti ādi prasaṅgataḥ 
[089,02^1]	sarve eva gauḥ aśvāt bhinnaḥ abhinnaḥ vā iti bhedam abhedam vā pṛcchan viśeṣam eva bhāvasya svabhāva ākhyam adhikṛtya pravartate saḥ eva hi tathā ucyate dravya tva ādayaḥ tu na tatra śabda coditāḥ yathāsvam pṛthak abhidhānāt arthasya tat avyabhicārāt tatas gatiḥ syāt nirloṭhitam ca etat ācāryeṇa tat ayam gavā ādi śabda pratyupasthāpitam artham bhinnam abhinnam vā pṛcchan artha antara upakṣepeṇa tatra kim iti dvi mukha buddhiḥ kriyate tasmāt yaḥ asya ātmā ananya sādhāraṇaḥ yam puraskṛtya puruṣaḥ viśiṣṭa artha kriyā arthī pravartate yathā goḥ vāha doha ādau na anya sambhavinaḥ arthasya yathā yuddha praveśe saḥ eva svabhāvaḥ yathāsvam śabda coditaḥ na dravya tva ādi sāmānyam 
[089,02^2]	tat codanayā tadā prāptum anabhipreta tvāt gavā ādi samāveśāt tat ātma bhūtānām ca ananvayena tatra anubhaya rūpa tvāt tam eva ca ayam bhāvam prakāraiḥ paryanuyuṅkte tasya bhede dravya tva ādi abhedaḥ asya abādhakaḥ eva sarvatra svabhāvena bhedasya abhyupagamāt sāmānyasya ca vyāvṛtti lakṣaṇasya svabhāva bhūtasya ca sāmānyasya abhede api uktam sva ātmanā eva abhede tu tad svabhāva nibandhana artha kriyā arthī samam dvayoḥ api pravarteta ekaḥ api tām artha kriyām tad svabhāva tvāt eva karoti tad anyasya api tat tulyam iti saḥ api kim na karoti 
[089,22_089,27]	etena eva yat ahrīkāḥ kim api aślīlam ākulam pralapanti pratikṣiptam tat api ekānta sambhavāt yat ayam ahrīkaḥ syāt uṣṭraḥ dadhi syāt naḥ iti kim api aślīlam ayuktam aheya upādeyam apariniṣṭhānāt ākulam pralapanti tat api anena nirastam svabhāvena ekānta bhedāt tad anvaye vā sarvasya ubhaya rūpa tve tad viśeṣa nirākṛteḥ coditaḥ dadhi khāda iti kim uṣṭram na abhidhāvati 
[090,01_090,06]	tathā hi uṣṭraḥ api syāt dadhi na api saḥ eva uṣṭraḥ ye na anyaḥ api syāt uṣṭraḥ tathā dadhi api syāt uṣṭraḥ na api tat eva dadhi yena anyat api syāt dadhi tat anayoḥ ekasya api kasyacid tad rūpa abhāvasya abhāvāt svarūpasya vā atadbhāvinaḥ sva niyatasya abhāvāt na kaścid viśeṣaḥ iti dadhi khāda iti coditaḥ uṣṭram api khādet atha asti atiśayaḥ kaścid yena bhedena vartate saḥ eva dadhi saḥ anyatra na asti iti anubhayam param 
[090,08_090,14]	atha anayoḥ kaścid atiśayaḥ asti yena ayam tathā coditaḥ kṣīra vikāraḥ eva pravartate na anyatra saḥ eva atiśayaḥ artha kriyā arthi pravṛtti viṣayaḥ dadhi tad phala upādāna bhāva lakṣita svabhāvam hi vastu dadhi iti sa ca tādṛśaḥ svabhāvaḥ anyatra na asti iti pravṛtti abhāvāt arthinaḥ tasmāt tat naḥ ubhaya rūpam iti ekānta vādaḥ api ca sarva ātma tve ca sarveṣām bhinnau syātām na dhīdhvanī bheda saṃhāra vādasya tad abhāvāt asambhavaḥ 
[090,16^1]	saḥ ayam ahrīkaḥ kvacid api ekam ākāram pratiniyatam apaśyan vibhāga abhāvāt bhāvānām katham asaṃsṛṣṭāni ākāravatyā buddhyā adhimucyeta arthān abhilapet vā tatas bheda agrahāt tad saṃhāra vādaḥ na syāt syāt uṣṭraḥ dadhi syāt naḥ iti atha punar asaṃsṛṣṭau ākārau pratipadya saṃharet eka rūpa saṃsargiṇyāḥ buddheḥ kvacid pratiniyamāt tad pratibhāsa bheda kṛtaḥ eva tayoḥ rūpayoḥ svabhāva bhedaḥ api syāt eka aneka vyavasthiteḥ pratibhāsa viṣaya tvāt tathā ca naḥ ekaḥ tad ubhaya rūpaḥ syāt iti mithyāvādaḥ eṣaḥ sthitam etat na bhāvānām kaścid svabhāva anvayaḥ asti bheda lakṣaṇam eva tu sāmānyam atha ca prakṛtyā kecid eka jñāna ādi phalāḥ kecid naḥ iti 
[090,16^2]	bhavatu nāma bhāvānām svabhāva bhedaḥ sāmānyam yeṣām tu nirupākhyānām svabhāvaḥ eva na asti tatra katham svabhāva bheda viṣayāḥ śabdāḥ teṣu avaśyam śabda pravṛttyā bhāvyam kathaṃcid avyavasthāpiteṣu vidhi pratiṣedha ayogāt tathā ca sarvatra ayam anvaya vyatireka āśrayaḥ vyavahāraḥ na syāt uṣṇa svabhāvaḥ agniḥ na anuṣṇaḥ iti api svabhāva antarasya asataḥ kathaṃcid avyavasthāpanāt sarvathā apratipatteḥ agni svabhāvasya apratipattiḥ iti vyāmūḍham jagat syāt syāt etat na tatra kasyacid asataḥ niṣedhaḥ anuṣṇam sat eva artha antaram niṣidhyate iti katham idānīm sat asat nāma 
[090,16^3]	na brūmaḥ sarvatra asat tatra na asti iti deśa kāla dharma niṣedhaḥ eva sarva bhāveṣu kriyate na dharmiṇaḥ tad niṣedhe tad viṣaya śabda pravṛtti abhāvāt anirdiṣṭa viṣayasya nañaḥ aprayogāt saḥ api tarhi deśa ādi pratiṣedhaḥ katham yasmāt na tatra api deśa ādīnām pratiṣedhaḥ na api arthasya sambandhaḥ niṣedhyate iti ced nanu tad niṣedhe api tulyaḥ doṣaḥ niṣedhāt asati śabda apravṛttiḥ iti ādi asataḥ vai asya niṣedhe tadvat dharmiṇaḥ api niṣedhaḥ na vai sambandhasya na asti iti niṣedhaḥ kim tarhi na iha ghaṭaḥ naḥ idānīm na evam iti uktau na anena sambandhaḥ asti naḥ etat dharmāḥ vā iti pratītiḥ tathā ca sambandhaḥ niṣiddhaḥ bhavati iti 
[090,16^4]	tathā api katham niṣiddhaḥ yāvat asya sambandhaḥ dharmaḥ vā na asti iti matiḥ na bhavati na ca asyāḥ kathaṃcid bhāve sambhavaḥ abhāveṣu tathā abhāvāt tasmāt sambandha abhāva pratīteḥ na ayam iha iti ādyā pratītiḥ sa tad abhāve na syāt pratītau vā tad abhāvasya yathā pratītimataḥ tad prabhavāḥ śabdāḥ kena nivāryante saḥ eva hi śabdānām na viṣayaḥ yaḥ na vitarkāṇām te ced pravṛttāḥ kaḥ vacanasya niṣeddhā na hi avācyam artham buddhayaḥ samīhante sambandhasya tu svarūpeṇa anabhidhānam uktam abhidhāne sambandhi tvena buddhau upasthānāt yathā abhiprāyam apratītiḥ tat ayam pratīyamānaḥ api sambandhi rūpaḥ eva iti svarūpeṇa na abhidhīyate tasmāt na abhāva vat sambandhe api prasaṅgaḥ 
[092,08_092,16]	api ca ayam abhāvam abhidheyam bruvāṇam prati pratividadhat abruvāṇaḥ katham pratividadhyāt vacane vai asya katham abhāvaḥ anuktaḥ atha abhāvam eva na icchet tena avacanam tat eva idānīm katham abhāvaḥ na asti iti yat punar etat artha niṣedhe anarthaka śabda aprayogāt nirviṣayasya nañaḥ aprayogaḥ iti atra uttaram vakṣyate tasmāt santi abhāveṣu śabdāḥ teṣu katham svabhāva bhedaḥ iti tatra api rūpa abhāvāt abhāvasya śabdāḥ rūpa abhidhāyinaḥ na āśaṅkyāḥ eva siddhāḥ te vyavacchedasya vācakāḥ 
[092,18]	vastu vṛttīnām śabdānām kim rūpam abhidheyam āhosvit bhedaḥ iti śaṅkā syāt abhāvaḥ tu viveka lakṣaṇaḥ eva nimittīkartavyasya kasyacid rūpasya abhāvāt tad bhāve abhāva ayogāt tad bhāva lakṣaṇa tvāt bhāvasya tasmāt ayam eva sa mukhyaḥ vivekaḥ tasya tathā abhāva khyāpinaḥ śabdāḥ kim viveka viṣayāḥ iti asthānam eva etat āśaṅkāyāḥ tasmāt siddham etat sarve śabdāḥ viveka viṣayāḥ vikalpāḥ ca te ete eka vastu pratiśaraṇāḥ api yathāsvam avadhi bheda upakalpitaiḥ bhedaiḥ bhinneṣu iva pratibhātsu buddhau vivekeṣu upalayanāt bhinna viṣayāḥ eva tena svabhāvasya eva sādhya sādhana bhāve api na sādhya sādhana saṃsargaḥ tau na pratijñā artha eka deśaḥ hetuḥ iti sa ca ayam hetu tvena apadiśyamānaḥ 
[093,06_093,08]	upādhi bheda apekṣaḥ vā svabhāvaḥ kevalaḥ athavā ucyate sādhya siddhi artham nāśe kāryatva sattva vat apekṣita para vyāpāraḥ hi svabhāva niṣpattau bhāvaḥ kṛtakaḥ tena iyam kṛtaka śrutiḥ svabhāva abhidhāyinī api para upādhim enam ākṣipati etena pratyaya bheda bhedi tva ādayaḥ vyākhyātāḥ evam upādhi bheda apekṣaḥ kvacid svabhāvaḥ hetuḥ ucyate kvacid anapekṣaḥ sāmānyena yathā anitya tvaḥ eva sattvam kvacid svabhāva bhūta dharma viśeṣa parigraheṇa yathā tatra eva utpattiḥ anayā diśāḥ anye api svabhāva hetu pravibhāgāḥ draṣṭavyāḥ 
[093,15_093,17]	sattā svabhāvaḥ hetuḥ ced na sattā sādhyate katham ananvayaḥ hi bhedānām vyāhataḥ hetu sādhyayoḥ yadi sattvam anitya tve anyatra vā hetuḥ syāt sādhyam api kasmāt naḥ iṣyate tat kila evam prasādhyamānam viśeṣībhavati na ca viśeṣaḥ sādhāyitum śakyate ananvayāt yathā āha pramāṇa viśeṣayā ajñānāt iti saḥ ayam viśeṣaḥ na sādhyaḥ eva vyāhanyate kim tarhi hetau api tulya doṣa tvāt na hi hetuḥ ananvayaḥ siddheḥ aṅgam tatas saṃśayāt na eṣa doṣaḥ yasmāt 
[094,01_094,09]	bhāva upādāna mātre tu sādhye sāmānya dharmiṇi na kaścid arthaḥ siddhaḥ syāt aniṣiddham ca tādṛśam na sarvathā sattā sādhane viśeṣaḥ sādhitaḥ bhavati bhāva mātra viśeṣaṇaḥ asti kaścid dharmī iti prasādhayataḥ anirdiṣṭa svabhāva viśeṣasya kasyacid sattā mātre virodha abhāvāt na iha sattā sādhana pratiṣedhaḥ kim tu sa tathā asti kaścid iti kaṃcana asya bhedam aparāmṛśan bruvāṇaḥ kam sva artham puṣṇāti tasmāt anena upātta bhedaḥ eva sādhyaḥ upātta bhede sādhye asmin bhavat hetuḥ ananvayaḥ sattāyām tena sādhyāyām viśeṣaḥ sādhitaḥ bhavet 
[094,11^1]	sa hi dharmī pradhāna lakṣaṇaḥ ekaḥ nityaḥ sukha ādi ātmakaḥ anyaḥ vā iti yathā kathaṃcid api viśeṣitaḥ tad svabhāvaḥ prasādhitaḥ bhavati sa ca tathā na anveti yat api sattā mātram anveti na tena siddhena kiṃcid nanu evam agni ādiṣu api prasaṅgaḥ tatra api na agni sattā mātre kaścid vivādaḥ viśiṣṭa ādhāra viśeṣasya tu abhimatasya ananvayāt asiddhiḥ na vai saḥ ādhāraḥ tam viśeṣīkaroti tad ayoga vyavacchedena viśeṣaṇāt iti uktam vakṣyate ca tasmāt tatra sāmānyam eva sādhyate tad ayoga vyavacchedena na tathā iha api kvacid sattāyāḥ sādhanam pradhāna ādi śabda vācyasya eva arthasya kvacid abhāvāt nirviśeṣaṇā eva sā katham abhāvaḥ jñeya abhidheya prameya tvaiḥ saḥ api siddhaḥ eva tat kim idānīm jñeyam asti iti siddhiḥ astu tathā api kim siddham syāt anyatra tu tat eva agni sāmānyam tatra asiddham iti sādhyate 
[094,11^2]	nanu tatra api tad ayoga virahiṇā sāmānyena anvayaḥ na siddhaḥ eva na vai kaścid tathā abhūtena anvayam karoti pratipādayatā hi param dhūmaḥ agninā antarīyakaḥ darśanīyaḥ yatra dhūmaḥ tatra agniḥ iti sa tathā agni mātreṇa vyāptaḥ siddhaḥ yatra eva svayam dṛśyate tatra eva agni buddhim janayati tatra ca sādhya nirdeśena na kiṃcid tatra darśana sambandha ākhyāna mātrāt iṣṭa siddheḥ tad anirdeśe ca katham tad viśiṣṭena anvayaḥ tat ayam agninā avinā bhāvī siddhaḥ arthāt eva agneḥ tad pradeśa ayogam vyavacchinatti iti sa tathā sādhyaḥ ucyate na punar tathā asya upanyāsa pūrvakaḥ anvayaḥ sa adhya ukteḥ iha anaṅga tvāt tad pūrvaka tve vā kaḥ pratijñām sādhanāt apākaroti tathā ca āha liṅgasya avyabhicāraḥ tu dharmeṇa anyatra darśyate tatra prasiddham tat yuktam dharmiṇam gamayiṣyati tasmāt na agni ādi sādhana vat sattā sādhanam api anavadyam iti 
[095,11_095,17]	aparāmṛṣṭa tad bhede vastu mātre tu sādhane tanmātra vyāpinaḥ sādhyasya anvayaḥ na vihanyate sādhane punar sattve svabhāva viśeṣa aparigraheṇa vastu mātra vyāpini sādhya dharme na anvaya vyāghātaḥ na hi tatra avaśyam viśeṣa parigrahaḥ kāryaḥ sat mātra āśraye api sādhana sāmarthyāt na sādhya tve vaiphalyāt api ca na asiddhe bhāva dharmaḥ asti vyabhicāryu bhaya āśrayaḥ dharmaḥ viruddhaḥ abhāvasya sā sattā sādhyate katham 
[095,19^1]	sattāyām hi sādhyāyām sarvaḥ tad hetuḥ na trayīm doṣa jātim atipatati asiddhim vyabhicāram virodham ca tatra yadi bhāva dharmaḥ hetuḥ ucyate sa katham asiddha sattāke syāt yaḥ hi bhāva dharmam tatra icchati sa katham bhāvam na icchet svabhāvaḥ eva hi kayācid apekṣayā dharmaḥ iti vyatirekī iva dharmiṇaḥ nirdiśyate na hi dharma dharmi vācinoḥ śabdayoḥ vācye kaścid viśeṣaḥ asti iti uktam etat atha punar ubhaya dharmam brūyāt anāśrita vastunaḥ aparyudāsena vyatireka mātrasya abhāve api avirodhāt yathā na bhavati mūrtaḥ iti amūrta tvam nirupākhye api syāt nirupākhyasya abhāvāt na pratiṣedha viṣaya tā iti ced tat kim idānīm vidhi viṣayaḥ astu tat api naḥ iti ced katham idānīm na pratiṣedha viṣayaḥ vidhi ni vṛtti rūpa tvāt pratiṣedhasya 
[095,19^2]	tat etat vyavaccheda mātram dvayoḥ api sambhavat vipakṣa pracāra śaṅkā vyavacchedena labhyam gamaka tvam katham ātmasāt kuryāt sa ca svayam sva vāca ubhaya dharma tām bruvāṇaḥ sataḥ anyatra api asya vṛttim bhāṣate sattāyām ca avyabhicāram iti katham naḥ unmattaḥ abhāva dharmam tu bhāva mātra vyāpinaḥ arthasya vyavacchedam hetum sattāyām vadataḥ asya viruddhaḥ hetuḥ syāt tasya bhāve kvacid asambhavāt abhāve ca bhāva vyavacchedasya bhāvāt tat ayam tri prakāraḥ api dharmaḥ sattā sādhane na hetu lakṣaṇa bhāj na ca anyā gatiḥ asti tasmāt na sattā sādhyate sādhana tve punar asyāḥ sāmānyena tanmātra vyāpini vastu dharme siddha sattāke dharmiṇi na asiddhiḥ tena ca sādhya dharmeṇa vyāptiḥ yadi kathaṃcid niścīyate na virodhavyabhicārau iti na ayam prasaṅgaḥ aniścitāyām tu vyāptau dharmi samāśraye vā tad svabhāvatayā gamakaḥ na kaścid gamakaḥ atas eva svadharmeṇa vyāptaḥ
[096,26_097,07]	siddhaḥ svabhāvaḥ gamakaḥ vācyaḥ na hi prakāśa tayā prakāśayan pradīpaḥ tad rūpa apratipattau svām artha kriyām karoti vyāpakaḥ tasya niścitaḥ gamyaḥ svabhāvas tad dharma niścayāt eva niścitaḥ vyāpaka tvena tasya dharmiṇaḥ dharmaḥ gamyaḥ tasya ayam nivṛttau vā nivartakaḥ 
[097,08]	tasya vyāpyasya dharmasya ayam nivartakaḥ vyāpakaḥ dharmaḥ svayam nirvartamānaḥ evam hi ayam asya vyāpakaḥ siddhaḥ bhavati yadi asya abhāve na bhavet tat anena dvividhasya api sādhana prayogasya gamaka tā lakṣaṇam uktam veditavyam dvividhaḥ hi prayogaḥ sādharmyeṇa vaidharmyeṇa ca yathā āhuḥ eke anvayī vyatirekī ca iti na anayoḥ vastutas kaścid bhedaḥ anyatra prayoga bhedāt sādharmyeṇa api hi prayoge arthāt vaidharmya gatiḥ asati tasmin sādhyena hetoḥ anvaya abhāvāt tathā vaidharmye api anvaya gatiḥ asati tasmin sādhya abhāve hetu abhāvasya sandehāt iti vistareṇa vakṣyāmaḥ 
[097,18_097,19]	anitya tve yathā kāryam akāryam vā avināśini anena udāharaṇam anayoḥ darśayati tatra anvayī yat kiṃcid kṛtakam tat sarvam anityam yathā ghaṭa ādayaḥ śabdaḥ ca kṛtakaḥ iti kṛtaka tvasya api anitya tvena vyāptim pradarśya śabdaḥ yaḥ kṛtaka tve kathite sāmarthyāt eva anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti tasmāt na avaśyam iha pakṣa nirdeśaḥ iti ayam anvayinaḥ prayogaḥ vyatireke api na anitya tva abhāve kṛtaka tvam bhavati śabdaḥ ca kṛtakaḥ iti siddha tad svabhāva tayā tad abhāve na bhavataḥ kṛtaka tvasya śabde ca bhāva khyātau tad ātmanaḥ sataḥ bhāvaḥ iti sāmarthyāt siddheḥ pūrvavān na pratijñā vacanam anvayaḥ tu arthāpattyā siddhaḥ na hi atada ātma niyatasya tad nivṛttau nivṛttiḥ tasmāt tat niyamam prasādhya nivṛttiḥ vaktavyā sā ced sidhyati tad ātma niyamam arthāt sūcayati iti siddhaḥ anvayaḥ katham idānīm kṛtakaḥ avaśyam anityaḥ iti pratyetavyaḥ yena evam ucyate yasmāt 
[098,06_098,11]	ahetu tvāt vināśasya svabhāvāt anubandhitā na hi bhāvāḥ vinaśyantaḥ tad bhāve hetum apekṣante sva hetoḥ eva vinaśvarāṇām bhāvāt tasmāt yaḥ kaścid kṛtakaḥ sa prakṛtyāḥ eva naśvaraḥ tathā hi sa apekṣāṇām hi bhāvānām na avaśyaṃbhāvitā īkṣyate nirapekṣaḥ bhāvaḥ vināśe sa apekṣa tve hi ghaṭa ādīnām keṣāṃcid nityatā api syāt yena
[098,13_098,18]	bāhulye api hi tad hetoḥ bhavet kvacid asambhavaḥ yadi api bahulam vināśa kāraṇāni santi teṣām api sva pratyaya adhīna saṃnidhi tvāt na avaśyam saṃnidhānam iti kaścid na vinaśyet api na hi avaśyam hetavaḥ phalavantaḥ vaikalya pratibandha sambhavāt etena vyabhicāri tvam uktam kārya avyavasthiteḥ sarveṣām nāśa hetūnām hetum at nāśa vādinām 
[098,20^1]	iti antaraślokaḥ tat ayam bhāvaḥ anapekṣaḥ tad bhāvam prati tad bhāva niyataḥ asambhavat pratibandhāḥ iva kāraṇa sāmagrī sakalā kārya utpādane nanu anapekṣāṇām api keṣāṃcid kvacid na avaśyam tad bhāvaḥ bhūmi bīja udaka sāmagryām api kadācid aṅkurānutpatteḥ na tatra api santāna pariṇāma apekṣa tvāt na evam bhāvasya kācid apekṣā tatra api antyā kāraṇa sāmagrī yā avyavahitā kārya utpatteḥ sā phalavatī eva saḥ eva ca tatra aṅkura hetuḥ anyaḥ tu pūrvaḥ pariṇāmaḥ tad arthaḥ eva na ca tām tatra kaścid pratibandhum samarthaḥ ekatra bhāve vikārān utpatteḥ utpattau vai eka tva hāneḥ tad ātmanaḥ ca apracyutasya tad utpādanam prati vaiguṇyam kāraṇasya akurvāṇasya pratibandha hetoḥ apratibandhaka tvāt 
[098,20^2]	nanu yava bīja ādayaḥ api śāli aṅkure janye na sa apekṣāḥ tad utpatti pratyayānām kadācid tatra api saṃnidhānāt katham na sa apekṣāḥ yāvatā saḥ eva eṣām svabhāvaḥ na asti yaḥ tad utpādanaḥ śālibījasya iti tad svabhāva apekṣāḥ evam tarhi kṛtakānām api keṣāṃcid satām vā saḥ eva svabhāvaḥ na asti yaḥ vinaśvaraḥ tasmāt tad svabhāva apekṣa tvāt na vinaśvarāḥ śāli bīja ādīnām api sa svabhāvaḥ sva hetoḥ iti yaḥ na tad hetuḥ saḥ atad svabhāvaḥ syāt niyata śaktiḥ ca sa hetuḥ sva rūpeṇa pratītaḥ eva na ca svabhāva niyamaḥ arthānām ākasmikaḥ yuktaḥ anapekṣasya deśa kāla dravya niyama ayogāt tathā atra api niyama hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ yatas ime kecid naśvara ātmanaḥ jātāḥ na ca atra kaścid niyāmakaḥ svabhāvasya asti sarva janminām vināśa siddheḥ 
[098,20^3]	janmi svabhāvaḥ na āśī iti ced na vai janma nāśi svabhāvasya hetuḥ na ca ahetoḥ svabhāva niyamaḥ tasmāt na atra kaścid hetoḥ svabhāva pravibhāgaḥ tad abhāvāt phalasya api na asti iti asamānam sā iyam nirapekṣatā vināśasya kvacid kadācid ca bhāva virodhinī tad abhāvam svabhāvena sādhayati yaḥ hi svabhāvaḥ nirapekṣaḥ sa yadi kadācid bhavet kvacid vā tad kāla dravya apekṣaḥ iti nirapekṣaḥ eva na syāt iti uktam sa tarhi naśvaraḥ svabhāvaḥ nirapekṣaḥ iti ahetukaḥ syāt na ahetukaḥ sattā hetoḥ eva bhāvāt tathā utpatteḥ sataḥ hi bhavataḥ tādṛśasya eva bhāvāt na avaśyam sataḥ kutaścid bhāvaḥ iti ced ākasmikī tarhi sattā iti na iyam kasyacid kadācid kvacid viramet 
[098,20^4]	tat hi kiṃcid upalīyeta na vā yasya yatra kiṃcid pratibaddham apratibaddham vā sā iyam sattā apratibandhinī ced niyamavatī na syāt tasmāt na iyam ākasmikī kvacid katham tarhi idānīm ahetukaḥ vināśaḥ uktaḥ jātasya tad bhāve anya anapekṣaṇāt uktam ca atra na vināśaḥ nāma anyaḥ eva kaścid bhāvāt svabhāvaḥ eva hi nāśaḥ saḥ eva hi eka kṣaṇa sthāyī jātaḥ iti tam asya mandāḥ svabhāvam ūrdhvam vyavasyanti na prāk darśane api pāṭava abhāvāt iti tad vaśena paścāt vyavasthāpyate vikāra darśanena iva viṣam ajñaiḥ tat ayam sattā vyatirekeṇa na anyat kiṃcid vināśaḥ apekṣate iti tad vyāpī katham punar etat gamyate nirapekṣaḥ vināśaḥ iti 
[100,10_100,11]	asāmarthyāt ca tad hetoḥ abhāva kāriṇaḥ kriyā pratiṣedhāt ca iti caśabdāt katham asāmarthyam siddhe hi bhāve kārakaḥ na tam karoti na api anya kriyāyām tasya kiṃcid iti tad atad rūpā karaṇāt ca akiṃcitkaraḥ na apekṣyate iti katham kriyā pratiṣedhaḥ vināśaḥ iti hi te bhāva abhāvam manyante tat ayam vināśa hetuḥ abhāvam karoti iti prāptam tatra yadi abhāvaḥ nāma kaścid kāryaḥ syāt svabhāvaḥ saḥ eva bhāvaḥ iti na abhāvaḥ syāt tasmāt abhāvam karoti iti bhāvam na karoti iti kriyā pratiṣedhaḥ asya kṛtaḥ syāt tathā api ayam akiṃcitkaraḥ kim iti apekṣyate iti siddhā vināśam prati anapekṣayā bhāvasya tasmāt 
[100,21_100,28]	 bhavati eṣa svabhāvataḥ yatra nāma bhavati asmāt anyatra api svabhāvataḥ saḥ ayam kvacid bhavan dṛṣṭaḥ anapekṣa tvāt svabhāvataḥ eva bhavati tathā anyatra api svabhāva bhāvī viśeṣa abhāvāt iti yā kācid bhāva viṣayā dvidhā eva anumitiḥ tatas sva sādhye kārya bhāvābhyām sambandha niyamāt tayoḥ tasmāt dvi prakārāḥ eva vastu viṣaya anumitiḥ kārya liṅgā svabhāva liṅgā ca yathāsvam vyāpini sādhye tayoḥ eva pratibandhāt liṅgayoḥ liṅgini yathā uktam prāk 
[101,03_101,05]	pravṛtteḥ buddhi pūrva tvāt tad bhāva anupalambhane pravartitavyam naḥ iti ukta anupalabdheḥ pramāṇa tā tṛtīyaḥ tu hetuḥ anupalabdhiḥ aviśeṣeṇa kvacid arthe gamakaḥ iti ucyate sanniścaya śabda vyavahāra pratiṣedhe hi sarvāḥ eva anupalabdhiḥ liṅgam sanniścayāt hi śabda vyavahārāḥ pravartante te pravṛttiḥ iti uktāḥ tathā hi anupalabdhiḥ eva asattvam iti uktam prāk tat ca pratipattṛ vaśāt na vastu vaśāt tāvat hi sa bhāvaḥ asya na asti yāvat atra apratipattiḥ satā api te na tad artha ākaraṇāt vastutas tu anupalabhyamānaḥ na san na asan satām api svabhāva ādi viprakarṣāt kadācid anupalambhāt tasya asatsu api tulya tvāt tat etat pratipattuḥ pramāṇa abhāvāt nivṛttam sattvam anupalabdhi lakṣaṇam sva nimittān śabda vyavahārān nivartayati tena yāḥ api iyam anupalabdhiḥ upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptānām vastutas api asattva rūpāḥ apravṛtti yogya tvāt tasyāḥ api etat tulyam prāmāṇyam atra viṣaye asat niścaya phalāḥ api sā asattāyām api iyam pramāṇam eva na hi asti sambhavaḥ yat upalabdhi yogyaḥ sakaleṣu anyeṣu kāraṇeṣu san naḥ upalabhyeta na punar pūrvā asattā sādhānī yasmāt 
[101,21_101,23]	śāstra adhikāra asambaddhāḥ bahavaḥ arthāḥ atīndriyāḥ aliṅgāḥ ca katham teṣām abhāvaḥ anupalabdhitaḥ saḥ ayam asattām sādhayan anupalabdhi mātreṇa sarva arthānām pramāṇa traya nivṛttyā sādhayet tatra na śāstra nivṛttiḥ abhāva sādhanī tasya kvacid anadhikāre apravṛtteḥ śāstram hi pravartamānam kaṃcid puruṣa artha sādhanam upāyam āśritya pravartate anyathā abaddha pralāpasya aprāmāṇyāt tatra ca prakaraṇe bahavaḥ arthāḥ na avaśyam nirdeśyāḥ yathā pratyātma niyatāḥ kāścana puruṣāṇām cetaḥ vṛttayaḥ aniyata nimitta bhāvinyaḥ deśa kāla vyavahitāḥ vā prakaraṇa anupayoginaḥ dravya viśeṣāḥ na tān śāstram viṣayīkaroti na ca tathā viprakṛṣṭeṣu sva sāmarthya upadhānau jñāna utpādana śaktiḥ asti na ca avaśyam eṣām kārya upalambhaḥ yena anumīyeran na ca te pramāṇa traya nivṛttau api na santi iti śakyante vyavasātum tasmāt na sarva anupalabdhiḥ sādhanī nivṛtti niścayasya tat iyam 
[102,13_102,23]	sat asat niścaya phalā naḥ iti syāt vā apramāṇa tā na eva vā iyam anupalabdhiḥ pramāṇam vyavasāya phala tvāt pramāṇānām na hi pravṛtti niṣedhe api iyam niḥśaṅka paricchedam cetaḥ karoti saṃśayāt api kvacid lokasya pravṛtteḥ tathā tve tat niravadyam yadi niścaya pūrvam vyavaharet iti sā iyam apravṛttiphalā proktā pramāṇam api kācid syāt liṅga atiśaya bhāvinī atra na sarva anupalabdhiḥ apramāṇam pramāṇam api kācid liṅga viśeṣa bhāvinī yathā udāhṛtā prāk yat punar uktam apramāṇam anupalabdhiḥ iti svabhāva jñāpaka ajñānasya ayam nyāya udāhṛtaḥ 
[103,01]	yasya kasyacid svabhāvaḥ naḥ upalabhyate deśa ādi viprakarṣāt na sa tad anupalambha mātreṇa asat nāma yathoktam prāk yaḥ api jñāpakasya liṅgasya abhāvāt atīndriyaḥ pratikṣipyate arthaḥ svabhāva viśeṣaḥ vā yathā na asti viraktam cetaḥ devatā viśeṣaḥ vā na asti dāna hiṃsā virati cetanānām abhyudaya hetu tāḥ iti pratyakṣe api arthe phalasya ānantarya abhāvāt atad phala sādharmyāt viparyastaḥ apavadeta api na tāvatā tad abhāvaḥ eva vyavahitānām api hetoḥ phalānām utpatti darśanāt mūṣika alarka viṣa vikāra vat tad bhāve virodha abhāvāt atra anupalabdhi mātram apramāṇam bhāve kim pramāṇam iti ced atas eva saṃśayaḥ astu bhavet vā pramāṇam iti apratikṣepaḥ tat atra keṣāṃcid arthānām svabhāvānām vā darśana pāṭava abhāvāt kāraṇānām kārya utpādana niyama abhāvāt ca bhavet jñāpakā siddhiḥ neyatā tad abhāvaḥ punar paryāyeṇa keṣāṃcid abhivyakteḥ 
[103,15_103,16]	kārye tu kāraka ajñānam abhāvasya eva sādhakam svabhāva abhāve sādhye tad anupalambhaḥ eva apramāṇam ucyate kāraka anupalambhaḥ tu pramāṇam eva na hi asti sambhavaḥ yat asati kāraṇe kāryam syāt nanu kadācid kāraṇa nāśe api kārya sthitiḥ dṛṣṭā na brūmaḥ kāraṇa sthiti kāla bhāvī kāryam iti hetu rahitā tu bhāva utpattiḥ na asti iti ucyate na ca tathā sthāyī bhāvaḥ tad upādānaḥ pāraṃparyeṇa tu santāna upakārāt tad kārya vyapadeśaḥ yadi asya kathaṃcid abhāvaḥ sidhyet tat phalam na asti iti niścīyate 
[103,23_104,01]	svabhāva anupalambhaḥ ca svabhāve arthasya liṅgini svabhāva abhāvaḥ eva liṅgini svabhāva anupalambhaḥ api kaścid pramāṇam eva eva yadi anupalabhyamānaḥ vyāpakaḥ svabhāvaḥ asya siddhiḥ syāt yathā vṛkṣa tvam śiṃśapāyāḥ tad abhāvaḥ pratīyeta hetunā yadi kenacid yadi asya kāraṇasya svabhāvasya vyāpakasya vā abhāvaḥ kutaścid gamakāt hetoḥ sidhyet saḥ ayam asan eva sva kāryam vyāpyam vā nivartayati tad abhāva asiddhau nivartye api saṃśayāt katham idānīm bhāvasya svayam anupalabdheḥ abhāva siddhiḥ 
[104,06_104,13]	dṛśyasya darśana abhāva kāraṇā sambhave sati bhāvasya anupalabdhasya bhāva abhāvaḥ pratīyate bhāvaḥ hi yadi bhavet yathāsvam grāhakeṇa karaṇena upalabhyaḥ eva bhavet sa darśana pratibandhiṣu vyavadhāna ādiṣu asatsu upalabhyaḥ eva anupalabdhaḥ tu asan iti niścīyate tādṛśaḥ sataḥ upalambha avi abhicārāt ayam eva hetuḥ hetu vyāpakayoḥ abhāve api veditavyaḥ viruddhasya ca bhāvasya bhāve tad bhāva bādhanāt tad viruddha upalabdhau syāt asattāyāḥ viniścayaḥ 
[104,15^1]	yaḥ hi bhāvaḥ yena saha na avatiṣṭhate tad upādānayoḥ anyonya vaiguṇya āśraya tvena ārambha virodhāt tayoḥ viruddhayoḥ ekasya bhāve api anya abhāva gatiḥ bhavati yathoktam prāk idam anupalabdheḥ na pṛthak vyavasthāpyate tatas eva virodha gateḥ virodhāt ca abhāva sādhanāt bhavatu nāma evaṃvidhāyāḥ anupalabdheḥ abhāva gatiḥ sā punar katham anumānam katham ca na syāt dṛṣṭānta anapekṣaṇāt na hi asyām kaścid dṛṣṭāntaḥ asti kim na nirupākhyam vyoma kusuma ādi dṛṣṭāntaḥ tat asat katham avagantavyam yena evam syāt 
[104,15^2]	anupalabdheḥ eva iti ced tatra katham adṛṣṭāntikāḥ asattā siddhiḥ sa dṛṣṭānta tve vā anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ tathā ca apratipattiḥ tasmāt nirupākhya abhāva siddhi vat anyatra api dṛṣṭānta anapekṣaṇāt ananumānam śṛṇvan api devānāṃpriyaḥ na avadhāraṇa paṭuḥ nimittam hi asat śabda vyavahārāṇām upalabhya anupalabdhiḥ sā sva saṃnidhānāt sva nimittān etān sādhayati iti sva nimitta sāmagrī yogya saṃnidhānaḥ sarvaḥ atra dṛṣṭāntaḥ asattā punar atra anupalabdhiḥ eva atas eva iyam kāraṇāt kārya anumāna lakṣaṇa tvāt 
[104,15^3]	svabhāva hetau antar bhavati iti vakṣyāmaḥ sat śabda vyavahāra pratiṣedhe api pramāṇa nivṛttyā nimitta vaikalya abhāvinaḥ aṅkura ādayaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ na kevalam nirupākhyam nirupākhye api iyam eva pravṛttiḥ niṣidhyate anupalabdhi lakṣaṇāḥ asattā siddhāḥ eva saḥ ayam mūḍhaḥ nimittam tad abhāvam vā abhyupagamya pravṛtti nivṛttī vilomayan yathā abhyupagamam pratipādyate nirupākhya vat anya vat vā iti saḥ eva tāvat upalabdhi abhāvaḥ katham siddhaḥ iti ced etat uttaratra vakṣyāmaḥ 
[104,15^4_105,20]	anyatra api anumāne sādhya dharmeṇa vyāptam sādhanam icchan kim iti dṛṣṭāntena pratyāyyaḥ vyāpya nirdeśāt eva vyāpnuvataḥ siddheḥ niścita arthasya api smṛti arthaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti ced tat itaratra api samānam saḥ ayam anyatra anupalambha mātrāt asat vyavahāram pratipadyamānaḥ api iha vyāmūḍhaḥ iti smāryate atha yat idam na santi pradhāna ādayaḥ anupalabdheḥ iti tatra katham asat vyavahāra vidhiḥ sat vyavahāra niṣedhaḥ vā katham ca na syāt tad artha pratiṣedhe dharmi vācinaḥ aprayogāt abhidhānasya nirviṣayasya ca pratiṣedhasya ayogāt na eṣa doṣaḥ yasmāt anādi vāsanā udbhūta vikalpa pariniṣṭhitaḥ śabda arthaḥ trividhaḥ dharmaḥ bhāva abhāva ubhayāśrayaḥ tasmin bhāvānupādāne sādhye asya anupalambhanam tathā hetuḥ na tasya eva abhāvaḥ śabda prayogataḥ 
[105,24]	niveditam etat yathā naḥ ete śabdāḥ sva lakṣaṇa viṣayāḥ anādi vāsanā prabhava vikalpa pratibhāsinam artham viṣaya tvena ātmasāt kurvanti vaktuḥ śrotuḥ ca tad vikalpa bhājaḥ yathā pratibhāsi vastu pratipādana samīhā prayogāt tad ākāra vikalpa jananāt ca na ca upādāna kārya pratyaya apratibhā asi rūpam śakyam tad viṣaya tvena adhyavasātum sa tu vikalpaḥ sat asat ubhaya pratyaya ahita vāsanā prabhavaḥ iti tad pratibhā asi a ākāra adhyavasāya vaśena ca bhāva abhāva ubhaya dharmaḥ iti ucyate tat atra dharmiṇi vyavasthitāḥ sat asat tvam cintayanti kim ayam pradhāna śabda pratibhāsi arthaḥ bhāva upādānaḥ na vā iti tasya bhāvān upādāna tve sādhye saḥ eva pratyātma vedya tvāt apratikṣepa arhaḥ arthaḥ dharmī na ca saḥ eva arthaḥ sva lakṣaṇam iti śakyam vaktum asamprāpta niruddhayoḥ api arthayoḥ tasya anapāyāt vastu viparīta ākāra niveśiṣu api tīrtha ānantarīya pratyayeṣu bhāvāt 
[106,11_106,15]	parama artha eka tāna tve śabdānām anibandhanā na syāt pravṛttiḥ artheṣu darśana antara bhediṣu atīta ajātayoḥ vā api na ca syāt anṛta artha tā vācaḥ kasyāścid iti eṣā bauddha artha viṣayā matā iti saṃgraha ślokau tasya ca yathā samīhita rūpa anupādāna tve sādhye tathā anupalambhaḥ asya dharmaḥ asti iti na sādhana dharma asiddhiḥ na punar atra ayam eva śabda vikalpa pratibhāsi arthaḥ apahnūyate tasya buddhau upasthāpanāya śabda prayogāt tad abhāve tad ayogāt api ca 
[106,20_106,27]	śabda artha apahnave sādhye dharma ādhāra nirākṛteḥ na sādhyaḥ samudāyaḥ syāt siddhaḥ dharmaḥ ca kevalaḥ yadi hi śabda arthaḥ eva apohyeta pradhāna śabda vācyasya dharmiṇaḥ eva nirākaraṇāt nirādhāraḥ sādhya dharmaḥ syāt tat ayam ādhāravyavaccheda anapekṣaḥ na vivāda āśrayaḥ iti naḥ upanyasanīyaḥ eva syāt kim ca sat asat pakṣa bhedena śabda arthānapavādibhiḥ vastu eva cintyate hi atra pratibaddhaḥ phala udayaḥ artha kriyā samarthasya vicāraiḥ kim tad arthinām ṣaṇḍhasya rūpa vairūpye kāminyāḥ kim parīkṣayā 
[107,01]	na hi śabda arthaḥ asan san vā kaṃcid puruṣa artham uparuṇaddhi samādadhāti vā yathā abhiniveśam atattvāt yathā atattvam ca asamīhita tvāt tat ayam pravartamānaḥ sarvadā sat asat cintāyām avadhīrita vikalpa pratibhāsaḥ vastu eva adhiṣṭhānīkaroti yatra ayam puruṣa arthaḥ pratibaddhaḥ yathā agnau śīta pratīkāra ādiḥ na hi atra śabda arthaḥ samarthaḥ tad anubhava āptau api tad abhāvāt tat ayam artha kriyā arthī tat asamartham prati datta anuyogaḥ bhavitum na yuktaḥ na hi vṛṣasyantī ṣaṇḍhasya rūpa vairūpya parīkṣāyām avadhat te yat punar etat uktam kalpitasya anupalabdhiḥ dharmaḥ iti tasya kaḥ arthaḥ 
[107,11_107,13]	śabda arthaḥ kalpanā jñāna viṣaya tvena kalpitaḥ dharmaḥ vastu āśraya asiddhiḥ asya uktaḥ nyāya vādinā kalpanā viṣaya tvāt śabda arthaḥ eva kalpitaḥ tasya vastu āśraya anupalambhaḥ dharmaḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ yat uktam na pramāṇa traya nivṛttau api bhāva abhāva siddhiḥ iti tat mā bhūt anya pramāṇa anivṛttau nivṛttiḥ tayoḥ asakala viṣaya tvāt āgamaḥ punar na kiṃcid na vyāpnoti tad nivṛttiḥ katham na gamikāḥ iti uktam atra naḥ āgameṣu sarva arthāḥ upanibadhyante aprakaraṇa āpanna tvāt iti 
[107,19_107,22]	api ca na antarīyaka tā abhāvāt śabdānām vastubhiḥ saha na artha siddhiḥ tatas te hi vaktrabhiprāya sūcakāḥ na hi śabdāḥ yathābhāvam vartante yatas tebhyaḥ artha prakṛtiḥ niścīyeta te hi vaktuḥ vivakṣā vṛttayaḥ iti tat na antarīyakāḥ tām eva gamayeyuḥ na ca puruṣa icchāḥ sarvāḥ yathā artha bhāvinyaḥ na ca tad apratibaddha svabhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ anyam gamayati yat tarhi idam āpta vāda avisaṃvāda sāmānyāt anumāna tā iti āgamasya prāmāṇyam anumāna tvam uktam tat katham na ayam puruṣaḥ anāśritya āgama asitum samarthaḥ atyakṣa phalānām keṣāṃcid pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ mahā anuśaṃsā pāpa śravaṇāt tad bhāve virodha adarśanāt ca tat sati pravartitavye varam evam pravṛttaḥ iti parīkṣayā prāmāṇyam āha tat ca 
[108,07_108,09]	sambaddha anuguṇa upāyam puruṣa artha abhidhāyakam parīkṣā adhikṛtam vākyam atas anadhikṛtam param sambaddhaḥ vākyānām eka artha upasaṃhāra upakāraḥ na daśa dāḍima ādi vākyānām iva anupasaṃhāraḥ eva anyathā vaktuḥ vaiguṇyam udbhāvayet aśakya upāya phalāni ca śāstrāṇi phala arthī na ādriyeta vicārayitum apuruṣa artha phalāni ca viṣa śamanāya takṣaka phaṇa ratna alaṃkāra upadeśa vat kāka danta parīkṣā vat ca tat viparyayeṇa upasaṃhāra vat śakya upāyam puruṣa artha abhidhāyi ca śāstram parīkṣyeta anyatra avadhānasya eva ayukta tvāt tat yadi na parīkṣāyām visaṃvāda bhāj pravartamānaḥ śobheta kaḥ punar asya avisaṃvādaḥ 
[108,18_108,20]	pratyakṣeṇa anumānena dvividhena api abādhakam dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa arthayoḥ asya avisaṃvādaḥ tad arthayoḥ pratyakṣeṇa abādhanam pratyakṣa abhimatānām arthānām tathā abhāvaḥ yathā nīla ādi sukha duḥkha nimitta upalakṣaṇa rāga ādi buddhīnām atatha abhimatānām ca apratyakṣatā yathā śabda ādi rūpa saṃniveśinām sukha ādīnām dravya karma sāmānya saṃyoga ādīnām ca tathā anāgama apekṣa anumāna viṣaya abhimatānām tathā abhāvaḥ yathā catūrṇām ārya satyānām ananumeyānām tathā abhāvaḥ yathā ātma ādīnām āgama apekṣā anumāne api yathā rāga ādi rūpam tat prabhavam ca adharmam abhyupagamya tad prahāṇāya snāna agni hotra ādeḥ anupadeśaḥ saḥ iyam śakya pariccheda aśeṣa viṣaya viśuddhiḥ avisaṃvādaḥ 
[109,05_109,13]	āpta vāda avisaṃvāda sāmānyāt anumāna tā buddheḥ agatyāḥ abhihitā parokṣe api asya gocare tasya ca asya evaṃbhūtasya āpta bhūtasya avisaṃvāda sāmānyāt adṛṣṭa vyabhicārasya pratyakṣa anumāna agamye api arthe pratipatteḥ tad āśraya tvāt tad anya pratipatti vat avisaṃvādaḥ anumīyate tatas śabda prabhavāḥ api satī na śābda vat abhiprāyam nivedayati eva iti artha avisaṃvādāt anumānam api athavā anyathā āpta vādasya avisaṃvādāt anumāna tvam ucyate heya upādeya tattvasya saḥ upāyasya prasiddhitaḥ pradhāna artha avisaṃvādāt anumānam paratra vā 
[109,15]	heya upādeya tad upāyānām tad upadiṣṭānām avaiparītyam avisaṃvādaḥ yathā catūrṇām ārya satyānām vakṣyamāṇanītyā tasya asya puruṣa artha upayoginaḥ abhiyoga arthasya avisaṃvādāt viṣaya antare api tathā tva upagamaḥ na vipralambhāya anuparodhāt niṣprayojana vitatha abhidhāna vaiphalyāt ca vaktuḥ tat etat agatyāḥ ubhayathā api anumāna tvam āgamasya upavarṇitam varam āgamāt pravṛttau evam pravṛttiḥ iti na khalu evam anumānam anapāyam anāntarīyaka tvāt artheṣu śabdānām iti niveditam etat 
[109,23_110,03]	puruṣa atiśaya apekṣam yathārtham apare viduḥ yathā artha darśana ādi guṇa yuktaḥ puruṣaḥ āptaḥ tad praṇayanam avisaṃvādaḥ iti anye iṣṭaḥ ayam arthaḥ śakyeta jñātum saḥ atiśayaḥ yadi sarve eva āgamam anāgamam vā pravṛtti kāmaḥ anveṣate prekṣā pūrva kārī na vyasanena api nāma anuṣṭheyam atas jñātvā pravṛttaḥ arthavān syām iti sa śakya darśana avisaṃvāda pratyayena anyatra api pravartate evaṃprāya tvāt loka vyavahārasya 
[110,06_110,11]	puruṣa parīkṣayā tu pravṛttau apravṛttiḥ eva tasya tathābhūtasya jñātum aśakya tvāt na aniṣṭeḥ tādṛśām avitatha abhidhānāt tathā hi ayam evam na vā iti anya doṣa anirdoṣa tā api vā durlabha tvāt pramāṇānām durbodhāḥ iti apare viduḥ ca etasyebhyaḥ hi guṇa doṣebhyaḥ puruṣāḥ samyak mithyā pravṛttaḥ te ca atīndriyāḥ sva prabhava kāya vāc vyavahāra anumeyāḥ syuḥ vyavahārāḥ ca prāyaśas buddhi pūrvam anyathā api kartum śakyante puruṣa icchā vṛtti tvāt teṣām ca citra abhisandhi tvāt tat ayam liṅga saṃkarāt katham aniścinvan pratipadyeta atha kim naḥ eva sa tādṛśaḥ puruṣaḥ asti yaḥ nirdoṣaḥ 
[110,17_110,27]	sarveṣām sa vipakṣa tvāt nirhrāsa atiśaya śritām saḥ ātmībhāvāt tad abhyāsāt dhīyeran āśravāḥ kvacid sa tu prahīṇa āśravaḥ durjñānaḥ doṣāḥ hi nirhrāsa atiśaya dharmaṇaḥ vipakṣa abhibhava utkarṣa apakarṣam sādhayanti jvālā ādi vat te hi vikalpa prabhavāḥ sati api upādāne kasyacid manaḥ guṇasya abhyāsāt apakarṣiṇaḥ tad pāṭave niranvaya vināśa dharmāṇaḥ syuḥ jvālā ādi vat eva tena syāt api nirdoṣaḥ katham nirdoṣaḥ nāma yāvatā doṣa vipakṣa sātma tve api doṣa sātmanaḥ vipakṣa utpatti vat yathāpratyayam doṣa utpattiḥ api na ayam doṣaḥ yasmāt nirupadrava bhūta artha svabhāvasya viparyayaiḥ na bādhā yatnavat tve api buddheḥ tad pakṣa pātataḥ 
[111,01]	na hi svabhāvaḥ ayatnena vinivartayitum śakyaḥ śrotriya kāpālika ghṛṇā vat yatnaḥ ca prāpya nivartyayoḥ svabhāvayoḥ guṇa doṣa darśanena kriyeta tat ca vipakṣa sa ātmanaḥ puruṣasya doṣeṣu na sambhavati tasya nirupadrava tvāt aśeṣa doṣa hāneḥ paryavasthāna janma pratibaddha duḥkha vivekāt praśama sukha rasasya anudvejanāt ca abhūta artham khalu api upādāna bala bhāvi santānasya viparyaya upādānāt na syāt na tu bhūta artham vastu bala utpatteḥ abhūta arthāḥ ca doṣāḥ na pratipakṣa sātmya bādhinaḥ tasmāt na punar doṣa utpattiḥ yatne api buddheḥ guṇa pakṣapātena pratipakṣaḥ eva yatna ādhānāt parīkṣāvataḥ viśeṣeṇa aduṣṭa ātmanaḥ kaḥ punar eṣām doṣāṇām prabhavaḥ yat pratipakṣa abhyāsāt prahīyante
