[111,13_111,21]	sarvāsām doṣa jātīnām jātiḥ sat kāya darśanāt sā avidyā tatra tad snehaḥ tasmāt dveṣa ādi sambhavaḥ na hi na aham na mama iti paśyatam parigraham antareṇa kvacid snehaḥ na ca ananurāgiṇaḥ kvacid dveṣaḥ ātmā ātmīya anuparodhini uparodha pratighātini ca tad abhāvāt tasmāt samāna jātīya abhyāsa jam ātma darśanam ātmīya graham prasūte tau ca tat sneham sa ca dveṣa ādīni iti sat kāya darśana jāḥ sarva doṣāḥ tat eva ca ajñānam iti ucyate mohaḥ nidānam doṣāṇām atas eva abhidhīyate satkāya dṛṣṭiḥ anyatra tad prahāṇe prahāṇataḥ 
[111,23]	moham doṣa nidānam āhuḥ amūḍhasya doṣān utpatteḥ punar anyatra sat kāya dṛṣṭim tat ca etat pradhāna nirdeśe sati syāt aneka janmanām doṣāṇām eka utpatti virodhāt na ca dvayoḥ prādhānye ekaika nirdeśaḥ para bhāga bhāj ubhayathā api ekasya nirdeśe na virodhaḥ prādhānyam punar tad upādāna tvena tad prahāṇe doṣāṇām prahāṇāt tasmāt sambhavati sat kāya darśana janmanām doṣāṇām tad pratipakṣa nairātmya darśana abhyāsāt prahāṇam sa tu kṣīṇa doṣaḥ duranvayaḥ yat upadeśāt ayam pratipadyeta 
[112,06_112,14]	mā bhūt puruṣa āśrayam vacanam āgamaḥ praṇetuḥ duranvayatvāt girām mithyātva hetūnām doṣāṇām puruṣa āśrayāt apauruṣeyam satya artham iti kecid pracakṣate na khalu sarve eva āgamaḥ sambhāvya vipralambhaḥ vipralambha hetūnām doṣāṇām puruṣa āśrayāt apauruṣeyam satya artham iti eke kāraṇa abhāvaḥ hi kārya abhāvam sādhayati iti yaḥ evaṃvādinaḥ tān eva prati girām satya artha hetūnām guṇānām puruṣa āśrayāt apauruṣeyam mithyā artham kim naḥ iti anye pracakṣate 
[112,16]	yathā rāga ādi parītaḥ puruṣaḥ mṛṣāvādī dṛṣṭaḥ tathā dayā dharma tā ādi yuktaḥ satya vāc tat yathā vacanasya puruṣa āśrayāt mithyā artha tā tathā satya artha tāḥ api iti sa nivartamānaḥ tām api nivartayati iti ānarthakyam syāt viparyayaḥ vā na hi śabdāḥ prakṛtyāḥ arthavantaḥ samayāt tatas artha khyāteḥ kāya saṃjñā ādi vat aprātikūlyam tu yogya tā samaye tad icchā praṇayanāt nisarga siddheṣu icchā vaśāt pratipādana ayogāt te anarthakāḥ puruṣa saṃskārāt arthavantaḥ syuḥ tad saṃskāryatā eva ca eṣām pauruṣeya tā yuktā naḥ utpattiḥ tatas eva artha vipralambhāt utpannaḥ api anyathā samitaḥ naḥ uparodhī tad anya puruṣa dharma vat tat ayam nivartamānaḥ sva kṛta samaya sambhavām artha pratibhām nivartayati tat kutas tad nivṛttyā satya artha tā atha punar utpattiḥ eva pauruṣeya tā na samaya ākhyānam 
[113,02_113,04]	artha jñāpana hetuḥ hi saṃketaḥ puruṣa āśrayaḥ girām apauruṣeya tve api atas mithyātva sambhavaḥ kim hi asya apauruṣeya tayā yatas hi samayāt artha pratipattiḥ sa pauruṣeyaḥ vitathaḥ api syāt śīla sādhana svarga vacanam tat anyathā samayena viparyāsayet tena ayathārtham api prakāśana sambhavāt saḥ eva doṣaḥ 
[113,08_113,13]	sambandha apauruṣeya tve syāt pratītiḥ asaṃvidaḥ syāt etat akārya sambandhāḥ eva śabdāḥ na te artheṣu puruṣaiḥ anyathā viparyasyante tena adoṣaḥ iti kim idānīm saṃketena sa hi sambandhaḥ yatas artha pratītiḥ sa ced apauruṣeyaḥ na ayam samayam apekṣeta apratīti āśrayaḥ vā katham sambandhaḥ saṃketāt tad abhivyaktau asamartha ani akalpanā 
[113,14^1]	na vai sambandhaḥ vidyamānaḥ api anabhivyaktaḥ pratīti hetuḥ saṃketaḥ tu enam abhivyanakti sa tarhi siddha upasthāyī kim akāraṇam poṣyate nanu iyān sambandhasya vyāpāraḥ yat artha pratīti jananam tat samayena eva kṛtam iti na ayogye samayaḥ samarthaḥ iti yogyatā tad sambandhaḥ ced tat kim vai śabdaḥ sambandhaḥ astu samartham hi rūpam śabdasya yogyatā kārya kāraṇa yogya tāvat sā ced artha antaram kim śabdasya iti sambandhaḥ vācyaḥ yogyatā upakāraḥ iti ced na nityāyāḥ niratiśaya tvāt tatra api atiprasaṅgāt upakāra asiddheḥ 
[113,14^2]	yogyatāyām ca svatas yogya tve arthaḥ eva kim naḥ iṣyate samayaḥ tarhi katham śabda artha sambandhāḥ puruṣeṣu vṛtteḥ na amiśrāṇām siddhānām kaścid sambandhaḥ abheda prasaṅgāt anapekṣaṇāt ca artha viśeṣa samīhā preritā vāc atas idam iti viduṣaḥ sva nidāna ābhāsinam artham sūcayati iti buddhi rūpa vāc vijñaptyoḥ janya janaka bhāvaḥ sambandhaḥ tatas śabdāt pratipattiḥ avinā abhāvāt tad ākhyānam samayaḥ tatas pratyāyaka sambandha siddheḥ sambandha ākhyānāt na tu saḥ eva sambandhaḥ astu vai anyaḥ eva nityaḥ sambandhaḥ tena
[114,05_114,10]	girām eka artha niyame na syāt artha antare gatiḥ na hi tena sambandhena asambaddhe arthe pratītiḥ yuktā tasya vaiphalya prasaṅgāt dṛṣṭaḥ ca icchā vaśāt kṛta samayaḥ sarvaḥ sarvasya dīpakaḥ aneka artha abhisambandhe viruddha vyakti sambhavaḥ atha mā bhūt dṛṣṭa virodhaḥ iti sarve sarvasya vācakāḥ tathā na sarvaḥ sarva sādhanaḥ asaṃkarāt kārya kāraṇa tāyāḥ tatra pratiniyata sādhane abhimate arthe sarva sādhya sādhana sādhāraṇasya śabdasya iṣṭa vyaktim eva samaya kāraḥ karoti iti kutas etat saḥ aniyataḥ niyamam puruṣāt pratipadyate tadā 
[114,15_114,16]	apauruṣeya tāyāḥ ca vyarthā syāt parikalpanā api nāma asaṃkīrṇam artham jānīyām iti saṃkara hetuḥ puruṣa upākīrṇaḥ tatra yādṛśāḥ puruṣaiḥ kvacid prayuktāḥ saṃkīryante tādṛśāḥ eva sarva sādhāraṇāḥ santaḥ kvacid taiḥ viniyamitāḥ tattva aparijñānāt prakṛtyāḥ eva vaidikāḥ niyatāḥ iti ced na upadeśam apekṣeran na anyathā saṃketena prakāśayeyuḥ vyākhyā vikalpaḥ ca na syāt upadeśasya ca iṣṭa saṃvādaḥ śakya vikalpe na asti iti vyarthāḥ eva apauruṣeya tā 
[114,23_115,03]	vācyaḥ ca hetuḥ bhinnānām sambandhasya vyavasthiteḥ arthāḥ hi bāhyāḥ na rūpam śabdasya na śabdaḥ arthānām yena abhinna ātma tayā vyavasthā bhede api na antarīyaka tā syāt kṛtaka tva anitya tva vat na api ete vivakṣā janmānaḥ dhvanayaḥ ajanmānaḥ vā vivakṣā vyaṅgyāḥ na artha āyattāḥ tatas katham idānīm tad pratiniyama saṃsādhyam tat anvayam sādhayeyuḥ na hi apratibaddhaḥ tad sādhanaḥ iti asaṃskārya tayā pumbhiḥ sarvathā syāt nirarthatā saṃskāra upagame mukhyam gaja snānam idam bhavet 
[115,05_115,13]	iti saṃgrahaślokaḥ api ca śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ nityaḥ vā syāt anityaḥ vā yadi anityaḥ puruṣa icchā vṛttiḥ avṛttiḥ vā apuruṣa adhīna tve puruṣāṇām yathā abhiprāyam deśa ādi parāvṛttyā tena pratipādanam na syāt icchāyām api anāyattasya kadācid ayogāt parvata ādi vat ayam eva nitya tve api doṣaḥ tasya sthira rūpasya parāvṛttyayogāt iti samam sarva avasthāne api iṣṭa pratiniyama abhāvāt tatas viśeṣa pratipattiḥ na syāt iti pūrvavat prasaṅgaḥ icchā vṛttau ca pauruṣeya tvam iti vipralambha āśaṅkā api ca sambandhinām anitya tvāt na sambandhe asti nityatā 
[115,14]	para āśrayaḥ hi sambandhaḥ apratibandhe tayoḥ sambandhitā ayogāt sa ca āśrayaḥ anityaḥ apāye asya sambandhasya api apāyaḥ anyathā anāśritaḥ syāt tatas na nityaḥ tad āśraya arthaḥ ca vaktavyaḥ nityasya anupakārya tvāt anupakurvāṇaḥ ca anāśrayaḥ jāteḥ vācya tvāt adoṣaḥ iti ced na tad vacane prayojana abhāvāt iti nirloṭhitam etat sarvatra ca jāti a sambhavāt ayogaḥ yādṛt chikeṣu vyakti vāciṣu sarvadā jāti codane viśeṣa antara vyudāsena pravṛtti ayogāt ca tasmāt anvaya vyatirekiṇaḥ bhāvasya bhāva abhāvau sambandhaḥ 
[115,23_116,08]	arthaiḥ atas sa śabdānām saṃskāryaḥ puruṣaiḥ dhiyā tau eva bhāva abhāvau āśritya asaṃsṛṣṭau api saṃsṛṣṭau iva puruṣasya vyavahāra bhāvanātaḥ pratibhātaḥ iti pauruṣeyaḥ bhāvānām saṃśleṣaḥ kim ca āśraya vināśāt naṣṭe sambandhe sa śabdaḥ punar asambandha tvāt na apūrveṇa yojyeta utpanna utpannāḥ ca bhāvāḥ sthita sambandha abhāvāt asambandhinaḥ avācyāḥ syuḥ tatra api arthaiḥ eva saha utpāde kalpyamāne na svabhāva viparyayaḥ śabdeṣu yuktaḥ 
[116,10]	atha mā bhūt naṣṭa sambandhasya śabdasya artha antare vaiguṇyam arthānām ca avācya tā iti utpannaḥ arthaḥ sambandhavān yadi utpadyeta sa sambandhaḥ utpannaḥ api na śabde syāt tasya tena asambandhi svabhāvasya svabhāva viparyayam antareṇa tad bhāva ayogāt arthena saha utpannasya anyatas siddhasya anupakāriṇi śabde asamāśrayāt ca tasya api tad utpatti sahakāri tve samarthasya nitya utpādana prasaṅgaḥ anapekṣa tvāt nityasya anupakārāt asāmarthye api paścāt api svabhāva atyāgāt aśaktiḥ 
[116,18_116,19]	 sambandhe na ayam doṣaḥ vikalpite na hi bhāva śleṣa apekṣī puruṣa bhāvanā pratibhāsī tad apekṣā lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ saḥ ayam nityānām api aparāvartayan svabhāvam kutaścid svayam utprekṣya ghaṭayet iti te api tathā syuḥ na ca cyavana dharmāṇaḥ yat uktam āśraya apāyena āśrita sambandha vināśāt anityaḥ saḥ iti tatra 
[116,24_117,01]	nitya tvāt āśraya apāye api anāśaḥ yadi jāti vat nityeṣu āśraya sāmarthyam kim yena iṣṭaḥ saḥ āśrayaḥ śrūyate etat nityā jātiḥ āśrayitā ca na api āśrayeṇa saha naśyati iti kevalam nityeṣu āśraya sāmarthyam na paśyāmaḥ yena asau āśrayaḥ kṛtasya karaṇa abhāvāt akārakasya ca anapekṣa tvāt vyaktiḥ upakāraḥ jāteḥ sambandhasya ca āśrayāt tena āśrayaḥ iti ced jñāna utpādana hetūnām sambandhāt sahakāriṇām tad utpādana yogya tvena utpattiḥ vyaktiḥ iṣyate ghaṭa ādiṣu api yukti jñaiḥ aviśeṣe avikāriṇām vyañjakaiḥ svaiḥ kutas kaḥ arthaḥ vyaktāḥ taiḥ te yatas matāḥ 
[117,06_117,17]	sahakāriṇaḥ sakāśāt upādāna apekṣāt jñāna janana yogya kṣaṇa antara utpattiḥ eva ghaṭa ādīnām abhivyaktiḥ anyathā anapekṣya tad upakāram jñāna utpādana prasaṅgāt sāmarthya kāriṇaḥ ca janakatvāt tasya ca tad ātmaka tvāt artha antara tve ca bhāvān upakāra prasaṅgāt sāmarthyāt ca jñāna utpatteḥ nityam ghaṭa ādīnām agrahaṇa āpatteḥ anāloka apekṣa grahaṇa prasaṅgāt anapekṣa ātmā anupakārāt tat ime sva viṣaya jñāna janane param apekṣamāṇāḥ tatas svabhāva atiśayam svīkurvanti tena asya te janyāḥ jñeya rūpā sādhanāt tu jñāna vaśena kārya atiśaya vācinā śabdena viśeṣa khyāti artham vyaṅgyāḥ khyāpyante na evam jāti sambandha ādayaḥ kathaṃcid api anupakārya tvāt anupakāriṇā vyaktā yujyate sambandhasya ca vastu tve syāt bhedāt buddhi citra tā 
[117,18^1]	sa ca ayam sambandhaḥ vastu bhavat niyamena śabda arthābhyām bheda abhedau na ativartate rūpam hi vastu tasya atattvam eva anyat tvam iti uktam sa ca ayam aindriyaḥ san sva buddhau tad anya vivekinā pratibhāsamānaḥ rūpeṇa katham tathā syāt dṛśyau ivekā darśanayoḥ viveka sattā viparyaya āśraya tvāt anyathā tat sthiteḥ abhāva prasaṅgāt atīndriya tvāt apratibhāse api indriya ādiṣu iva adoṣaḥ iti ced na tatas apratipatti prasaṅgāt aprasiddhasya ajñāpaka tvāt saṃnidhi mātreṇa jñāpane avyutpannānām api syāt na anumānāt pratipattiḥ liṅga abhāvāt dṛṣṭānta asiddheḥ ca tatra api atīndriya tvena sādhana apekṣaṇāt tulyam indriya ādiṣu api iti ced na teṣām anyathā anumānāt jñānam hi keṣucid satsu vyatireka anvaya vat tanmātrā sambhavam tad vyatirikta apekṣām ca sādhayati tatas kārya dvāreṇa indriya siddhiḥ na evam sambandhasya tasya asiddhau tad kāryasya eva jñānasya abhāvāt 
[117,18^2]	na hi tatra śabda rūpam arthaḥ vā liṅgam tayoḥ sarvatra yogya tvāt viśeṣa pratīti samāśrayasya apratyāyanāt apratītiḥ asya na hi asati sambandha viśeṣe sā yuktā tasyām vā animittāyām tad viśeṣa pratīti niyama vat artha pratipādanam api śabdānām animittam kim naḥ iṣyate tasmāt tat sadṛśam liṅgam sarva sambandhe tatas aviśeṣeṇa gamayet tatas aviśeṣeṇa eva pratītiḥ syāt sarvasya ca tasmāt sambandha siddhi artha pratīteḥ na kaścid sampradāyam apekṣeta sampradāya sahitasya liṅga tvam iti ced tat kim anayā paraṃparayā saḥ eva sampradāya apekṣaḥ artha jñāpanam kim na karoti sa ca śabdaḥ yat abhiprāyaiḥ prayujyamānaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ anyathā na dṛṣṭaḥ darśana adarśanābhyām dhūma ādi vat tad pratītim janayati iti saḥ eva sambandhaḥ avinābhāva ākhyaḥ na ca atra anyasya sāmarthyam paśyāmaḥ na api siddhi upāyam atha punar na śabda arthayoḥ anyaḥ eva sambandhaḥ 
[118,20_119,01]	tābhyām abhede tau eva na atas anyā vastunaḥ gatiḥ rūpa bheda nibandhana tvāt vyavasthā antarasya tad rūpam tat eva syāt dharma bhedaḥ tu syāt pūrva ukta krameṇa sa ca aviruddhaḥ eva na vastu bhedaḥ na ca bheda abhedau muktvā vastunaḥ anyā gatiḥ tasya rūpa lakṣaṇa tvāt rūpasya ca etad vikalpa anati vṛtteḥ api ca bhinna tvāt vastu rūpasya sambandhaḥ kalpanā kṛtaḥ iti uktam prāk na hi śleṣa lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ aśliṣṭeṣu padārtheṣu sambhavati na ca artha antaram eṣām sambandhaḥ yasmāt sat dravyam syāt para adhīnam sambandhaḥ anyasya vā katham 
[119,03_119,10]	na hi siddham sat param apekṣate na anapekṣaḥ svatantraḥ sambandhaḥ dravyam iti ca svabhāvaḥ ucyate sa katham para bhāvasya śleṣaḥ syāt na hi svabhāva antara sattayā anyaḥ śliṣṭaḥ nāma mā bhūt aśliṣṭena śliṣṭena tu syāt iti ced na tasya eva tābhyām śleṣa asiddheḥ saḥ eva asiddhaḥ yaḥ tau śleṣayet tat ayam atiprasaṅgaḥ yadi arthau artha antareṇa śliṣyataḥ viśeṣa abhāvāt kim ca varṇāḥ nirarthakāḥ santaḥ pada ādi parikalpitam avastuni katham vṛttiḥ sambandhasya asya vastunaḥ 
[119,12^1]	vācakaḥ hi vacana aṅgena tadvān syāt santaḥ api avācakāḥ varṇāḥ tat na teṣu vācya vācaka sambandhaḥ tad vṛttau sva rūpa hāni prasaṅgāt krama viśeṣeṇa vācakāḥ varṇāḥ iti ced na kramasya anartha antara tvena abhedaka tvāt tad rūpasya krama antare api aviśeṣāt tulyā syāt pratipattiḥ artha antara tvam api kramasya niṣetsyāmaḥ tat asati varṇānām vācaka tve pada ādi vācakam syāt tat ca na kiṃcid vyatireka avyatireka virodhāt tasmāt indriya vijñāna viśeṣa anubandhī sa bhāga vāsana upādāna vikalpa pratibhāsa vibhramaḥ padam vākyam ca eka avabhāsi mithyā eva eka aneka tva ayogāt na hi ekam anekayā buddhyā krameṇa grahaṇa ayogāt na ca tat ekayā grāhyam varṇa anukrama grahaṇāt eka varṇa grahaṇa kāle ca aneka buddhi vyatikramāt kṣaṇika tvāt buddhīnām kṣaṇasya eka paramāṇu vyatikrama kāla tvāt 
[119,12^2]	ādhikye vibhāgavataḥ paryavasāna ayogāt aneka aṇu vyatyaya nimeṣa tulya kāla tvāt antya varṇa parisamāpteḥ yathā anubhavam smaraṇāt smṛtiḥ api tad kāle eva anubhava smaraṇa anukramayoḥ viśeṣa anupalakṣaṇa tvāt ca na api anekam pada ādi abheda pratibhāsanāt buddheḥ tad aneka tvasya niṣetsyamāna tvāt ca tat na vastu tasya etad vikalpa anatikramāt vastu ca sambandhaḥ sa katham tad āśrayaḥ syāt āśrayanīyā yogāt anāśritaḥ hi evam syāt tathā ca asambandhaḥ tasmāt na svābhāvikaḥ śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ tad abhiprāyasya prayogāt utpannaḥ abhivyaktaḥ vā śabdaḥ tat avyabhicārī iti tattvam asya sambandhaḥ sā ca utpattiḥ abhivyaktiḥ vai avyabhicāra āśrayaḥ pauruṣeyī iti pauruṣeya eva sambandhaḥ tad dvāreṇa ca artha pratyāyane aniyamaḥ śabdānām iti apauruṣeya tve api saḥ eva vipralambhaḥ 
[120,08_120,12^1]	apauruṣeya tā api iṣṭā kartṝṇām asmṛteḥ kila yāḥ api iyam apauruṣeya tā veda vākyānām kartuḥ asmaraṇāt varṇyate santi asya api anuvaktāraḥ iti dhik vyāpakam tamaḥ tasya eva tāvat īdṛśam prajñā skhalitam katham vṛttam iti sa vismaya anukampam naḥ cetaḥ tat apare api anuvadanti iti nirdaya ākrānta bhuvanam dhik vyāpakam tamaḥ kaḥ prāṇinaḥ hita īpsā vipralabdhasya aparādhaḥ tathā hi smaranti saugatāḥ mantrāṇām kartṝn aṣṭaka ādīn hiraṇyagarbham ca kāṇādāḥ teṣām sa mithyāvādaḥ iti ced kaḥ idānīm evam pauruṣeyaḥ anyaḥ api kumāra sambhava ādiṣu ātmānam anyam vā praṇetāram upadiśantaḥ yat evam prativyūhyeran tatra prativahane abhyupeta bādhāḥ iti ced nanu idam eva abhyupagama aṅgam iti kasya bādhā tat parasya api tulyam eva tasya iṣṭa tvāt adoṣaḥ iti ced 
[120,12^2]	kutas asya iyam iṣṭiḥ apramāṇikā prāk āsīt akasmāt grāhī ca ayam kim punar kvacid sādhanam apekṣate yat pauruṣeya apauruṣeya cintayā ātmānam āyāsayati tatas eva iṣṭeḥ anabhyupeta bādhāyām tad anyasya api tulyam iti anupālambhaḥ anatiśaya darśī ca ayam vākyeṣu evaṃprakārāṇām apauruṣeya tva sādhanānām kārya dharmāṇām vā kvacid atiśayam abhyupetaḥ iti apratyayaḥ eva asya vṛttiḥ dṛśyante ca vicchinna kriyā sampradāyāḥ kṛtakāḥ ca tān yatnavantaḥ upalabhante iti ced na niyama abhāvāt anyatra anupalambhasya upalambhasya vā para upadeśāt apratyayāt aniścaya artha tvāt svayaṃkṛtānām api apahnotṛ darśanāt niṣṭhā gamanasya aśakya tvāt 
[121,07_121,11]	yathā ayam anyatas aśrutvā na imam varṇa pada kramam vaktum samarthaḥ puruṣaḥ tathā anyaḥ api iti kaścana tasya api tat eva uttaram evam apauruṣeya tve api kim idānīm pauruṣeyam iti ādi tathā hi anyaḥ vā racitaḥ granthaḥ sampradāyāt ṛte paraiḥ dṛṣṭaḥ kaḥ abhihitaḥ yena saḥ api evam na anumīyate 
[121,13_121,18]	na khalu kiṃcid anyat apauruṣeya tva āśrayaḥ anyatra idānīntanānām anupadeśa pāṭhā śakteḥ sā ca anyatra api ekena racite granthe anyasya tulyā tad anusāriṇā sarvaḥ tathā unneyaḥ na vā kaścid tasya tathā aniṣṭa tvāt iti ādau api uktam iṣṭeḥ tad āśraya tvāt iti ādi api ca yat jātīyaḥ yatas siddhaḥ sa tasmāt agni kāṣṭha vat adṛṣṭa hetuḥ anyaḥ api aviśiṣṭaḥ sampratīyate 
[121,20_122,01]	na adarśanāt hetuḥ ahetukaḥ nāma adṛṣṭa hetavaḥ api hi bhāvāḥ tad anyaiḥ svabhāva abhedam anubhavantaḥ tathāvidhāḥ samunnīyante hetu rūpa nivṛttau api tad rūpam anivṛttam kārya dharma vyatikramāt na tatas syāt iti na kaścid tathā vacanīyaḥ rūpa viśeṣaḥ vā tathā darśanīyaḥ yaḥ enam hetum anuvidadhyāt yena iṣṭa aniṣṭayoḥ iṣṭa viparyayaḥ na syāt svabhāva nivṛtteḥ ca hetoḥ abhedane bhāvānām bhedaḥ syāt ākasmikaḥ iti na kvacid vinivarteta tasmāt yaḥ svabhāvaḥ yat janmā dṛṣṭaḥ saḥ anyatra api avibhajyamānaḥ sva ātmanā tad kārya dharma tām na ativartate agni in dhana vat tatra apradarśya ye bhedam kārya sāmānya darśanāt hetavaḥ pravitanyante sarve te vyabhicāriṇaḥ 
[122,03^1]	yathā ādyaḥ api pathika kṛtaḥ agniḥ jvālā antara pūrvakaḥ na araṇi nirmathana pūrvakaḥ pathika agni tvāt anantara agni vat iti katham punar pathika agneḥ vyabhicāraḥ jvālodbhava sāmarthyam hi āśritya dahanasya hetu antaram pratikṣipyate yadi hi vinā jvālayā syāt anyatra api syāt iti tatra jvālā itara janmanoḥ abādhya bādhaka tve jvālā prabhava tvam anyathā api syāt iti dharmayoḥ ekatra arthe sambhavāt sa pathika agniḥ anyaḥ vai arthaḥ eka pratiniyataḥ na syāt iti āśaṅkyate vyabhicāraḥ saḥ api anyonya vyatirekī dharma dvaya avatāraḥ vastu sāmānye aviruddhaḥ iti ucyate na avasthā bhedini viśeṣe niṣkalasya ātmanaḥ tad atattva virodhāt na ca jvālā itara janmanoḥ bādhya bādhaka tā pathika agnau tasya jvālā prabhava vyatirekeṇa asambhava abhāvāt evaṃbhūtaḥ pathika agniḥ jvālā prabhavaḥ iti syāt 
[122,03^2]	na sarvaḥ tatra viśeṣa pratikṣepasya kartum aśakya tvāt sambhavat viśeṣasya ca tādavasthya aniyamāt yat api vinā jvālayā syāt anyatra api syāt iti bhavati eva yayā sāmagryā sambhavati sā yadi syāt asyāḥ sambhavam pradarśya tad abhāvam pradarśayet tatra vā jvālām syāt etat tasmāt naḥ ekasya parapūrvakam adhyayanam sarvasya tathā abhāvam sādhayati tasya anyathā asambhava abhāvāt tathāvidhasya tu tad kriyā pratibhā ra hitasya tathā syāt iti tathābhūtam evam vācyam syāt tat aviśeṣeṇa sambhavat viśeṣam ucyamānam chāyām na puṣṇāti katham viśeṣasya sambhavaḥ yāvatā teṣām api puruṣāṇām aśaktiḥ eva idānīntana puruṣa vat atra api śakti puruṣayoḥ na kiṃcid virodha darśanam iti na aviruddha vidhiḥ anupalabdhi prayogaḥ gamakaḥ 
[122,03^3]	na hi atīndriyeṣu virodha gatiḥ asti iti uktam na ca ayam pūrva prayogāt bhidyate yadi puruṣāḥ śaktāḥ syuḥ idānīntanāḥ api iti viśeṣa asambhavaḥ etat syāt sa ca duḥsādhaḥ yatra ekasya aśaktiḥ tatra sarva puruṣāṇām iti api pūrvavat vyabhicāri bhārata ādiṣu idānīntanānām aśaktau api kasyacid śakti siddheḥ tasmāt kāraṇāni vivecayata artheṣu api tad atad pratibhaveṣu svabhāva bhedaḥ darśanīyaḥ tad abhāve sarvaḥ tad ātmā na vā kaścid na ca atra laukika vaidikayoḥ svabhāva bhedam paśyāmaḥ asati tasmin tayoḥ sāmānyasya eva dṛṣṭeḥ ekasya kaścid dharmam vivecayan tad svabhāva sambhavinā tena āśaṅkya vyabhicāra vādaḥ kriyate nanu veda avedayoḥ tattva lakṣaṇaḥ asti eva viśeṣaḥ satyam asti na kevalam tayoḥ eva 
[122,03^4]	kim tarhi ḍiṇḍikapurāṇa itarayoḥ api na ca sva prakriyā bheda dīpanaḥ nāma bhedaḥ puruṣa kṛtim bādhate anyatra api prasaṅgāt yadi tādṛśīm racanām puruṣāḥ kartum na śaknuyuḥ kṛtām vā akṛta saṃketaḥ vivecayet vyaktam apauruṣeyaḥ vedaḥ nanu na śaknuvanti eva puruṣāḥ mantrān kartum etat uttaratra vicārayiṣyāmaḥ api ca na mantraḥ nāma anyat eva kiṃcid kim tarhi satya tapaḥ prabhāvavatām samīhita artha sādhanam vacanam tat adya tve api puruṣeṣu dṛśyate eva yathāsvam satya adhiṣṭhāna balāḥ viṣa dahana ādi stambhana darśanāt śabarāṇām ca keṣāṃcid adya api mantra karaṇāt avaidikānām ca bauddha ādīnām mantra kalpānām darśanāt teṣām ca puruṣa kṛteḥ tatra api apauruṣeya tve katham idānīm apauruṣeyam avitatham 
[122,03^5]	tathā hi bauddha itarayoḥ mantra kalpayoḥ hiṃsā maithuna ātma darśana ādayaḥ anabhyudaya hetavaḥ anyathā ca varṇyate tat katham ekatra viruddha abhidhāyi dvayam satyam syāt tatra artha antara kalpane tat anyatra api tulyam iti artha anirṇayāt kvacid apratipattiḥ tathā ca sat api anupayogam apauruṣeyam bauddha ādīnām amantra tve tat anyatra api koṣa pānam syāt karaṇīyam viṣa karma adhikṛtaḥ bauddhāḥ api dṛśyante tatra amantra tvam api vipratiṣiddham mudrā maṇḍala dhyānaiḥ api anakṣaraiḥ karmāṇi kriyante na ca tāni apauruṣeyāṇi nityāni yujyate teṣām kriyā sambhave akṣara racanāyām kaḥ pratighātaḥ puruṣāṇām tasmāt na kiṃcid aśakya kriyam eṣām katham idānīm satya prabhavau mantra kalpau paraspara virodhinau na vai sarvatra tau satya prabhavau 
[122,03^6]	prabhāva yukta puruṣa pratijñā lakṣaṇau api tau staḥ sa prabhāvaḥ gati siddhi viśeṣābhyām api syāt yadi pauruṣeyāḥ mantrāḥ kim na sarve puruṣāḥ mantra kāriṇaḥ tad kriyā sādhana vaikalyāt yadi tādṛśaiḥ satya tapaḥ prabhṛtibhiḥ yuktāḥ syuḥ kurvanti eva api ca kāvyāni puruṣaḥ karoti iti sarvaḥ puruṣaḥ kāvya kṛt syāt akaraṇe vā naḥ eva kaścid tadvat iti apūrvā eṣā vācoyuktiḥ satyam mantra kriyā sādhana vikalāḥ mantrān na kurvate tat tu kasyacid sākalyam na paśyāmaḥ puruṣāṇām samāna dharma tvāt uktam atra na mantraḥ nāma anyat eva kiṃcid satya ādimatām vacana samayāt iti tāni ca kvacid puruṣeṣu dṛśyante sarva puruṣāḥ tad rahitāḥ iti api tad sambhava virodha abhāvāt anirṇayaḥ na ca atyakṣa svabhāveṣu anupalabdhiḥ niścaya hetuḥ 
[122,03^7]	na ca smṛti mati prativedha satya śaktayaḥ sarva bhāvinyaḥ tad sādhana sampradāya bheda vat guṇa antara sādhanāni api syuḥ na api san api sarvaḥ draṣṭum śakyaḥ atas eva adṛṣṭasya anapahnavaḥ na api puruṣeṣu utpitsoḥ kasyacid guṇasya pratiroddhā bādhya adṛṣṭeḥ bādhya bādhaka bhāva asiddheḥ etena sarva jñāna pratiṣedha ādayaḥ api nirvarṇita uttarāḥ tatra api evaṃbhūtaḥ yādṛśaḥ ayam asambhavat tad sādhana sampradāyaḥ naḥ iti nyāyaḥ na adṛṣṭa jñāpakaḥ atad svabhāvaḥ iti api satām api kārya anārambha sambhavāt svabhāva vipra karṣeṇa draṣṭum aśakya tvāt ca tasmāt adhyayanam adhyayana antara pūrvakam adhyayanāt iti bhārata adhyayane api bhāvāt vyabhicāri nanu vedane viśeṣaṇāt adoṣaḥ kaḥ punar atiśayaḥ veda adhyayanasya yat anyathā adhyetum na śakyate 
[122,03^8]	na hi viśeṣaṇam aviruddham vipakṣeṇa asmāt hetum vyāvartayati aviruddhayoḥ ekatra sambhavāt idānīntanānām adhyayanāt iti ced ukta uttaram etat adarśanāt iti ced idam api prativyūḍham na api adarśana mātram abhāvam gamayati iti vyabhicāraḥ eva tasmāt na viśeṣaṇam atiśaya bhāj iti anupātta samam yat kiṃcid veda adhyayanam sarvam tad adhyayana antara pūrvakam iti api vyāptiḥ na sidhyati sarvasya tathā abhāva asiddheḥ yādṛśam tu tad nimittam dṛṣṭam tat tathā iti syāt dṛṣṭe viśeṣe tad nimitta tayā tad tyāgena sāmānya grahaṇam vyabhicāri eva hutāśana saṃsiddhau pāṇḍu dravya tva vat etena vacana āt ayaḥ rāga ādi sādhane pratyuktāḥ astu vedam adhyayanam adhyayana pūrva tā sādhanam 
[125,11_125,21]	sarvathā anāditā sidhyet evam na apuruṣa āśrayaḥ tasmāt apauruṣeya tve syāt anyaḥ api anarāśrayaḥ puruṣaḥ eva hi svayam abhyūhya paratas vā ādhīyate na eṣām avyāpṛta karaṇānām svayam śabdāḥ dhvananti yena apauruṣeyāḥ syuḥ api syuḥ apauruṣeyāḥ yadi puruṣāṇām ādiḥ syāt tadā api anya pūrvakam na sidhyati adhyāpayituḥ abhāvāt tat prathamaḥ adhyetā kartā eva syāt tat ayam anādiḥ pūrva pūrva darśana pravṛttaḥ ḍimbhakapāṃsu krīḍā ādi vat puruṣa vyavahāraḥ iti syāt na apauruṣeyaḥ iti anādi tvāt apauruṣeya tve bahutaram idānīm apauruṣeyam tathā hi mleccha ādi vyavahārāṇām nāstikya vacasām api anādi tvāt tathā abhāvaḥ pūrva saṃskāra santateḥ 
[125,23]	mleccha vyavahārāḥ api kecid mātṛ vivāha ādayaḥ madana utsava ādayaḥ ca anādayaḥ nāstikya vacāṃsi ca apūrva para loka ādi apava ādīni na hi tāni anāhita saṃskārāḥ paraiḥ pravartayanti sva pratibhā ra cita samayānām api yathā aśruta artha vikalpa saṃhāreṇa eva pravṛtteḥ tat kiṃcid kutaścid āgatam iti ekasya upadeṣṭuḥ prabandhena abhāvāt apara pūrvakam iti ucyate prāk eva yathā darśana pravṛttayaḥ samyak mithyā pravṛttayaḥ loka vyavahārāḥ nanu ādi kalpikeṣu adṛṣṭāḥ eva vyavahārāḥ paścāt pravṛttāḥ iṣyante na teṣām api anya saṃskāra āhitānām yathāpratyayam prabodhāt bhavatu sarveṣām apauruṣeya tvam iti ced tādṛśe apauruṣeya tve kaḥ siddhe api guṇaḥ bhavet kāmam avisaṃvādakam iti apauruṣeya tvam iṣṭam tat visaṃvādakānām api keṣāṃcid anādi tvāt asti iti kim apauruṣeya tvena 
[126,06_126,08]	sati vā veda vākyānām eva apauruṣeya tve artha saṃskāra bhedānām darśanāt saṃśayaḥ punar yadi apauruṣeya tve api pratiniyatām eva tad artha pratibhām janayet āśvāsanam syāt yatheṣṭam tu samāropa apavādābhyām nairukta mīmāṃsaka ādayaḥ veda vākyāni viśasantaḥ dṛśyante na ca te arthāḥ teṣām na saṃghaṭante samaya prādhānyāt artha niveśasya ekasya api vākyasya aneka vikalpa sambhavāt prakṛti pratyayānām aneka artha pāṭhāt rūḍheḥ api ekāntena ananumateḥ arūḍha śabda bāhulyāt tad arthasya puruṣa upadeśa apekṣaṇāt tad upadeśasya tad icchā anuvṛtteḥ anirṇayaḥ eva veda vākya artheṣu api ca ayam apauruṣeya tvam sādhayan varṇānām vā sādhayet vākyasya vā tatra 
[126,18_127,01]	anya aviśeṣāt varṇānām sādhane kim phalam bhavet na hi loka vedayoḥ nānā varṇāḥ bhede api ca pratyabhijñāna aviśeṣāt tatas ekatva asiddhi prasaṅgāt bheda anupalakṣaṇāt ca vaidika varṇa asiddhiḥ pratyabhijñānāt apratipatti prasaṅgāt anabhyupagamāt ca teṣām ca apauruṣeya tva sādhane te tulyāḥ sarvatra iti kim anena pariśeṣitam tathā ca sarvaḥ vyavahāraḥ apauruṣeyaḥ na ca sarvaḥ avitathaḥ iti vyarthaḥ pariśramaḥ atha vākyam apauruṣeyam iṣṭam vākyam na bhinnam varṇebhyaḥ vidyate anupalambhanāt 
[127,03]	na hi vayam devadatta ādi pada vākyeṣu dakāra ādi pratibhāsam muktvā anyam pratibhāsam buddheḥ paśyāmaḥ dvitīya varṇa pratibhāsa vat na ca apratibhāsamānam grahaṇe grāhya tayā iṣṭam asti anyat vā iti śakyam avasātum ākāra antara vat anyāsambhavi kāryam gamakam iti ced syāt etat yadi teṣu varṇeṣu satsu api tat kāryam na syāt na bhavati teṣām aviśeṣe api pada vākya antare abhāvāt iti ced na teṣām aviśeṣa asiddheḥ aviśeṣaḥ pratyabhijñānāt siddhaḥ iti ced na tasya vyabhicārāt anidarśana tvāt ca varṇa aviśeṣe api vākya bhedāt pratipatti bhedaḥ kārya bhedaḥ syāt sā ca vākyāt tat ca atīndriyam iti kutas syāt saṃnidhāna mātreṇa janane avyutpannasya api syāt tasmāt na vākyam nāma kiṃcid artha antaram varṇebhyaḥ yasya apauruṣeya tvam sādhyeta tad abhāvāt veda aviśiṣṭa varṇā pauruṣeya tvam api prathama pakṣe pratyuktam api ca astu artha antaram vākyam tat aneka avayava ātmakam vā syāt anavayavam vā 
[127,18_127,21]	aneka avayava ātma tve pṛthak teṣām nirarthatā te api tasya bahavaḥ avayavāḥ pṛthak prakṛtyāḥ yadi anarthakāḥ atad rūpe ca tādrūpyam kalpitam siṃhatā ādi vat arthavān eva ātmā vākyam te ca avayavāḥ svayam anarthakāḥ teṣu saḥ ātmā kalpanā samāropitaḥ syāt siṃhatā ādi vat māṇavaka ādiṣu iti pauruṣeyaḥ eva atha mā bhūt eṣa doṣaḥ iti pratyekam te avayavāḥ sā arthakāḥ iṣyante 
[128,01_128,09]	pratyekam sā arthaka tve api mithyā aneka tva kalpanā eka avayava gatyā ca vākya artha pratipad bhavet parisamāpta artham hi śabda rūpam vākyam te ca avayavāḥ tathāvidhāḥ pṛthak pṛthak iti pratyekam te vākyam tathā ca na aneka avayavam vākyam eka avayava pratipattyā ca vākya artha pratipatteḥ avayava antara apekṣā kālakṣepaḥ ca na syāt tasya niṣkala ātmanaḥ kṣaṇena pratipatteḥ eka jñāna utpattau niḥśeṣa avagamāt anyathā ca ekatva virodhāt sakṛt śrutau ca sarveṣām kāla bhedaḥ na yujyate 
[128,10_128,23]	atha mā bhūt avayava antara apratīkṣaṇena ekasmāt eva avayavāt vākya artha siddheḥ aneka avayava tva hāniḥ vākyasya iti sakṛt sarva avayavānām śravaṇam iṣyate tadā api kāla kṣepaḥ na yuktaḥ eva eka avayava pratipatti kāle eva sarveṣām śravaṇāt krama śravaṇe ca pṛthak arthavatām ekasmāt eva tad artha siddheḥ anyasya vaiyarthyāt sakṛt śrutau ca pṛthak artheṣu adṛṣṭa sāmarthyānām arthavat tā ca na sidhyati sahiteṣu artha darśanāt adoṣaḥ na pṛthak asataḥ rūpasya saṃghāte api asambhavāt artha antara anutpatteḥ ca śabda utpāda vādinaḥ tāvat ayam adoṣaḥ eva pṛthak asamarthānām api avayavānām upakāra viśeṣāt atiśayavatām kārya viśeṣa upayogāt pratyekam tu avayaveṣu samartheṣu vyarthā syāt anya kalpanā atha punar ekam eva anavayavam vākyam tatra eka tve api hi abhinnasya kramaśas gati asambhavāt 
[128,24^1]	kāla bhedaḥ eva na yujyate na hi ekasya krameṇa pratipattiḥ yuktā gṛhīta agṛhītayoḥ abhedāt krameṇa ca vākya pratipattiḥ dṛṣṭā sarva vākya vyāhāra śravaṇa smaraṇa kālasya aneka kṣaṇa nimeṣa anukrama parisamāpteḥ varṇa rūpa asaṃsparśinaḥ ca ekabuddhi pratibhāsinaḥ śabda ātmanaḥ apratibhāsanāt varṇa anukrama pratīteḥ tad aviśeṣe api anukrama kṛta tvāt vākya bhedasya anukramavatī vākya pratītiḥ varṇa anukrama upakāra anapekṣaṇe taiḥ yathā kathaṃcid prayuktaiḥ api yat kiṃcid vākyam pratīyeta vinā vā varṇaiḥ taiḥ anukramavadbhiḥ akramasya upakāra ayogāt akrameṇa ca vyāhartum aśakya tvāt gati antara abhāvāt ca na eva vākye varṇāḥ santi tat ekam eva śabda rūpam vyañjaka anukrama vaśāt anukrama vat varṇa vibhāga vat ca pratibhāti iti ced anukramavatā vyañjakena akramasya vyaktiḥ pratyuktā 
[128,24^2]	vyakta avyakta virodhāt avarṇa bhāge ca vākye asakala śrāviṇaḥ asakala vākya gatiḥ na syāt ekasya śakala abhāvāt sakala śrutiḥ na vā kasyacid samasta varṇa saṃskāravatyā antyayā buddhyā vākya avadhāraṇam iti api mithyā tasya avarṇa rūpa saṃsparśinaḥ kasyacid kadācid apratipatteḥ varṇānām ca akrameṇa apratipatteḥ kutas akramam eka buddhi grāhyam vākyam nāma na ca antya varṇa pratipatteḥ ūrdhvam anyam aśakalam śabda ātmānam upalakṣayāmaḥ na api svayam ayam vaktā vibhāvayati kevalam evam yadi syāt sādhu me syāt iti kalyāṇa kāma tā mūḍha matiḥ antyāyām buddhau samāpta kalaḥ śabdaḥ bhāti iti svapnāyate na hi smaryamāṇāyoḥ api pada vākyayoḥ varṇāḥ krama viśeṣam antareṇa vibhāvyante akramāyām buddhau paurvāparya abhāvāt teṣām tad kṛtaḥ pada vākya bhedānām bhedaḥ na syāt na api avarṇa kramam anyat śabda rūpam paśyāmaḥ iti uktam sati vā tat anityam vā syāt nityam vā yadi 
[129,23_130,02]	anityam yatna sambhūtam pauruṣeyam katham na tat avaśyam hi anityam utpattimat kutaścid bhavati tathā hi ākasmika tve sattvasya deśa ādi niyamaḥ na syāt iti uktam tat ca yatna prerita aviguṇa karaṇānām dṛṣṭam anyathā naḥ iti kāraṇa dharma darśanāt puruṣa vyāpāraḥ eva kāraṇam atas pauruṣeyam syāt nitya upalabdhiḥ nitya tve api anāvaraṇa sambhavāt 
[130,03^1]	atha tat śabda rūpam nityam syāt upalabhya svabhāvam ca sa ca tasya svabhāvaḥ kadācid na apaiti iti nityam upalabhyeta evam hi sa nityaḥ syāt yadi na kutaścid sāmarthyāt pracyavet jñāna janana sāmarthyasya tad ātmaka tvāt artha antara tvasya ca prāk eva niṣiddha tvāt na api tasya upalabhya ātmanaḥ kiṃcid upalambha āvaraṇam sambhavati tasya sataḥ api tad ātmanam akhaṇḍayataḥ sāmarthya tiraskārā yogāt na hi tatra atiśayam anutpādayan kiṃcitkaraḥ nāma akiṃcitkaraḥ ca kaḥ kasya āvaraṇam anyat vā iti nirloṭhita prāyam etat 
[130,03^2]	kuḍya ādayaḥ ghaṭa ādīnām kam atiśayam utpādayanti khaṇḍayanti vā yena āvaraṇam iṣyante na brūmaḥ te kaṃcid atiśāyayanti iti api tu na sarve ghaṭa kṣaṇāḥ sarvasya indriya vijñāna hetavaḥ paraspara sahitāḥ tu viṣaya indriya ālokāḥ parasparataḥ viśiṣṭa kṣaṇa antara utpādāt vijñāna hetavaḥ anupakāryasya apekṣā yogāt śakta svabhāvasya nityam jananam ajananam vā anyasya sarvadā syāt iti uktam te ca avyavahitāḥ pratighātinā anyena anyonyasya upakāriṇaḥ avyavadhāna deśa yogya tā sahakāri tvāt teṣām anyonya atiśaya utpatteḥ vyavadhāne tu hetu abhāvāt samartha kṣaṇa antara anutpatteḥ jñāna anutpattiḥ 
[130,03^3]	tasmāt pūrva utpanna samartha nirodhāt sati kuḍye anyasya utpitsoḥ kāraṇa abhāvena anutpatteḥ kāraṇa vaikalyāt jñāna anutpattiḥ iti kuḍya ādayaḥ āvaraṇam ucyante na prāk yogyasya pratibandhāt tasya svabhāvāt apracyuteḥ athavā sambhavati api bhāvānām kṣaṇikānām anyonya upakāraḥ acintya tvāt hetu pratyaya sāmarthyasya asarva vidā tena yat indriya viṣaya madhya sthitam āvaraṇam tat tau vijñāna utpatti vaiguṇya tāratamya bhedena atiśayayet api āvaraṇa bhede na śabda ādau śruti māndya pāṭava darśanāt anyathā kvacid api akiṃcitkarasya saṃnidhānasya api asaṃnidhāna tulya tvāt tasya idam iti 
[130,03^4]	upasaṃhāraḥ vikalpa nirmitaḥ eva syāt na vastu āśrayaḥ na ca samāropa anuvidhāyinaḥ artha kriyāḥ na hi māṇavakaḥ dahana upacārāt ādhīyate pāke tasmāt satyām api kalpanāyām atatparāvṛttayaḥ bhāvāḥ yathā svabhāva vṛttayaḥ eva syuḥ tat sati api āvaraṇe vijñāpayeyuḥ eva indriya ādayaḥ na ca tathā tasmāt tena ādheya viśeṣāḥ iti gamyante na khalu evam nityānām śabdānām kasmiṃścid sati atiśaya hāniḥ utpattiḥ vā tat yadi teṣām jñāna jananaḥ svabhāvaḥ sarvasya sarvadā sarvāṇi sva viṣaya jñānāni sakṛt janayeyuḥ no ced na kadācid kasyacid kiṃcid iti ekāntaḥ eṣaḥ 
[131,11_131,15]	aśrutiḥ vikala tvāt ced kasyacid sahakāriṇaḥ syāt etat na āvaraṇāt nityam sarve śabdāḥ na śrūyante api tu kiṃcid teṣām pratipattau sahakāri pratiniyatam asti tat kadācid kasyacid bhavati iti tad kṛtam eṣām kadācid kvacid śravaṇam iti kāmam anya pratīkṣā astu niyamaḥ tu virudhyate 
[131,16]	na vai vayam kāraṇānām saha kārīṇi pratikṣipāmaḥ kim tu apekṣante eva kāraṇāni tad avasthā upakāriṇam tatas labhyasya atiśayasya kārya upayogāt tathā śabdaḥ api yadi kiṃcid apekṣya kāryam kuryāt karotu pūrva svabhāva niyate iti etat na syāt tasya pracyuteḥ apekṣyāt ca svabhāva antara pratilambhāt na hi anupakārī apekṣyate iti uktam etat tad upakārasya ca artha antara tve tasya iti sambandha abhāva ādayaḥ api uktāḥ tasya ca ajñeya tvam upakārāt eva jñāna utpatteḥ tasmāt eva śabdaḥ naḥ indriyam na saṃnikarṣam na ātmānam anyat vā kiṃcid jñāna utpatti samāśrayam sva vijñāna janane apekṣate sarvasya tatra akiṃcitkara tvāt api ca ete śabdāḥ vyāpinaḥ vā syuḥ avyāpinaḥ vā 
[131,27_131,28]	sarvatra anupalambhaḥ syāt teṣām avyāpitā yadi katham eka deśa vartitam tat śūnya deśa sthitaḥ upalabdheta aprāpta grahaṇa pakṣe adoṣaḥ iti ced na tatra api yogya deśa sthiti tāratamya apekṣaṇāt ayaskānta ādi vat anyathā spaṣṭa aspaṣṭa śruti bhedaḥ na syāt sati ca upalambha pratyaye sarvatra deśe tulyam upalabhyeran tasmāt na avyāpinaḥ 
[132,05_132,10]	sarveṣām upalambhaḥ syāt yugapad vyāpitā yadi na hi kaścid śabda kvacid na asti iti sarve yugapad upalabhyeran sarva deśa sthitaiḥ ca yogya indriya tvāt viṣaya saṃnidhānāt apratibandhāt ca saṃskṛtasya upalambhe ca kaḥ saṃskartā avikāriṇaḥ syāt etat san api na sarvaḥ śabdaḥ upalabhyate sarveṇa saṃskṛtasya saṃskṛtena eva upalambhāt iti tatra na saṃskṛtasya upalambhaḥ anādheya vikārasya saṃskāra ayogāt 
[132,13_132,17]	indriyasya hi saṃskāraḥ śṛṇuyāt nikhilam ca tat tatra yadi saṃskṛtena upalambhaḥ iti asaṃskṛtena indriyaḥ naḥ upalabhate yasya saṃskāraḥ indriyasya kṛtaḥ sa sarva śabdān yugapad śṛṇuyāt iti prasaṅgaḥ anivṛttaḥ eva saṃskāra bhedāt bhinna tvāt eka artha niyamaḥ yadi aneka śabda saṃghāte śrutiḥ kalakale katham 
[132,19]	atha api syāt pratiniyatāḥ te saṃskārāḥ śabdānām tatra kenacid saṃskṛtam indriyam kasyacid eva grāhakam iti na yugapad sarva śabda śrutiḥ iti saṃskāra viśeṣāt śruti niyame indriyāṇām aneka śabda saṃghātasya kalakalasya śrutiḥ na syāt na hi ekaḥ śabdaḥ kalakalaḥ nāma bhinna svabhāvānām yugapad śravaṇāt svabhāva bheda āśraya tvāt ca bheda vyavasthiteḥ laghu vṛtteḥ sakṛt śrutiḥ bhrāntiḥ iti ced vaṃśa ādi svara dhārāyām gamaka avayava saṃhārāt saṃkulā pratipattiḥ syāt vakṣyate ca atra pratiṣedhaḥ tasmāt eka gati śakti pratiniyamāt indriyasya aneka ātmā kalakalaḥ na śrūyeta 
[132,29_133,05]	dhvanayaḥ kevalam tatra śrūyante ced na vācakāḥ na vai kalakale varṇa pada vākyāni śrūyante dhvanīnām eva kevalānām śravaṇāt vācake ca pratiniyata śakti indriyam na dhvaniṣu tatra dhvanibhyaḥ bhinnam asti iti śraddhā iyam ati bahu idam na hi vayam dhvanim śabdam ca vācakam pṛthak rūpam upalakṣayāmaḥ ekam eva ekadā varṇa anukrama śravaṇe śabda ātmānam vyavasyāmaḥ tat katham vyavasāya pūrvakam vyavahāram avyavasyantaḥ pravartayāmaḥ tasmāt dhvani viśeṣaḥ eva iyam varṇa ādi ākhyaḥ api ca 
[133,10_133,20]	sthiteṣu anyeṣu śabdeṣu śrūyate vācakaḥ katham na dhvaniḥ atas bhinnaḥ tena saha pṛthak vā na hi pratyakṣe arthe para upadeśaḥ garīyān tat ayam sthiteṣu anyeṣu vyāhartṛṣu kevalam eva śabdam śṛṇvan tad upalambha pratyayānām tad anya niṣpādane sāmarthya abhāvam pratyeti yadi hi samarthāḥ syuḥ tad sādhitam tat upalabhyeta tad svabhāvāḥ eva punar pratyayāḥ katham kalakale artha antaram ārabheran na hi kāraṇa abhede kārya bhedaḥ yuktaḥ bhedasya ahetuka tva prasaṅgāt iti uktam na ca kalakale vācakaḥ na śrūyate pada vākya vicchedānām upalakṣaṇāt katham vā śakti niyamāt bhinna dhvani gatiḥ bhavet 
[133,21]	tāni pratiniyata śaktīni api indriyāṇi nānā rūpān prati śabda niyatān dhvanīn śṛṇvanti na tu evam śabdān iti kaḥ śabdeṣu eṣām nirvedaḥ yat uktam na dhvanayaḥ bhedena vācakebhyaḥ siddhāḥ iti katham na siddhāḥ vacanāt artha pratipatteḥ na hi dhvani bhāgāt alpīyasaḥ śabda artha pratītiḥ na ca saḥ anyam samaḥ iti tat iyam samasta pada vākya rūpa sādhya artha pratītiḥ asamasta bhāgeṣu dhvaniṣu na sambhavati iti siddham akrama sattvam śabda rūpam kramavat bhāgaḥ ca dhvaniḥ iti tat na akramasya kramavat vyatirekiṇaḥ prāk eva niṣiddha tvāt atiprasaṅgaḥ ca evam karma bhāgānām pūrveṇa aparasya apratisandhānāt eka aṃśāt ca apratipatteḥ tad vyatirekī hasta saṃjñā ādiṣu artha pratipatti hetuḥ samasta rūpaḥ karma ātmā abhyupagantavyaḥ syāt śabda vat eva krama bhāvinaḥ eva yathāsvam karaṇa prayogāt bhinnāḥ varṇa bhāgāḥ karma bhāgāḥ vā krameṇa vikalpa viṣayāḥ yathā saṃketam eva artha pratītim janayanti iti nyāyyam kim ca 
[134,14_134,16]	dhvanayaḥ sammatāḥ yaiḥ te doṣaiḥ kaiḥ api avācakāḥ dhvanibhiḥ vyajyamāne asmin vācake api katham na te krama utpādibhiḥ dhvani bhāgaiḥ vyaktaḥ kila vācakaḥ vakti tam api te naḥ eva sakṛt prakāśayanti krama bhāvāt na api ekaḥ eva bhāgaḥ śabdam vyanakti tad anya vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt eka varṇa bhāga kāle ca samasta rūpa anupalakṣaṇāt tat ayam apratisaṃhita sakala upalambhaḥ dhvani vat upalambha sākalya saṃnidhāna artham katham sādhayet kaḥ hi viśeṣaḥ atyanta anupalambhe sat asatoḥ upalambha sādhyeṣu artheṣu na ca saṃnidhi mātreṇa sādhanaḥ vyakti apekṣaṇāt sā ca iyam krama bhāvinī sat asatoḥ tulya upayogaḥ iti dhvanibhiḥ aśakya sādhanam kāryam tatra api tathā iti alam anyena tasmāt na varṇeṣu vākye vā apauruṣeya tā 
[134,26_135,07]	varṇa ānupūrvī vākyam ced na varṇānām abhedataḥ na artha antaram eva śabda rūpam vākyam apauruṣeyam kim tarhi varṇa anukrama lakṣaṇam hi naḥ vākyam tat apauruṣeyam sādhyam iti ced na varṇānām ānupūrvyā abhedāt na iyam artha antaram varṇebhyaḥ dṛśyāyām vibhāga upalambhāt adṛśyāyām tatas apratipatteḥ liṅga abhāvāt bhedavatyāḥ ca ānupūrvyā abhāve varṇa mātram avaśiṣṭam sarvatra iti pūrvavat prasaṅgaḥ teṣām ca na vyavasthānam krama antara virodhataḥ 
[135,08]	yadi akṛtaka ānupūrvī varṇānām te ca na bahavaḥ samāna jātīyāḥ yena kecid vyavasthita kramāḥ syuḥ anye yathā iṣṭa parāvṛttayaḥ kim tarhi ekaḥ eva trailokye akāraḥ tathā gakāraḥ tadā agniḥ iti eva syāt na gaganam iti akāragakārayoḥ pūrva apara bhāvasya vyavasthita tvāt kṛtakānām api hetu pariṇāma niyamavatām aśakyaḥ krama viparyayaḥ kartum yathā bīja aṅkura patra ādīnām ṛtu saṃvatsara ādīnām ca kim punar acalita avasthā svabhāvānām akṛtakānām kathaṃcid sthitānām pūrva avasthā tyāgam antareṇa anyathā abhāva ayogāt tyāge vā vināśa prasaṅgāt viśeṣeṇa nityāyām ānupūrvyām tat etat pratipadam krama anya tvam varṇa anya tve apūrva utpādāt varṇa bāhulyāt vā syāt tat ca anabhimatam api ca 
[135,20_135,21]	deśa kāla krama abhāvaḥ vyāpti nitya tva varṇanāt sā ca iyam ānupūrvī vā arṇānām deśa kṛtā vā syāt yathā pipīlikānām paṅktau kāla kṛtā vā yathā bīja aṅkura ādīnām sā dvividhāḥ api varṇeṣu na sambhavati vyāpteḥ nitya tvāt ca anyonya deśa parihāreṇa vṛttiḥ hi deśa paurvāparyam tat sarvasya sarveṇa tulya deśa tvāt varṇeṣu na sambhavati vāta ātapa vat ātma ādi vat ca tathā kāla parihāreṇa vṛttiḥ kālapaurvāparyam yadā ekaḥ na asti tadā anyasya bhāvāt tat api nityeṣu na sambhavati sarvadā sarvasya bhāvāt na ca anyā gatiḥ asti tat katham varṇa paurvāparyam vākyam yat apauruṣeyam sādhyeta 
[136,07_136,16]	anitya avyāpitāyām ca doṣaḥ prāk eva kīrtitaḥ atha mā bhūt ayam doṣaḥ iti anityān avyāpinaḥ ca varṇān icchet tau api pakṣau prāk eva nirākṛtau iti aparihāraḥ vyakti kramaḥ api vākyam na nitya vyakti nirākṛtaḥ na varṇānām rūpa ānupūrvī vākyam kim tarhi tad vyakteḥ sā yathā sva varṇa abhivyakti pratyaya kramāt bhavantī krama yoginī iti tadā anupūrvī vākyam iti api mithyā tasyāḥ nityeṣu prāk eva niṣiddha tvāt kārya tā viśeṣaḥ eva sākṣāt śakti upadhānena jñāna janakānām vyaktiḥ iti ākhyātam etat vyāpārāt eva tad siddheḥ karaṇānām ca kārya tā 
[136,17^1]	yat khalu rūpam yatas eva upalabhyate tasya tad upalabdhinā antarīyakām upalabdhim eva āśritya lokaḥ kārya tām prajñāpayati sā varṇeṣu api asti saḥ eva ca anyatra api tad āśrayaḥ na viśeṣaḥ tat katham tulye abhyupagama nibandhane na varṇāḥ kāryāḥ na ca etat upalabdhi āśrayā kārya tā sthitiḥ kim tarhi yat sati eva bhavati iti sattā āśrayā sā sattā kutas siddhāḥ ye na kārya tām sādhayet na hi asiddhāyām asyām evam bhavati iti tasmāt sattā siddhiḥ tad sādhanī sā ca upalabdhiḥ eva satyam evam yadi tasya prāk na sattā siddhā syāt sā hi sattā siddhiḥ yā asiddhi pūrvikā 
[136,17^2_137,12]	nanu tat rūpam asiddham eva yat tathābhūta vijñāna avyavadhāna upayogi siddham eva tat anya vaikalyāt naḥ upayuktam iti ced katham idānīm upayukta anupayuktayoḥ abhedaḥ na api bhedaḥ śabda svabhāva asaṃsparśī tasya eva atiśayasya upayoga siddheḥ tasyāḥ kāraṇa tva prasaṅgāt yasya eva bhāve sādhya siddhiḥ tat eva hi tatra upayogi yuktam tad atiśaya upayoge api asya tadvat prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt atiśetaḥ eva avyavahita sāmarthya upayogaḥ avasthā bhedaḥ tad anyam anatiśayasya apekṣā ca prāk eva niṣiddhā sa ca karaṇa vyāpārāt eva siddhaḥ iti sarva kārya tulya dharmā tasya tādṛśasya vyaktau sarvam vyaṅgyam na vā kiṃcid api aviśeṣāt tathā hi sva jñānena anya dhīhetuḥ siddhe arthe vyañjakaḥ mataḥ yathā dīpaḥ anyathā vā api kaḥ viśeṣaḥ asya kārakāt 
[137,14^1]	sva pratipatti dvāreṇa anya pratipatti hetuḥ loke vyañjakaḥ siddhaḥ dīpa ādi vat sa ced prāk siddhaḥ syāt samāna jātīya upāda ana kṣaṇa siddheḥ na tasya eva atiśayasya jñāna hetoḥ tasya tad sāmagrī pratyaya tvāt ye punar asiddha upalambhanāḥ kārakāḥ eva kulāla ādi vat ghaṭa ādau pratyabhijñāna ādayaḥ api siddhi hetavaḥ na hetu lakṣaṇam puṣṇanti yat api kiṃcid uttarā akāra pratītiḥ akāra pratīteḥ pūrva abhinna viṣayā tadvat iti ādi tat api na sva lakṣaṇayoḥ abheda sādhane samartham tad svabhāva siddheḥ sāmānyena vacane bhinna viṣaya tvasya api avirodhaḥ eka viṣayayoḥ ca pratītyoḥ pūrva apara bhāva ayogāt saṃnihita asaṃnihita kāraṇa tvena utpāda an utpādāt saṃnidhāne api anutpannasya atad kāraṇa tvāt tayoḥ bhinna akhila kāraṇa tvam 
[137,14^2_138,14]	tatra eka abhede api śaktasya apratīkṣaṇāt yukti viruddham pūrva aparayoḥ pratītyoḥ eka viṣaya tvam pratīti pratibhāsa svabhāva bhede api nāma sāmyāt eka viṣaya tvam api ayuktam ghaṭa ādiṣu api prasaṅgāt tatra dṛṣṭa virodhāt asādhana tvam iti ced iha api virodha abhāvaḥ kena siddhaḥ yāvat tathā abhidheya ta artha bhedena vyāptā na sādhyate tāvat sandigdhaḥ vyatirekaḥ pratikaraṇa bhedam ca bhinna svabhāvaḥ śabdaḥ śrutau niviśamānaḥ yadā ekaḥ sādhyate kim na ghaṭa ādayaḥ tatra api śakyam evam vyañjaka bhedāt pratibhāsa bhedaḥ iti pratyavasthātum api ca karaṇānām samagrāṇām vyāpārāt upalabdhitaḥ niyamena ca kārya tvam vyañjake tad asambhavāt 
[138,16^1]	na hi kadācid vyāpṛteṣu karaṇeṣu śabda anupalabdhiḥ na ca avaśyam vyañjaka vyāpāraḥ artham upalambhayati kvacid prakāśe api ghaṭa ādi anupalabdheḥ sā iyam niyamena upalabdhiḥ tad vyāpārāt śabdasya tad udbhave syāt akartuḥ vyāpāre api tad siddhi ayogāt vyāpi nitya tvāt upalambhaḥ iti ced kaḥ idānīm ghaṭa ādiṣu samāśvāsaḥ teṣām tathā aniṣṭeḥ iti ced śabdaḥ kim iṣṭaḥ tad samāna dharmā na ca asya kaścid atiśayaḥ iti uktam pratiṣiddhe ca vyāpi nitya tve ghaṭa ādīnām vyañjaka antara sambhavāt adoṣaḥ prakāśaḥ hi eṣām vyañjakaḥ siddhaḥ kulāla ādīnām vyañjaka tve tādṛśāḥ eva syuḥ 
[138,16^2]	atiśerate ca tatas vyañjaka atiśayāt kārakāḥ eva upakārakasya gati antara abhāvāt tat etat śabdeṣu api tulyam tatra api indriya yogya deśatā ādibhyaḥ karaṇānām atiśayāt ghaṭa ādi kāraka dharmasya ca karaṇeṣu dṛṣṭeḥ tasya eva pradīpa ādeḥ viṣaya antarasya ca kasyacid vyañjaka antara abhāvāt tad kāraṇāni teṣām vyañjakāni syuḥ tasmāt na vyaktiḥ śabdasya bhavantī vā karaṇebhyaḥ atiśayattā vā śabdasya vyaktiḥ āvaraṇa vigamaḥ vijñānam vā gati antara abhāvāt tatra na atiśaya utpattiḥ anitya tā prasaṅgāt tasyāḥ pūrva apara rūpa hāni upajanana lakṣaṇa tvāt atha
[139,05_139,13]	tad rūpa āvaraṇānām ca vyaktiḥ te vigamaḥ yadi abhāve karaṇa grāma sāmarthyam kim nu tat bhavet na hi āvaraṇasya akiṃcitkarāṇi karaṇāni samarthāni nāma vigamaḥ ca abhāvaḥ na ca abhāvaḥ kāryam iti niveditam etat na api śabdasya nityasya kiṃcid āvaraṇam asāmarthyāt iti api uktam tasmāt na āvaraṇe karaṇa upakṣepaḥ na api eṣām asāmarthyam tad vyāpāra abhāve śabda anupalabdheḥ atas yuktam ete yat śabdān kuryuḥ anyathā śabda aviśeṣāt anyeṣām api vyaktiḥ prasajyate tathā abhyupagame sarva kāraṇānām nirarthatā 
[139,15_139,24]	yadi sarva kāraṇa samāna dharmāṇi api karaṇāni vyañjakāni na kiṃcid idānīm kāryam syāt na ca etat yuktam sarva kāraṇānām ānarthakya prasaṅgāt vastunaḥ anādheya viśeṣa tvāt āvaraṇa abhāvasya akārya tvāt vastu vat eva jñānasya api siddha tvāt jñānam prati kāraka tve kasyacid tathābhūtānām anyeṣām api tathā abhāva prasaṅgena sarvasya kārya tā prasaṅgāt tasmāt ayam kāraka abhimataḥ artha kalāpaḥ na vyaktau na kriyāyām iti vyarthaḥ eva syāt tathā ca idam anupakārya upakārakam nirīham jagat syāt śabda nitya tve ca sādhanam pratyabhijñānam sat prayoga ādi yat matam anudāharaṇam sarva bhāvānām kṣaṇa bhaṅgataḥ 
[140,01^1]	kṣaṇa bhaṅginaḥ hi sarva bhāvāḥ vināśasya akāraṇa tvāt iti uktam vakṣyate ca utpattimantaḥ ca paratas sattāyāḥ ākasmika tva ayogāt tat naḥ idam pratyabhijñānam sat prayoga ādikam kvacid anveti sthira eka rūpe apara apara svabhāva parāvṛttiṣu eva dīpa ādiṣu dṛṣṭam iti viruddham eva na abhinna janmanaḥ sādharmya vipralambhāt bhrāntyā dīpa ādiṣu bhāvāt abhinna janma iti kena avaṣṭambhena ucyate tasya eva abhedasya sarvatra paurvāparyeṇa cintya tvāt tathā bhedasya api iti ced tena eva saṃśayaḥ astu na ca saṃśayitāt siddhiḥ viveka adarśanāt ekatvam iti ced na jñāna paurvāparyeṇa sat asattva siddheḥ 
[140,01^2]	svabhāva viveka sadbhāvāt yadi aparāṇi jñānāni prāk saṃnihita kāraṇāni pūrva jñāna vat jātāni eva syuḥ ajātāni tu kāraṇa vaikalyam sūcayanti samarthasya jananāt asamarthasya api punar sāmarthya apratilambhāt pratilambhe vā sthairya ayogāt tat ayam sat prayogaḥ iti api jananam eva prayoktuḥ sāmarthyāt svayam samarthe tasya anupayogāt prayogaḥ iti api iṣṭa sādhana samartha utpādanam eva samāna jātīya upādāna apekṣam anapekṣam vā vā asya ādi prayoga vat karma ādi prayoga vat ca kathyate yaḥ api manyate samakṣe pratyabhijñānam pratyakṣam eva tatas pratyakṣāt eva sthairya siddhiḥ iti tat api uttaratra niṣetsyāmaḥ 
[140,21_140,25]	dūṣyaḥ kuhetuḥ anyaḥ api na eva kaścid dharmaḥ yaḥ samāna jātīyam anveti sarva dharmāṇām etad avastha tvāt sarva sthairya pratijñāyāḥ ca yathā abhidhānam yukti virodhāt anye api nitya hetavaḥ vācya doṣāḥ buddheḥ apuruṣa āśraye bādhāḥ abhyupeta pratyakṣa pratīta anumitaiḥ samam 
[140,27_141,08]	yadi vyaktiḥ buddhiḥ tadā ānupūrvī vādyam tasyāḥ apauruṣeya tva prasādhane buddhīnām puruṣa guṇa tva abhyupagamāt sama yaḥ asya bādhyate pratyakṣam khalu api etat yat imāḥ buddhayaḥ puruṣa saṃkhyātebhyaḥ puruṣa guṇebhyaḥ vā manaskāra ādibhyaḥ bhavanti iti na ca kārya tā nāma anyāḥ bhāva abhāva viśeṣābhyām sa ca bhāvaḥ pratyakṣaḥ abhāvaḥ api anupalabdhi lakṣaṇaḥ pratyakṣa sāmarthya siddhaḥ iti vakṣyāmaḥ tatas eva puruṣa kārya tā buddhīnām anumeya anvaya vyatireka liṅga tvāt asyāḥ kim ca ānupūrvyāḥ ca varṇebhyaḥ bhedaḥ sphoṭena cintitaḥ kalpanā āropitā sā syāt katham vā apuruṣa āśrayā 
[141,10_141,19]	varṇa vyatirekiṇī ānupūrvī sphoṭa vicāra anukrameṇa eva prativihitā na api sā varṇa svabhāvā vastu svabhāvasya etad vikalpa anatikramāt atad rūpeṣu tad rūpa samāropa pratibhāsinyā buddheḥ ayam vibhramaḥ syāt ānupūrvī iti sā ca katham apauruṣeyī buddhi viṭhapana pratyupasthāpanāt api ca ātyantikasya kasyacid svabhāvasya abhāvāt bhavatā dhvaninā anātyantikena bhavitavyam sa ca ahetukaḥ anya hetukaḥ vā nityam bhavet na ca puruṣa vyāpārāt tasmāt na apauruṣeyaḥ katham idam gamyate anātyantikaḥ dhvaniḥ anyaḥ vā bhāvaḥ iti sattā mātra anubandhi tvāt nāśasya anitya tā dhvaneḥ 
[141,20]	na hi nāśaḥ bhāvānām kutaścid bhavati tat bhāva svabhāvaḥ bhavet bhāvasya eva sva hetubhyaḥ tad dharmaṇaḥ bhāvāt na ca bhāva viśeṣa svabhāvaḥ tasya niṣetsyamāna tvāt tasmāt bhāva mātra svabhāvaḥ syāt tena śabdaḥ anyaḥ vā sattā bhājanaḥ sarve eva bhāvaḥ anātyantikaḥ iti siddham na siddham tasya eva vināśasya apara janma asiddheḥ tathā hi agninā kāṣṭham daṇḍena ghaṭaḥ iti vināśa hetavaḥ bhāvānām dṛśyante anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānam hetu tadvatoḥ lakṣaṇam āhuḥ na pūrvasya svarasa nirodhe anyasya viśiṣṭa pratyaya āśrayeṇa vikṛtasya utpatteḥ astu vai agniḥ kāṣṭha vināśa hetuḥ sa vināśaḥ agni janmā kim kāṣṭham eva āhosvit artha antaram 
[142,06_142,13]	agneḥ artha antara utpattau bhavet kāṣṭhasya darśanam avināśāt kim iti artha antarāt artha antara janmani kāṣṭham abhūtam nāma na dṛśyate vā atiprasaṅgaḥ hi evam syāt saḥ eva asya vināśaḥ iti ced yadi saḥ eva arthaḥ agni janmā abhāvaḥ tat idam abhūta tvāt na dṛśyate iti bhavatu tasya idam nāma abhāvaḥ iti tathā api katham 
[142,14^1]	anyaḥ anyasya vināśaḥ na hi kasyacid arthasya nāmakaraṇa mātreṇa kāṣṭham na dṛśyate iti yuktam na ca anyaḥ anyasya vināśaḥ atiprasaṅgāt viśeṣa abhāvāt tasya artha antara tvena vastu bhūtasya tad anyebhyaḥ kāṣṭhe agni kṛtaḥ svabhāvaḥ vināśaḥ na sarve iti ced kāṣṭhāḥ iti kaḥ sambandhaḥ āśraya āśrayi sambandhaḥ ced na tasya niṣetsyamāna tvāt janya janaka bhāvāḥ ced agneḥ iti kim kāṣṭhāt eva bhāvāt tad apekṣāt utpatteḥ adoṣaḥ iti ced anatiśaya lābhinaḥ kā apekṣā lābhe vai apara kāṣṭha janma syāt 
[142,14^2]	pūrvam tu apracyuti kāraṇam tathā eva dṛśyata tatas eva agneḥ pūrva vināśaḥ iti ced pūrveṇa asya kaḥ sambandhaḥ iti saḥ eva prasaṅgaḥ aparyavasānaḥ ca tat avaśyam vināśa sambandha yogyam uttaram atiśayam pratyupakurvāṇaḥ agniḥ apūrvam eva janayati iti pūrvam tad avastham dṛśyeta kāṣṭha vināśaḥ iti ca kāṣṭhābhāvaḥ ucyate na ca abhāvaḥ kāryaḥ tad kārī ca akārakaḥ eva iti anapekṣaṇīyaḥ iti uktam svabhāva abhāvasya ca tatas bhede tatas nivartamānasya bhāvasya svabhāvaḥ eva samarthitaḥ syāt iti katham abhūtaḥ nāma tasmāt na
[143,05_143,08]	anyaḥ anyasya vināśaḥ astu kāṣṭham kasmāt na dṛśyate kaḥ ayam artha antara bhāva kāṣṭha darśanayoḥ virodhaḥ tad parigrahataḥ ced na tena anāvaraṇam yatas yadi tena artha antareṇa parigṛhītam iti kāṣṭham na dṛśyeta tat kāṣṭhasya āvaraṇam iti āpannam na ca etat yuktam āvaraṇam hi darśanam bibadhnīyāt na abhighāṭa ādīni dravya sāmarthyāni sarva pratibandhe ca nanu anena eva dravyam vināśitam syāt sarva śakti pracyāvanāt punar tatra api agnau iva prasaṅgāt anavasthā apracyuteṣu vai asya abhighāṭa sāmarthya ādiṣu satā vā tena anyena kim vināśitam yadi ca agni samudbhavasya vināśa ākhyasya arthasya parigrahāt kāṣṭham na dṛṣṭam 
[143,16_143,22]	vināśasya vināśi tvam syāt utpatteḥ tatas punar kāṣṭhasya darśanam avaśyam hi utpattimatā vināśena vinaṣṭavyam tasmin vinaṣṭe punar kāṣṭha ādīnām unmajjanam syāt hantṛ ghāte caitrāpunarbhavaḥ yathā atra api evam iti ced dhantuḥ na amaraṇa tvataḥ vināśa vināśe api ca vastunaḥ pratyāpattiḥ na hi hantari hate api tadvatas pratyujjīvati iti ced na hantuḥ tad ghāta hetu tvāt na brūmaḥ vināśa hetoḥ agni daṇḍa ādeḥ nivṛttau bhāvena bhavitavyam iti kim tarhi bhāva abhāvasya atyanta anupalabdhi lakṣaṇasya tad nivṛttau kā anyā gatiḥ svabhāva sthiteḥ hantā hi caitrasya na nāśa kalpaḥ kim tarhi daṇḍa ādi kalpaḥ nāśa kalpam hi asya maraṇam tad nivṛttau ca syāt eva asya punarbhāvaḥ 
[144,02_144,04]	ananya tve api nāśasya syāt nāśaḥ kāṣṭham eva tu tasya sattvāt ahetu tvam na atas anyā vidyate gatiḥ anartha antara bhūtaḥ vināśaḥ kāṣṭhāt tat eva tat bhavati tat ca prāk eva asti iti kim atra sāmarthyam vahni ādīnām tasmāt tad anupakārāt tena na apekṣyante kathaṃcid na api asya idam iti sambandham arhati tasya upakāra nibandhana tvāt anyathā atiprasaṅgāt pāraṃparyeṇa upakāre api avaśyam ayam vikalpaḥ anveti sa kim upakāraḥ artha antaram āhosvit tat eva iti tad artha antara tve api tasya iti punar upakāra tva ādi paryanuyogaḥ tad avasthā eva tathā ananya tve tasmāt sataḥ rūpasya tattva anyat tva avyatikramāt upakāra utpādanasya ca rūpa niṣpādana lakṣaṇa tvāt tad atad kriyā vikalaḥ na kartā eva iti na kasyacid hetuḥ ahetuḥ ca na apekṣate tasmāt svayam ayam bhāvaḥ tad svabhāvaḥ iti siddham 
[144,15_144,22]	ahetu tve api nāśasya nitya tvāt bhāva nāśayoḥ sahabhāva prasaṅgaḥ ced asataḥ nityatā kutas syāt etat yasya api vināśaḥ ahetukaḥ saḥ avaśyam nityaḥ iti bhāvaḥ tad abhāva lakṣaṇaḥ vināśaḥ ca saha syātām iti na tasya nitya anitya dharma ayogāt na hi asati ayam vikalpaḥ sambhavati tayoḥ vastu dharma tvāt vināśasya ca akiṃcitvāt bhavataḥ hi kenacid sahabhāvaḥ syāt na ca vināśaḥ bhavati tasmāt adoṣaḥ asattve abhāva nāśi tva prasaṅgaḥ api na yujyate yasmāt bhāvasya nāśena na vināśanam iṣyate 
[144,24]	katham asan vināśaḥ bhāvam nāśayet atas avināśī bhāvaḥ syāt iti aprasaṅgaḥ eva vināśāt bhāva nāśa anabhyupagamāt yaḥ hi vināśaḥ iti kiṃcid naḥ iti āha sa katham tatas bhāva nāśam icchet katham idānīm asati vināśe bhāvaḥ naṣṭaḥ nāma na hi asat vināśāḥ naṣṭāḥ gaṇyante pratyutpanna avasthāyām na hi yaḥ yena atadvān sa tena tathā vyapadiśyate pratīyate vā yathā aśvaḥ viṣāṇena na vai vināśaḥ na asti eva sa tu na asti yaḥ bhāvasya bhavanti bhāvaḥ eva tu kṣaṇa sthiti dharmāḥ vināśaḥ tam asya svabhāvam uttara kālam vibhāvayantaḥ vināśaḥ asya bhūtaḥ iti yathāprati iti vyapadiśanti iti uktam na hi bhāvasya kiṃcid kadācid bhavati saḥ eva kevalam sva hetubhyaḥ tathābhūtaḥ bhavati tat na kenacid bhavatā sa naṣṭaḥ kim tarhi svabhāvaḥ eva asya yena sa naṣṭaḥ nāma katham tarhi idānīm ahetukaḥ vināśaḥ bhavati iti ucyate 
[145,12_145,14]	naśyan bhāvaḥ apara apekṣaḥ iti tat jñāpanāya sā avasthā ahetuḥ uktāḥ asyāḥ bhedam āropya cetasā na bhāvaḥ jātaḥ aparasmāt nāśam pratilabhate tathābhūtasya eva svayam jāteḥ iti apara apekṣa dharma antara pratiṣedha artham tad svabhāva jñāpanena artha antaram iva dharmiṇaḥ dharmam cetasā vibhajya tanmātra jijñāsāyām svabhāvaḥ eva tathā ucyate tat etat manda buddhayaḥ kvacid tathā darśanāt ghoṣa mātra vipralabdhāḥ nāśam guṇam tasya ca bhāvam āropya sa hetukam ahetukam vā apratiṣṭhita tattvayā bhāva cintayā ātmānam ākulayanti 
[145,21_145,26]	svatas api bhāve abhāvasya vikalpaḥ ced ayam samaḥ nanu apara bhāvi tve api vināśasya svatas eva bhāvasya bhavataḥ ayam tattva anyat tva vikalpaḥ tulyaḥ tadā kim artha antara bhāve bhāvaḥ na dṛśyate anartha antara tve api tat eva tat bhavati tat na kiṃcid asya jātam iti katham vinaṣṭaḥ nāma nanu atra na tasya kiṃcid bhavati na bhavati eva kevalam 
[145,27^1]	iti uktam na hi ayam vināśaḥ anyaḥ vā kaścid bhāvasya bhavati iti āha kim tarhi saḥ eva bhāvaḥ na bhavati iti yadi hi kasyacid bhāvam brūyāt na bhāvaḥ anena nivartitaḥ syāt tathā ca bhāva nivṛttau prastutāyām aprastutam eva uktam syāt na hi kasyacid bhāvena bhāvaḥ na bhūtaḥ nāma tadā na bhūtaḥ yadi svayam na bhavet na bhavati iti ca prasajya pratiṣedhaḥ eṣa na paryudāsaḥ anyathā iha api kasyacid bhāve na pratiṣedha paryudāsayaḥ rūpa bhedaḥ syāt ubhayatra vidheḥ prādhānyāt evam ca apratiṣedhāt kasyacid paryudāsaḥ api kvacid na syāt yadi hi kiṃcid kutaścid nivarteta tadā tad vyatireki saṃspṛśyeta tad paryudāsena tat ca na asti 
[145,27^2]	sarvatra nivṛttiḥ bhavati iti ukte kasyacid bhāvasya eva pratītiḥ tathā ca anena artha antara bhāvaḥ eva uktaḥ syāt na tayoḥ parasparam vivekaḥ aviveke ca na paryudāsaḥ tat evam vyatireka abhāvāt anvayaḥ api na syāt tasya eka svabhāva sthiti lakṣaṇa tvāt tad sthitiḥ ca tad anya vyatireke sati syāt sa ca na asti iti apravṛtti nivṛttikam jagat syāt tasmāt yasya nāśaḥ bhavati iti ucyate sa svayam eva na bhavati iti uktam syāt na vai ghoṣa sāmyāt viṣaya antara dṛṣṭaḥ vidhiḥ sarvatra yojanām arhati na hi gardabhaḥ iti nāmakaraṇāt bāleya dharmāḥ manuṣye api saṃyojyāḥ tathā na caitrasya putraḥ bhavati iti atra dṛṣṭaḥ vidhiḥ nāśe api virodhāt evam ca abhidhāne api prayojanam āveditam eva atas 
[146,17_146,18^1]	bhāve hi eṣa vikalpaḥ syāt vidheḥ vastu anurodhataḥ bhāvaḥ avaśyam bhavantam apekṣate sa ca svabhāvaḥ eva niḥsvabhāvasya kvacid vyāpāre samāveśa abhāvāt vyāpāraḥ iti hi tathābhūta svabhāva utpattiḥ sā niḥsvabhāvasya katham syāt katham idānīm bhavati abhāvaḥ śaśa viṣāṇam iti ādi vyavahāraḥ na vai śaśa viṣāṇam kiṃcid bhavati iti ucyate api tu evam asya na bhavati iti bhāva pratiṣedhaḥ eva kriyate api ca vyavahartāraḥ eva etat evam vyāpāra vat iva samāropya ādarśayanti prakaraṇena kenacid na tu tat tathā sarva artha vivecanam hi tatra tattvam na kasyacid samāveśaḥ na khalu evam vināśaḥ vastuni tad bhāvāt asau api yadi vaktṛbhiḥ evam khyāpyate na tu svayam tathā tadā na kiṃcid bhavati iti iṣṭam eva 
[146,18^2]	tasmāt svayam bhavan svabhāvaḥ vikalpa dvayam na ativartate tattvam anyat tvam iti atattvam eva svabhāvasya anyat tvam na hi rūpa rasayoḥ api anyat eva parasparam anyat tvam svabhāva apratibandhaḥ anyat tvam iti ced kaḥ ayam pratibandhaḥ nāma yena sa ca na syāt na anya svabhāvaḥ ca janma iti ced sarva kāraṇānām parasparam avācya tā syāt tathā ca sarvaḥ sarvasya kathaṃcid upayogi iti na kaścid kutaścid anyaḥ syāt evam ca avācya tā iti api kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ eva śabda antareṇa uktaḥ syāt na artha bhedaḥ svabhāvān anugamanam tu anyat tvam brūmaḥ sa ca svabhāvavatām parasparam asti eva iti anyat tvam eva na ca tad janma lakṣaṇāt svabhāva pratibandhāt anyaḥ pratibandhaḥ nāma 
[146,18^3]	anāyattasya vyabhicāra avirodhāt tatas dharma bhedāt ca anyat tvam jñāna kṛtaḥ pratibandhaḥ iti ced syāt etat yat pratipattinā antarīyakam yat jñānam tad gatau niyamena tad pratibhā āsanāt tat atad rūpam api avācyam iti na tasya niḥsvabhāva tvāt svayam saḥ eva hi tasya svabhāvaḥ yaḥ pratibhāti svabhāvavat tve asya tadvat pratibhāsa prasaṅgāt apratibhāsamānasya ca dṛśya abhāvāt adṛśya tve api na tad rūpam jñānam iti kasya kim āyattā pratipattiḥ na ca yat yat āyatta apratītikam tasya svabhāva pratibhāsaḥ eva naśyati prakāśa āyatta pratītīnām iva nīla ādīnām kā vā tasya pratyāsattiḥ tatra yat tasmin anātma rūpe pratīyamāne sa svayam pratyupatiṣṭhate 
[146,18^4]	atiprasaṅgaḥ hi evam syāt pratīyamānasya tad upādāna tā iti ced kaḥ ayam upādāna arthaḥ na kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ anabhyupagamāt abhyupagame vā na kārya kāraṇe anyonya pratīti pratyupasthāpane pratīteḥ eva tat na antarīyaka tā pratyāsattiḥ iti ced nanu saḥ eva asati pratibandhe na yuktāḥ iti ucyate na akārya kāraṇayoḥ kaścid pratibandhaḥ iti ca uktam yat pratipattinā antarīyakam yat jñānam iti api tad jñāne sati syāt na hi yaḥ vijñāne svarūpeṇa asvarūpa asaṃsargeṇa na pratibhāsate tasya kiṃcid jñānam tad abhāvāt na sidhyati avācya tā lakṣaṇam artha rūpasya tat bhavatā vastutas tattva anyat tva bhājā bhavitavyam yasya tu vinaśyataḥ bhāvasya na kiṃcid bhavati tena
[148,07_148,12]	na bhāvaḥ bhavati iti uktam abhāvaḥ bhavati iti api yat api ayam bhāvasya abhāvaḥ bhavati iti āha tat api bhāvaḥ na bhavati iti eva uktam bhavati evam hi sa nivartitaḥ bhavati pratiṣedhe vidheḥ asambhavāt tatas eva asya vināśe na kaścid hetuḥ tathā hi apekṣyeta paraḥ kāryam yadi vidyata kiṃcana yat akiṃcitkaram vastu kim kenacid apekṣyate 
[148,14]	sati hi kārye kāraṇam bhavati na ca naśyataḥ bhāvasya kiṃcid kāryam iti uktam tasmāt yaḥ nāma nāśa hetuḥ sa bhāve na kiṃcid karoti iti akiṃcitkaraḥ na apekṣyaṇīyaḥ tat katham idānīm anutpanna atiśayaḥ tad avasthaḥ eva bhāvaḥ naṣṭaḥ nāma nanu atiśaya utpattau api saḥ eva tasya atiśayaḥ utpannaḥ iti katham sa naṣṭaḥ nāma tena na ayam tad avasthaḥ naṣṭaḥ nāma yena svayam na bhavati tena naṣṭaḥ na artha antara utpādāt iti uktam na hi atiśaya utpattyā svayam na bhūtaḥ nāma abhāvasya sarva atiśaya upākhyā nivṛttyā sarva bhāva dharma viveka lakṣaṇa tvāt bhāvasya ca utpatti samāveśa lakṣaṇa tvāt tasmāt na abhāve kasyacid bhāva upakṣepaḥ anyasya 
[148,25_148,27]	etena ahetuka tve api hi abhūtvā nāśa bhāvataḥ sattā nāśi tva doṣasya pratyākhyātam prasañjanam yaḥ api manyate ahetuke api vināśe abhūtvā asya bhāvāt sattā nitya tvam ca durnivāram abhūtvā bhavan ahetukaḥ bhavati iti api viruddham iti saḥ api anena eva pratyākhyātaḥ kasyacid bhāvān abhyupagamāt 
[149,04_149,10]	yathā keṣāṃcid eva iṣṭaḥ pratighaḥ janminām tathā nāśaḥ svabhāvaḥ bhāvānām na anutpattimatām yadi atha api syāt bhavatu nāma svabhāvaḥ eṣa bhāvānām ye ime kṣaṇa sthiti dharmāṇāḥ sa tu utpattimatām eva bhaviṣyati na hi svabhāvaḥ iti sarvaḥ sarvasya svabhāvaḥ bhavati pratigha ātma tāvat satyam etat tathā api svabhāva niyamāt hetoḥ svabhāva niyamaḥ phale na anitye rūpa bhedaḥ asti bhedakānām abhāvataḥ 
[149,12^1]	na vai pratighaḥ anyaḥ vā svabhāvaḥ akasmāt pratiniyamavān yādṛśī tu sva hetoḥ śakti sthitiḥ tādṛśam phalam bhavati iti hetu svabhāva niyamāt phala svabhāva niyamaḥ ākasmika tve api asya uktaḥ doṣaḥ pratighāta ātma tā hetu svabhāva pratiniyama vat na naśvara janana pratiniyata svabhāvam bhāvam paśyāmaḥ yena tad janmā tathā syāt na anyaḥ sarva ākāra janmanām vināśa darśanāt nanu idam api aniśceyam eva sarva ākāra janmānaḥ naśyanti iti tāsām aniḥśeṣa darśanāt vicitra śaktayaḥ hi sāmagryaḥ dṛśyante tatra kācid syāt api yā anaśvara ātmānam janayet na 
[149,12^2]	jñeya adhikārāt ye kadācid kvacid kenacid jñātāḥ santaḥ na jñāyante teṣām sattā anubandhī nāśaḥ iti brūmaḥ te eva kṛtakāḥ anityāḥ sādhyante na hi ayam sambhavaḥ asti yat te jñāna janana svabhāvāḥ punar anaṣṭāḥ na janayeyuḥ apekṣeran vā param tad janana svabhāvasya niṣpatteḥ na ca teṣu anapekṣeṣu kasyacid kadācid kiṃcid jñānam nivarteta na ca evaṃbhūtam kiṃcid asti sarvasya kenacid kadācid jñānāt jñāna mātra artha kriyāyām api asāmarthye vastu eva na syāt tathā hi tad lakṣaṇam vastu iti vakṣyāmaḥ tasya ca vināśa avyabhicārāt sa sattā anubandhī 
[150,03_150,10]	pratyākhyeyāḥ atas eva eṣām sambandhasya api nityatā atas eva yathā uktāt vastu mātra anubandhāt vināśasya śabda vat sambandha nitya tā api pratyākhyeyā yā ca śabda śaktiḥ yogyatā ākhyāḥ artha pratipattyā āśrayaḥ jaiminīyaiḥ varṇyate sa artha antaram eva na bhavati tathā hi yogya tā iti rūpa atiśayaḥ eva bhāvānām iti āveditam prāk astu vai artha antaram tathā api sambandha doṣaiḥ prāk uktaiḥ śabda śaktiḥ ca dūṣitā uktaḥ hi sambandha artha antara vāde aneka prakāraḥ doṣaḥ tena eva sā śabda śaktiḥ dūṣitāḥ iti na punar ucyate 
[150,11_150,14^1]	api ca na apauruṣeyam iti eva yathā artha jñāna sādhanam dṛṣṭaḥ anyathā api vahni ādiḥ aduṣṭaḥ puruṣa āga sā bhavantu nāma apauruṣeyāḥ vaidikāḥ śabdāḥ tathā api sambhāvyam eva eṣām ayathārtha jñāna hetu tvam na hi puruṣa doṣa upadhānāt eva artheṣu jñāna vibhramaḥ tad rahitānām api pradīpa ādīnām nīlotpala ādiṣu vitatha jñāna jananāt tat ime śabdāḥ saṃskāra nirapekṣāḥ prakṛtyā ca artheṣu pratibhāna hetavaḥ syuḥ svabhāva viśeṣāt vahni ādi vat vitatha vyaktayaḥ ca niyamena eva niyama kāraṇa abhāvāt ayuktam iti ced avitatha vyakti niyame kim kāraṇam tasmāt yathā artha vyakti niyama vat prakṛtyāḥ ayathārtha vyakti niyamaḥ kim na kalpyate 
[150,14^2]	athavā vahni ādi vat eva artheṣu ubhaya jñāna hetu tvam syāt na hi apauruṣeyāḥ api vahni ādayaḥ ekatra yathā artha jñāna hetavaḥ api sarvatra tathā bhavanti iti tathā śabdānām api apauruṣeya tve api ubhayam syāt iti bhavatu vahni ādīnām kṛtaka tvāt yathāpratyayam anyatra anyathātvam na punar nityeṣu śabdeṣu etat asti nanu evaṃvidhaḥ anyatra api asti eva dharmaḥ teṣām api saṃketa balāt anyathā vṛtteḥ kārya janana svabhāva sthitau ca eṣām samaya ādeḥ apekṣaṇīyasya abhāvāt tatas pratītiḥ artheṣu sarvasya sarvadā syāt na ca asti tasmāt na śabdāḥ sthita svabhāvāḥ iti api ca 
[151,03_151,14]	na jñāna hetu tā eva syāt tasmin akṛtake mate nityebhyaḥ avastu sāmarthyāt na hi janma asti kasyacid yadi akṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ na tasmāt artheṣu pratītiḥ eva syāt pratīti janma itara kālayoḥ tulya rūpasya pratīti janmani sāmarthya sambhāvanā yogāt evam ayam janakaḥ naḥ evam iti vivecanīyasya rūpa bhedasya abhāvāt na yādṛśaḥ asya ajanakaḥ tādṛśaḥ eva janakaḥ yuktaḥ anya apekṣāḥ api niṣiddhāḥ eva tasmāt na nityānām kvacid vijñāna janana sāmarthyam kadācid ajanane nityam ajanana prasaṅgāt kārya sātatya adarśanāt ca na te kathaṃcid kartāraḥ iti ukta prāyam yāḥ api etāḥ nitya abhimateṣu ākāśa ādiṣu pratipattayaḥ tāḥ api na tad svabhāva bhāvinyaḥ tathā hi vikalpa vāsanā udbhūtāḥ samāropita gocarāḥ jāyante buddhayaḥ tatra kevalam na artha gocarāḥ 
[151,16^1]	sva lakṣaṇa viṣayā hi buddhiḥ niyamena tad yogya tā upasthāpana anuvidhāyinī iti tasmin sati asyāḥ kāraṇe yogye sā bhavati eva tat yadi nityānām padārthānām sva lakṣaṇe kasyacid jñānam syāt sarvasya sarvadā syāt kārya viśeṣāḥ hi vyaktayaḥ kathaṃcid kvacid upayujyamānāḥ tad upajanana yogyā atiśaya pratilambha hetum vastu viśeṣam apekṣante iti yuktam tathā akārya viśeṣaḥ nityaḥ bhāvaḥ kenacid gṛhyamāṇaḥ tad kāraṇa apekṣaḥ yadi grahaṇam asya janayet yuktam yat tena eva gṛhyeta tat ca sthita svabhāva tvāt na sambhavati iti sarveṇa samam gṛhyeta na vā kenacid iti san kenacid dṛṣṭaḥ na nityaḥ kaścid atīndriyaḥ syāt na ca etat asti tasmāt artha sāmarthya anapekṣāḥ samāropita gocarāḥ āntaram eva upādānam vikalpa vāsanā prabodham āśritya bāhya artha śūnyāḥ bhrāntayaḥ eva ākāśa ādiṣu sarvasya sambhavanti iti 
[151,16^2]	tasmāt na aparāvṛtti dharmāḥ śabdāḥ tattve vā kutas etat avitatha artha pratītayaḥ eva iti na hi agniḥ himasya bheṣajam iti ādiṣu śīta pratighāta sāmarthyam loka prasiddham agneḥ khyāpyate iti sarvam tathā bhavati lokasya sva icchā kṛta saṃketa anuvyavahārāt kim ayam lokaḥ sva saṃketam anuvidadhat evam pratyeti āhosvit śabda svabhāva sthiteḥ iti sandehaḥ loka icchayā api parāvartyamānāḥ śabdāḥ punar anyatra anyathā dṛśyante iti loka prasiddhi anuvidhāne api sambhavati eṣām anyathā bhāvaḥ tasmāt kasyacid avaiparītya darśane api sarveṣām tathā abhāvaḥ na sidhyati akṛtaka svabhāva tve api hi eṣām kaścid mithyā artha niyataḥ api syāt iti svabhāva aparijñānāt sarvatra saṃśayaḥ syāt 
[152,12_152,14]	mithyātvam kṛtakeṣu eva dṛṣṭam iti akṛtam vacaḥ satya artham vyatirekasya virodhi vyāpanāt yadi atha yat mithyā artham vacanam tat akhilam kṛtakam iti hetu vyatirekeṇa sādhya vyatirekasya vyāpteḥ anyatra asambhavāt akṛtakam satya artham iti syāt vinā api anvayena yaḥ hi yena avyāptaḥ tatra tad vyatirekaḥ śaṅkyeta na ca viruddhayoḥ ekatra sambhavaḥ asti asambhave ca vijātīyasya gati antara abhāvāt iṣṭa artha siddheḥ tad sādhana tvāt ca liṅgasya vyartham anvaya darśanam vyatireka mātreṇa eva siddheḥ iti satyam etat yadi vipakṣayoḥ vyāpya vyāpaka bhāvaḥ sidhyet sa tu na siddhaḥ yasmāt 
[152,22_153,01]	hetau asambhave anukte bhāvaḥ tasya api śaṅkyate viruddhānām padārthānām api vyāpaka darśanāt yadi hetoḥ sādhya vipakṣe abhāvaḥ sidhyet tadā sādhya vyatirekam hetu vyatirekaḥ vyāpnuyāt na ca tatra tasya asambhave pramāṇam paśyāmaḥ na ca aviruddha vidhiḥ pratiṣedha sādhanaḥ yuktaḥ atiprasaṅgāt na ca ekatra dṛṣṭasya anyatra asambhavaḥ eva pṛthak viruddha sahabhāvinām api darśanāt anitya tva vat prayatna ānantarīyaka itarayoḥ na ca tathāvidhasya adarśanāt asattvam eva yasmāt na asattā siddhiḥ iti uktam sarvatas anupalambhanāt asiddhāyām asattāyām sandigdhā vyatirekitā 
[153,03]	na hi ayam puruṣa mātrakaḥ sarvam draṣṭum samarthaḥ yena asya darśana nivṛttyā na tathā syāt yasya hi jñānam jñeya sattām na vyabhicarati saḥ evam bruvāṇaḥ śobheta adarśanāt na asti iti tat ime svabhāva deśa kāla viprakarṣeṇa santaḥ api anupalakṣyāḥ syuḥ tathā hi kaḥ atyanta parokṣe arthe saṃvādanam itarat vā sarva darśī vacanasya akṛtakasya itarasya vā vibhāvayitum samarthaḥ pratipāditam ca etat kvacid tathā dṛṣṭānām api arthānām punar kathaṃcid anyathā bhāvaḥ yathā kvacid deśe madhurāṇi nimba phalāni saṃskāra viśeṣāt āmalakī phalāni ca na ca idānīm atad darśinā tāni pratikṣeptavyāni eva iti tasmāt akṛtakam ca syāt syāt mithyā artham ca iti na virodham paśyāmaḥ na hi iyam anupalabdhiḥ adṛśya ātmasu abhāva sa adhikāḥ iti uktam tena yat kiṃcid mithyā artham tat sarvam pauruṣeyam iti aniścayāt avyāptiḥ tathā hi 
[153,17_153,23]	anvayaḥ vyatirekaḥ vā sattvam vā sādhya dharmiṇi tad niścaya phalaiḥ jñānaiḥ sidhyanti yadi sādhanam tathā ca uktam yaḥ eva tu ubhaya niścita vācī sa sādhanam dūṣaṇam vā na anyatara prasiddha sandigdha vācī punar sādhana apekṣa tvāt iti kaḥ hi adṛṣṭa virodhasya sambhavam pratyācakṣīta tat ayam vyatirekaḥ saṃśayāt asādhanam api ca yatra sādhya vipakṣasya varṇyate vyatirekitā saḥ eva asya sa pakṣaḥ syāt sarvaḥ hetuḥ atas anvayī 
[154,01^1]	yat kiṃcid mithyā artham tat sarvam pauruṣeyam iti hetu vipakṣeṇa sādhya vipakṣasya vyāptiḥ tad abhāve abhāva siddhau syāt tad abhāve bhavataḥ tena vyāpti ayogāt yāḥ eva ca vijātīyayoḥ vyāvṛtti siddhiḥ sā eva anvaya sthitiḥ vipakṣa vyavaccheda lakṣaṇa tvāt sādhyasya pratiṣedha dvayāt ca vidhi siddhiḥ iti kā ananvaya avyatireka vyāpti siddhiḥ tat na kaścid hetuḥ ananvayaḥ nāma eka vyavacchedasya tad vijātīya siddhinā antarīyaka tvāt anitya nirātma tā ādi vyavacchede api tathā syāt na vyatireka vyavacchedasya bhāva rūpa tvāt na bhāva rūpa vyavacchede bhāva anuṣaṅgaḥ abhāva vyavacchedaḥ tu niyamena bhāva upasthāpanaḥ bhāva abhāvayoḥ anyonya viveka rūpa tvāt abhāva rūpaḥ tu vyatirekaḥ sa ca vyatiricyamānaḥ bhāvam upasthāpayati na evam nairātmya ādayaḥ svabhāva viśeṣāt kriyā bhoga adhiṣṭhāna asvatantraḥ hi ātmā nirātmā 
[154,01^2]	tad svātantrya lakṣaṇa tvāt ātmanaḥ tat rūpam nairātmyam naḥ ātma nivṛtti mātram anyathā nirupākhye kṛtaka tva ādya yogāt na tatas nairātmya siddhiḥ syāt ātma vyavacchedena nirātmanaḥ bhāvasya parāmarśāt adoṣaḥ iti ced paryudāsena vastu saṃsparśāt tat eva vastu rūpam nairātmyam āyātam yasya api na abhāva rūpaḥ vyatirekaḥ tasya bhāva rūpa vyavacchede na bhāva siddhiḥ syāt iti na anvaya anuṣaṅgaḥ tathā anairātmye api na bhāva siddhiḥ yathā naḥ idam nirātmakam jīvat śarīram prāṇa ādimat tvāt iti vipakṣayoḥ vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva cintāyām aprāṇa ādimattvaḥ eva nairātmyam dṛṣṭam tad abhāve ca na asti iti svayam na bhavat api prāṇa ādīnām naḥ ātmani siddhim upasthāpayati tathā sādhye api prāṇa ādibhiḥ vyudasyamānam syāt kevalam nairātmye abhāvāt prāṇa ādayaḥ tad nirasanāḥ naḥ ātma upasthāpanāḥ 
[154,01^3]	tatra bhāva asiddheḥ na ca nairātmya nivṛttyā ātma siddhiḥ syāt vipakṣa vyatireka darśane api prasaṅgāt tat na viparyaya vyāptiḥ vyatireka asiddhau tad siddhiḥ eva ca anvaya siddhiḥ asiddhau vā tad vyatireka nivṛtti siddhau api tad asiddhiḥ iti sādhye api prasaṅgaḥ tat na ananvayā vyatireka vyāptiḥ mithyā artha tāyāḥ tu pauruṣeya tvena vyāptyai apauruṣeyān nivṛttau api na satya artha tvam prakāra antara sambhavāt dvairāśye tu śabdānām etat syāt eka nivṛttau gati antara abhāvāt te tu anarthakāḥ api syuḥ iti naḥ iṣṭa siddhiḥ artha pratīteḥ na anarthakāḥ iti ced eṣa puruṣa vyāpāraḥ syāt artha antara vikalpavat yathā atad artha tve api bharata urvaśī ādi carita ādikam artham anye anyathā vyācakṣate tad anusāreṇa ca keṣāṃcid pratītiḥ 
[154,01^4]	tathā ayam anarthakeṣu artha vikalpaḥ puruṣa kṛtaḥ na tu śabda svabhāva kṛtaḥ puruṣa upadeśa apekṣaṇāt artha antara vat eva na hi prakṛtyā prakāśanāḥ tam apekṣante vahni ādayaḥ puruṣaḥ tu sva samaya vyāpāram ācakṣāṇe upadiśati iti nyāyyam puruṣa samita nisarga siddhayoḥ upadeśa apekṣaṇā viśeṣāt anya viśeṣa abhāvāt ca ekaḥ naisargikaḥ anyaḥ tu pauruṣeyaḥ iti duravasānam asti viśeṣaḥ pramāṇa saṃvādaḥ iti ced etat uttaratra niṣetsyāmaḥ na asti atyanta parokṣe arthe pramāṇa antara vṛttiḥ iti samāna dharmiṇoḥ arthayoḥ pramāṇa saṃvāda mātra viśeṣāt ekatra apauruṣeya tve bahutaram idānīm apauruṣeyam santi puruṣa kṛtāni api vākyāni kānicid evaṃvidhāni iti teṣu api prasaṅgaḥ tadvat eṣām api abhimata arthavattā pauruṣeyī ca syāt pramāṇa anurodhinī ca api ca idam mantrāḥ apauruṣeyāḥ ca iti vyāhatam paśyāmaḥ tathā hi 
[155,20_155,21]	samaya tve hi mantrāṇām kasyacid kārya sādhanam yuktam yadi ete mantrāḥ kasyacid samayaḥ yathā mad praṇītam etat abhimata artha upanibandhanam vākyam evam niyuñjānam anena arthena yojayāmi iti para artha parata anurodhena anyatas vā kutaścid hetoḥ kṛtaḥ syāt tadā mantra prayogāt kadācid artha niṣpattiḥ yuktā kavi samayāt iva pāṭhakānām 
[155,26_156,04]	atha api bhāva śaktiḥ syāt anyatra api aviśeṣatas na vai puruṣa samayāt mantrebhyaḥ artha siddhiḥ kim tarhi bhāva svabhāvaḥ eṣa yat ime kathaṃcid niyuktāḥ phala dāḥ tat tarhi rūpam varṇānām sarvatra aviśiṣṭam iti yathā kathaṃcid prayuktāt api phalam syāt varṇāḥ eva hi mantraḥ na anyat kiṃcid tad kramaḥ mantraḥ iti ced kramasya artha antara tvam ca pūrvam eva nirākṛtam 
[156,05]	na varṇa vyatiriktaḥ anyaḥ kramaḥ iti niveditam etat avyatireke ca varṇāḥ eva mantras te ca aviśiṣṭāḥ sarvatra iti sarvadā phala dāḥ syuḥ upaplavaḥ tu alpīyasaḥ api kramasya bhraṃśāt dṛṣṭaḥ kasyacid anuṣṭhānāt devatā saṃnidheḥ asākalyena virādhanāt ca sarva bhraṃśe tu kasyacid eva samayasya ananuṣṭhānāt asaṃnidheḥ na artha anarthau kim ca kramasya artha antara tve anartha antara tve vā varṇa ātmanaḥ tad krama ātmanaḥ vā mantrasya artha hetoḥ akṛtaka tvāt nityasya nityam saṃnidhānam iti
[156,13_156,18]	nityam tad artha siddhiḥ syāt yatas hi bhāva śakteḥ phala utpattiḥ sā avikalāḥ iti na phala vaikalyam syāt na hi kāraṇa sākalye kārya vaikalyam yuktam tasya akāraṇa tva prasaṅgāt na kevalāt mantra prayogāt iṣṭa siddhiḥ tasya vidhāna apekṣa tvāt iti ced asāmarthyam apekṣaṇe 
[156,19_156,23]	yadi mantrāḥ vidhānāt anyatas vā kaṃcid svabhāva atiśayam āsādayeyuḥ sa tatra samarthaḥ apekṣyaḥ syāt na ca nityeṣu etat asti iti uktam tat kim ayam asamarthaḥ apekṣyate iti anapekṣāḥ sadā kuryuḥ na vā kadācid anatiśayāt sarvasya sādhanam te syuḥ bhāva śaktiḥ yat īdṛśī prayoktṛ bheda apekṣā ca na asaṃskāryasya yujyate 
[156,25_157,04]	yadi bhāva śaktayā eva mantrāḥ siddhi pradā na te kaṃcid parihareyuḥ yajamānam anyam vā na hi anyam prati svabhāvaḥ atadbhāvaḥ bhavati tasya tena anapakarṣaṇāt anyena ca anutkarṣaṇāt kenacid saha kārya kāraṇa bhāva ayogāt pratyāsatti vipra karṣa abhāvāt atas eva asya asaṃskārya tvāt prayoktā api na asti atas prayoktā phalam aśnuvīta saṃskāryasya api bhāvasya vastu bhedaḥ hi bhedakaḥ prayoktṛ bhedāt niyamaḥ śaktau na samaye bhavet 
[157,06^1]	ādheya viśeṣāḥ hi anityāḥ bhāvāḥ tad hetoḥ svabhāva bhede tatas samāsādita atiśaya tvāt anyatra anyathā syuḥ na abhede kāraṇā viśeṣe kārya aviśeṣāt viśeṣe tasya ahetuka tva prasaṅgāt iti ukta prāyam tat ime mantrāḥ svabhāva atiśayāt phala dāyinaḥ kāryāḥ api na śūdra ādi prayoge api anyathā syuḥ śūdra vipra abhidhānayoḥ puruṣayoḥ svabhāva abhedāt na hi puruṣa icchā anuvidhāyinaḥ nāma vyavahāra bhedāt svabhāva bheda anubandhinām arthānām anyathātvam asti tayoḥ jāti bhedaḥ iti ced sa khalu ākṛti guṇa śakti bhede dṛṣṭaḥ gavāśva vat anupadeśam ca enam lokaḥ pratipadyate na tadvat anayoḥ kaṃcid api guṇam viniyatam paśyāmaḥ 
[157,06^2]	apaśyantaḥ ca katham bhedam pratipadyemahi yaḥ api ayam nāma bheda anvayaḥ loke pratīti bhedaḥ saḥ asati api jāti bhede vyāpāra viśeṣa anuṣṭhānāt anvayāt ca syāt vaidya vaṇij vi apadeśa ādi vat tat ime aviśiṣṭena prayujyamānāḥ mantrāḥ tatas aviśiṣṭam eva svabhāvam āsādayanti tena aviśeṣeṇa eva phala dāḥ syuḥ yadā tu samayāt ebhyaḥ phalam tadā ayam adoṣaḥ samaya kārasya ruceḥ phala utpatti niyamāt svabhāva vṛttayaḥ hi bhāvāḥ tad mukhena prasaṅgam arhanti na puruṣa icchā vṛttayaḥ teṣām yathā kathaṃcid vṛtteḥ yat api prayoktā phalam aśnutaḥ iti prayogam samīhita artha yogyasya utpādanam santāna pariṇāmanam vā paśyāmaḥ tat ubhayam viśeṣa janmani syāt anyathā 
[157,27_158,03]	anādheya viśeṣāṇām kim kurvāṇaḥ prayojakaḥ yena tatas kaścid phalam aśnute anyaḥ na prayogaḥ yadi abhivyaktiḥ sā prāk eva nirākṛtā na hi nityānām kācid abhivyaktiḥ iti uktam yatas abhivyañjakaḥ prayoktā syāt vyaktiḥ ca buddhiḥ sā yasmāt sa phalaiḥ yadi yujyate syāt śrotaḥ phala sambandhaḥ vaktā hi vyakti kāraṇam 
[158,06^1]	na hi śabdasya anyatas svarūpa pariṇāmaḥ vyaktiḥ na api āvaraṇa vigamanam kim tu tad viṣayā pratītiḥ aśrūyamāṇe avyakta vyapadeśāt tatra yadi buddhi hetuḥ vaktā syāt tat tulyam śrotari api iti saḥ api phalam vaktṛ vat aśnuvīta na hi vaktuḥ kaścid anyaḥ tad bhāvaḥ anyatra tad buddhi hetu tvāt para upādhi buddhiḥ śrotuḥ na vaktuḥ iti viśeṣaḥ iti ced kaḥ punar upayogaḥ vaktuḥ śrotari yena upādhiḥ iṣyate tatas śabda śrutiḥ iti ced nanu tat eva idam paryanuyujyate katham tatas iti asambandhāt viṣaya upanayanāt ayam asya śrāvakaḥ syāt 
[158,06^2_158,24]	tat ca na śakyam tasya kathaṃcid api apariṇāmāt indriya saṃskāra ādayaḥ api uktāḥ mām śrāvayati aham śrāvayāmi iti tayoḥ pratyayāt vaktṛ śrotṛ bhedaḥ iti ced anupakārya upakārakāt bhrānti mātrāt tad bhāve ati prasaṅgāt anyatra api bhrāntyā pratyaya darśanāt sarvathā upakāra abhāve ca tathā pratyayaḥ na yuktaḥ sarveṣām parasparam evam prasaṅgāt bhrāntiḥ api kutaścid upakāre sati kayācid pratyāsattyai anyatra bhavati sa api atyantān upakāre na syāt tasmāt vaktṛ śrotroḥ vyakti hetu tve aviśeṣāt tulyaḥ phala sambandhaḥ syāt api ca anabhivyakta śabdānām karaṇānām prayojanam manojapaḥ vā vyarthaḥ syāt śabdaḥ hi śrotra gocaraḥ 
[158,26_159,10]	śrotra grahaṇa lakṣaṇaḥ śabdaḥ tad atikrame ati prasaṅgāt nanu evam sāmānye api prasaṅgaḥ na brūmaḥ śabdaḥ eva iti śabdaḥ tu avaśyam tad lakṣaṇaḥ tasya lakṣaṇa antara abhāvāt tatra yadi śabda ātmanām mantrāṇām vyakti hetuḥ prayoktā anabhivyakta śruti viṣayāṇām karaṇānām prayoktā jāpī na mantra phalena yujyate na api manasā japan na hi tadā śrotreṇa kaṃcid artham vibhāvayāmaḥ na ca aśabda ātmā mantraḥ pāraṃparyeṇa tad ja tvāt tad vyaktiḥ sā api ced matiḥ na hi manasā dhyāyataḥ api mantra ābhāsā buddhiḥ śabda śravaṇāt ṛte tatas śabda prabhavāt sā api śabda vyaktiḥ eva anavasthā evam syāt śabda artha vikalpānām api paraṃparayā prasūtiḥ asti iti te api tathā syuḥ tad arthā ced asiddham kalpanā anvayāt 
[159,11]	na brūmaḥ sarvā śabda prabhavā buddhiḥ tad vyaktiḥ iti yā tu tad viṣayā sā tasya vyaktiḥ iti manaḥ vikalpasya tad viṣaya tvam asiddham na hi sva lakṣaṇe vikalpānām vṛttiḥ iti nivedayiṣyāmaḥ te hi yathāsvam āntarāt vikalpa vāsanā prabodhāt anapekṣita bāhya artha upanidhayaḥ bhavanti bāhya apāya anāgame api bhāvāt na hi yaḥ yasya satta upadhānam na apekṣate sa tasya hetuḥ ahetuḥ ca katham viṣayaḥ tasmāt na manaḥ vikalpaḥ śabda vyaktiḥ yatas tadvān prayoktā syāt tad prasūtā tad viṣayā buddhiḥ tad vyaktiḥ tad āśrayaḥ prayoktā iti atra api uktam śrotari api prasaṅgaḥ iti tad jñāne ca prayoge śabdaḥ puruṣe vyāpriyate tasya jñāna jananāt na puruṣaḥ śabde tad ātmani anupakārāt atha ca puruṣaḥ śabdānām prayoktā iti alaukikaḥ ayam vyavahāraḥ sarvathā śabda svabhāvānām mantrāṇām prayogāt phala avāptau vyarthaḥ manojapaḥ vikalpasya śabda rūpā saṃsparśāt 
[159,25_159,27]	sva sāmānya svabhāvānām eka bhāva vivakṣayā ukteḥ samaya kārāṇām avirodhaḥ na vastuni samaya kāraḥ tu sva lakṣaṇam indriya viṣayam sāmānya lakṣaṇam ca vikalpa pratibhāsam yathāvyavahāram saṃvṛtyā saṃkalayya samayam ārocayet yathāsamayam ca artham niṣpādayet iti na manojapa ādau doṣaḥ vastu svabhāvāt tu phalau āptau atad svabhāva saṃsparśe na syāt yat uktam na varṇebhyaḥ anyā kācid ānupūrvī iti tatra 
[160,04_160,06]	ānupūrvyām asatyām syāt saraḥ rasaḥ iti śrutau na kārya bhedaḥ iti ced na hi saraḥ rasaḥ iti ādi pādeṣu kaścid varṇa bhedaḥ na ca varṇa vyatiriktam anyat yatas kārya bhedaḥ syāt bhinnām ca tayoḥ pratibhām paśyāmaḥ ānupūrvīm eva ca atulyām na ca kāraṇa abhede kārya bhedaḥ yuktaḥ tasmāt asti sā bhedavatī yatas ayam pratīti bhedaḥ satyam
[160,11_160,13]	 asti sā puruṣa āśrayā tathā hi yaḥ yad varṇa samutthāna jñāna jāt jñānataḥ dhvaniḥ jāyate tad upādhiḥ sa śrutyā samavasīyate tad jñāna janita jñānaḥ sa śrutau apaṭu śrutiḥ apekṣya tad smṛtim paścāt ādhatte smṛtim ātmani iti eṣā pauruṣeyī eva tad hetu grāhi cetasām kārya kāraṇa tā varṇeṣu ānupūrvī iti kathyat 
[160,19]	citta samutthānā hi vāc vijñaptiḥ varṇa pada vākya abhidhānā tatra sakāra samutthāpana cetasā samanantara pratyayena akarotthāpana cittam utthāpyate tathā repha ākāra visarjanīya utthāpanāni pūrva pūrva pratyayāni tat ime anya ani ahetavaḥ varṇāḥ sva kāraṇa ānupūrvī janmānaḥ śruti kāle api yadā manda cāriṇaḥ pūrva varṇa jñāna sahakāri pratyaya apekṣāḥ sva jñānam janayanti tadā pūrva varṇa smaraṇa apekṣāḥ eva smṛtim upalīyante saḥ eṣa varṇānām bhinna kārya kāraṇa bhāva pratyaya nirvṛtti dharmā bhinna nirvartana dharmā ca svabhāvaḥ puruṣa saṃskāra bheda bhinnaḥ kramaḥ iti ucyate 
[161,07_161,12]	anyat eva tatas rūpam tat varṇānām padam padam kartṛ saṃskārataḥ bhinnam sahitam kārya bheda kṛt tasmāt na khalu ekaḥ eva padeṣu varṇānām svabhāvaḥ kartṛ citta saṃskāra bhedena bhedāt sa ca paraspara sahitaḥ kārya bheda hetuḥ sā ca ānupūrvī varṇānām pravṛttā racanā kṛtaḥ icchā aviruddha siddhīnām sthita krama virodhataḥ
