[161,14_161,21]	kārya kāraṇa bhūta pratyaya utpanna svabhāva viśeṣaḥ varṇānām ānupūrvī iti uktam sā ca puruṣa vitarka vicāra kṛtāḥ iti na sthita kramāḥ varṇāḥ icchā aviruddha siddhi krama tvāt krama viśeṣa anukrama vat na hi sthita kramāṇām deśa kālayoḥ himavat vindhya malaya ādīnām bīja aṅkura ādīnām ca sva icchayā kramaracanā śakyate kartum tatas eva puruṣa dharma saṃkhyāte vikalpa anukrame sati bhāvāt asati ca abhāvāt kārya kāraṇa tā siddheḥ puṃsām varṇa kramasya ca sarvaḥ varṇa kramaḥ pumbhyaḥ dahana indhana yukti vat 
[161,23]	sati indhane dāha vṛtteḥ asati abhāvāt adṛṣṭa indhanaḥ api dahanaḥ na anindhanaḥ tasya deśa kāla niyama ayogāt niyame ca tasya eva indhana tvāt dahana upādāna lakṣaṇa tvāt indhanasya tathā ayam api varṇa anukramaḥ puruṣa vikalpam yadi na apekṣeta nirālambanaḥ svayam prakāśeta yatne api na śakyeta atad prabhavāt kvacid śaktau sarvaḥ tathā syāt viśeṣa abhāvāt tad bhāva bhāvinaḥ atad viśiṣṭasya ca atatkṛtau sarvatra kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ ca nirākṛtaḥ syāt anvaya vyatireka lakṣaṇa tvāt tasya lakṣaṇa antaram vā vaktavyam sarve api ghaṭa ādayaḥ bhāvāḥ kṛtrimāḥ akṛtrimā prasajanti tatra api evam vikalpanāyāḥ sambhavāt viśeṣa abhāvāt ca tān api hi para kriyā darśana pūrvakam eva anyaḥ karoti avidita kartāraḥ ca kecid iti sarveṣām keṣāṃcid vā akriyā abhiniveśaḥ astu tasmāt sarvāḥ eva iyam varṇa ānupūrvī prasiddha kārya kāraṇa bhāva vastu dharma anatikramāt puruṣa kṛtā atas eva 
[162,12_162,14^1]	asādhāraṇa tā siddhāḥ mantra ākhya krama kāriṇām puṃsām jñāna prabhāvābhyām anyeṣām tad abhāvataḥ ayam kramaḥ varṇānām viṣa nirghāta ādi samarthaḥ na anyaḥ iti yadi anyaḥ api jānīyat tam tathā eva pratipadyeta na ca evam tasmāt ayam anukramaḥ svabhāvataḥ api kārya kṛt kaiścid eva vijñātaḥ iti asti parokṣa artha darśī puruṣaḥ na hi ayam arthaḥ samarthaḥ na ayam iti śakyam unnetum asaṃkīrṇasya liṅga viśeṣasya asiddheḥ pratyakṣayoḥ api anupadiṣṭayoḥ mantrā mantrayoḥ aparijñānāt upadeśe api kathaṃcid svabhāva vivekā pratīteḥ anyatra kārya saṃvādāt tasya ca karaṇāt prāk draṣṭum aśakya tvāt na ca ayam anukramaḥ svabhāvataḥ kārakaḥ kasyacid āśu siddheḥ anyasya cirāt aparasya vrata caraṇa ādi apekṣaṇāt 
[162,14^2]	ekasmāt api karmaṇaḥ kayościt artha anartha sandarśanāt vahatām api mantrāṇām punar kvacid visaṃvādāt na hi ayam prakāraḥ svabhāve yuktaḥ svabhāvasya sarvatra aviśeṣāt puruṣaḥ tu sva icchā pravṛttiḥ sattva sabhā gata ādi vaśāt sā iva aviśeṣāt vā kaṃcid anugṛhṇāti na aparam iti yuktam vrata caryā bhraṃśa ādinā dharma adharma upacaye dharma adharma ātmanoḥ vā prakṛtyā siddhi asiddhī iti ced na dharma viruddhānām api kraurya steya maithuna hīna karma ādi bahulānām vratānām ḍākinī bhaginī tantra ādiṣu darśanāt 
[162,14^3]	taiḥ ca siddhi viśeṣāt na ca evaṃvidhaḥ dharma svabhāvaḥ iti ca yathāvasaram nivedayiṣyāmaḥ maitrī śauca dharma parāyaṇānām ca tad nimittam eva kasyāścid siddheḥ asiddheḥ viparyaye ca punar siddheḥ na ca eka rūpāt karmaṇaḥ sa tad virodhī dharmaḥ yuktaḥ adharmaḥ ca katham idānīm dharma phalam iṣṭam adharma ātmanaḥ vrata ādeḥ aśnute na vai tasya eva tat iṣṭam phalam vrata ādeḥ vipākaḥ api tu pūrvasya karmaṇaḥ brahmahatyā deśa anuṣṭhānāt grāma pratilambha vat tasya tu adharma ātmanaḥ vratasya āgāmi phalam aniṣṭam 
[162,14^4]	sa tu mantra ādi prayogaḥ tasya iṣṭa phalasya karmaṇaḥ kathaṃcid upakārāt pācakaḥ citra tvāt upakāraka śakteḥ puruṣa viśeṣa āśraya vipāka dharmā sa dharmaḥ tena kṛtaḥ sa tathā tad ārādhanena phalati iti tad prayoga upakāra vipāka dharmaṇaḥ kṛta tvāt tad phalasya karmaṇaḥ vinā api puruṣeṇa tad upakārāt phalam iti ced na puruṣa ākāra svabhāva caryā adhimukti vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt tasya api upakāra tve siddhaḥ puruṣa viśeṣaḥ asādhāraṇa guṇaḥ tad adhimukteḥ eva hi viṣa karma ādi karaṇāt tasmāt ca mantrāḥ puruṣa pranītāḥ api tad upayoga nirapekṣāḥ svabhāvena phala dāḥ 
[163,23_163,25]	ye api tantra vidaḥ kecid mantrān kāṃścana kurvate prabhu prabhāvaḥ teṣām sa tad ukta nyāya vṛttitaḥ rathyā puruṣāḥ api kecana tantra jñāḥ svayaṃkṛtaiḥ mantraiḥ kiṃcid karma kurvanti tathā anyaḥ api anatiśayaḥ ca kartā ca mantrāṇām iti na teṣām prabhāvavatā eva adhiṣṭhānāt tat kṛtam hi te samayam anupālayantaḥ tad upadeśena ca vartamānāḥ samarthāḥ tad samaya upadeśa nirapekṣāṇām asāmarthyāt tatra api tad ākāra dhyāna ādeḥ eva prayogāt tasmāt tad adhiṣṭhānam eva tat tādṛśam iti unneyam api ca saḥ api tādṛśaḥ prabhāvavān eva ananya sādhāraṇa śakti tvāt iti puruṣa viśeṣaḥ eva samarthitaḥ
[164,04_164,13]	kṛtakāḥ pauruṣeyāḥ ca vācyāḥ mantrāḥ phala īpsunā na hi akṛtakānām prayogaḥ sambhavati na ca aprayuktebhyaḥ phalam iti prayogāt phalam icchatā kṛtakāḥ mantrāḥ vācyāḥ pauruṣeyāḥ ca puruṣa adhiṣṭhānam antareṇa anyatas asambhavat phalānām phala darśanāt kṛta samaya kāvya ādi vat aśakti sādhanam puṃsām anena eva nirākṛtam pratipāditāḥ hi puruṣa kṛtāḥ tad adhiṣṭhānāt ca phala dāḥ mantrāḥ tat asti kaścid atiśayavān iti tad pratikṣepa sādhanāni api prativyūḍhāni buddhīndriya ukti puṃstva ādi sādhanam yat tu varṇyate pramāṇa ābham yathārthāḥ asti na hi śeṣavataḥ gatiḥ 
[164,15_165,01]	yat tu buddhīndriya vacana yogāt puṃstvāt iti puruṣa atiśaya pratikṣepa sādhanam tat tu agamakam eva pratikṣepa sāmānya sādhanayoḥ asambhavāt na hi atīndriyeṣu atad darśinaḥ pratikṣepaḥ sambhavati satām api eṣām ajñānāt atas eva virodha asiddheḥ avirodhinā ca saha sambhava avirodhāt iti api uktam na api itara sāmānya siddhiḥ viśeṣa asambhavasya jñātum aśakya tvāt īdṛśeṣu ca anupalabdheḥ hetu tva pratikṣepāt puṃstva ādi sāmye api kasyacid viśeṣasya darśanāt sambhavat viśeṣe ca sāmya asiddhiḥ iti uktam tasmāt śeṣavat anumānam etat vyatirekasya sandehāt asamartham adarśane api vipakṣa vṛtteḥ api ca evaṃvādinaḥ jaiminīyāḥ svam eva vādam sva vācāḥ vidhurayanti tathā hi arthaḥ ayam na ayam arthaḥ naḥ iti śabdāḥ vadanti na kalpyaḥ ayam arthaḥ puruṣaiḥ te ca rāga ādi saṃyutāḥ tatra ekaḥ tattva vid na anyaḥ iti bhedaḥ ca kiṃkṛtaḥ tadvat puṃstve katham api jñānī kaścid katham na vaḥ 
[165,06_165,20]	na khalu ete vaidikāḥ śabdāḥ evam vikrośanti eta bhavantaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ ayam asmākam arthaḥ grāhyaḥ na anyaḥ iti kevalam anabhivyakta artha viśeṣa saṃsargāḥ śrutim abhipatanti tatra ekaḥ puruṣaḥ kaṃcid artham kalpayati anyaḥ aparam na ca śabdānām kaścid svabhāva pratiniyamaḥ yena ekam artham anurundhate na aparam kevalam samaya vaśāt tam tam āviśantaḥ dṛśyante teṣām avidita artha niyamānām atyakṣa āveśāt avidvān eva doṣa upaplavaḥ kaścid tattvam vyācaṣṭe na aparaḥ iti na nyāyyam atha kutaścid atiśayāt buddhīndriya ādīnām saḥ eva vetti na aparaḥ tasya kutas ayam atīndriya jñāna atiśayaḥ tathā anyaḥ api draṣṭā deśa kāla svabhāva viprakṛṣṭānām arthānām kim asambhavī dṛṣṭaḥ na hi tad pratikṣepa sādhanāni kānicid yāni naḥ enam upalīyante yathā ayam tad sādhana sambhave api asya viśeṣaḥ tathā anyasya api syāt iti anabhiniveśaḥ eva yuktaḥ yasya pramāṇa saṃvādi vacanam saḥ artha vid yadi na hi atyanta parokṣeṣu pramāṇasya asti sambhavaḥ 
[165,22]	syāt etat na vayam puruṣa prāmāṇyāt kasyacid vyākhyānam abhiniviṣṭāḥ kim tarhi pramāṇa antara saṃvādāt bahuṣu api vyākhyātṛṣu yaḥ pramāṇam pratyakṣa ādikam saṃsyandayati saḥ anumanyate tat na atīndriyeṣu adṛṣṭa ādiṣu pramāṇa antara āvṛtteḥ tad asambhavāt eva hi āgamaḥ tad pratipatti artham upayācyate anyathā sati api tasmin pramāṇa antara āvṛttau apratipatteḥ tatas ca kevalāt artha pratipatteḥ asādhanam eva āgamaḥ syāt kevalāt anyatas api atīndriyeṣu apratipattiḥ iti ced katham atīndriyaḥ ca nāma pratyakṣa ādi viṣayaḥ ca te punar sva viṣaye api āgamam apekṣye eva sādhakāḥ ced anāgamāt dhūma ādeḥ agni ādi pratyayaḥ na syāt na vai pravṛttaḥ āgame pramāṇa antaram anviṣyate kim tarhi saḥ eva āgama pravṛttiḥ na jñāyate iti ced svayam samarthasya prasādhane asya tad āgama upadhānam kam atiśayam puṣṇāti asamartham tu āgama pravṛttim api naḥ eva sādhayiṣyati sā ca atīndriya artha sambaddhā āgama pravṛttiḥ atīndriyā katham anyena siddhā anyat ca evam āgama lakṣaṇam syāt tathā hi 
[166,11_166,18]	yasya pramāṇa saṃvādi vacanam tat kṛtam vacaḥ saḥ āgamaḥ iti prāptam nirarthāḥ apauruṣeya tā tulye api āgama vāde pramāṇa balāt āgamasya kvacid āgama tve pramāṇa saṃvādaḥ vacanānām āgama lakṣaṇam syāt na apuruṣa kriyā tasyāḥ sarva artheṣu tulya tve api pramāṇa ābādhanāt pratipatteḥ tad bhāve api anyatra pramāṇa asaṃvādini aniṣṭa tvāt kim ca yadi atyanta parokṣe arthe anāgama jñāna sambhavaḥ atīndriya artha vid kaścid asti iti abhimatam bhavet 
[166,20_166,28]	yadi āgama anapekṣam jñāna āya athātathyam puruṣasya iṣyate parokṣe arthe santi puruṣāḥ atīndriya artha dṛśaḥ iti iṣṭam syāt pratyakṣa pūrvakānām pramāṇānām atad darśane asambhavāt pratyakṣa pramāṇam āgamaḥ pramāṇa antara vṛttiḥ tu pratyakṣam anvākarṣati iti na puruṣa atiśayaḥ nivāryaḥ syāt tasmāt na asti atīndriyeṣu pramāṇa antara vṛttiḥ atas eva āgamasya artha viśeṣa vṛtteḥ aparijñānāt ayam jaiminiḥ anyaḥ vā svayam rāga ādimān na artham vetti vedasya na anyatas na vedayati vedaḥ api veda arthasya kutas gatiḥ 
[167,02_167,09]	sarve eva hi puruṣaḥ anatikrānta doṣa viplavaḥ tam atīndriyam artha viśeṣa pratiniyamam vyākhyātā na svayam vetti na api enam anyaḥ vedayati tasya api tulya prasaṅga tvāt na hi andhena ākṛśyamāṇaḥ andhaḥ panthānam pratipadyate na api svayam vedaḥ sva artham vivṛṇoti upadeśa vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt tat ayam aparijñāta arthaḥ śabda gaḍuḥ evam śalya bhūtaḥ asat darśana snāyu vinibaddhaḥ duruddharaḥ duḥkham āsayati tena agnihotram juhuyāt svarga kāmaḥ iti śrutau khādet śva māṃsam iti eṣa na arthaḥ iti atra kā pramā 
[167,11^1]	kvacid api arthe pratyāsatti viprakarṣa rahitasya agnihotram juhuyāt svarga kāmaḥ iti ādi vākyasya bhūta viśeṣe yathā abhimatam ghṛta ādi prakṣipet iti ayam arthaḥ na punar śva māṃsam khādet iti na atiśayam paśyāmaḥ nanu ayam sarvatra samānaḥ prasaṅgaḥ parokṣa daiśikānām vacanānām artham yathā abhiprāyam idānīntanāḥ kim samanuyanti āhosvit viparyayam iti na upadeṣṭuḥ sva abhiprāya prakāśanena sampradāya sambhavāt na hi ayam adaiśikānām śabdānām sambhavati loka pratyāya na abhiprāyaḥ ca bruvāṇaḥ loka saṃketa prasiddhim anupālayati iti tatas api tad artha siddhiḥ syāt na apauruṣeyāṇām śabdānām tatra kasyacid samīha abhāvāt 
[167,11^2_168,07]	api ca nyāyam eva anupālayantaḥ paṇḍitāḥ heya upādeya tad āśrayeṣu saṃghaṭante na tu pravāda mātreṇa iti na samānaḥ prasaṅgaḥ tat ca yathāvasaram pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ nanu kaścid loka saṃniveśa ādiḥ ayukti viṣayaḥ api sambhāvanīya puruṣa vacanāt arthaḥ pratipadyate na apratyayāt na hi kvacid askhalitaḥ iti sarvam tathā vyabhicāra darśanāt tat pravṛtteḥ avisaṃvādena vyāpti asiddheḥ ca agatyā ca idam āgama lakṣaṇam iṣṭam na atas niścayaḥ tat na pramāṇam āgamaḥ iti api uktam apauruṣeyānām śabdānām artha jñānam na sampradāyāt na yukteḥ na lokāt iti tatra apratipattiḥ nyāyyā tatra api prasiddhaḥ loka vādaḥ ced pratipatti hetuḥ tatra kaḥ atīndriya artha dṛś aneka artheṣu śabdeṣu yena arthaḥ ayam vivecitaḥ 
[168,09^1]	na hi ayam loka vyavahāraḥ apauruṣeyāt śabda artha sambandhāt kim tarhi samayāt sva śāstra kāra samayāt pāṇinīya ādi vyavahāra vat upadeśa apekṣaṇāt na hi apauruṣeye tasmin upadeśaḥ yuktaḥ tasya kenacid ajñānāt atīndriya tvāt aindriyaka tve svayam pratipatti prasaṅgāt rūpa ādi vat upadeśe ca puruṣāṇām svatantrāṇām yathātattvam upadeśena avisaṃvādasya asiddheḥ anāśvāsaḥ veda vat tad vyākhyānam api apauruṣeyam sampradāya avicchedāt āgatam tatas artha siddhiḥ iti ced tasya api śabda ātmaka tve tulyaḥ paryanuyogaḥ katham asya arthaḥ viditaḥ iti puruṣaḥ hi svayam samitānām śabdānām artham śṛṅga grāhikayā api tāvat abudham bodhayet iti asti pauruṣeyānām śabdānām artha gatau upāyaḥ 
[168,09^2]	apauruṣeyaḥ tu śabdaḥ naḥ evam karoti na ca asya kaścid kvacid sambandha niyamam jñātum īśaḥ iti apratipattiḥ eva tad arthasya api ca vedaḥ tad vyākhyānam vā puruṣeṇa puruṣāya upadiśyamānam anaṣṭa sampradāyam eva anuvartate iti atra api samayaḥ śaraṇam āgama bhraṃśa kāriṇām āhopuruṣikayā tad darśana vidveṣeṇa vā tad pratipanna khalīkārāya dhūrta vyasanena anyatas vā kutaścid kāraṇāt anyathā racanā darśanāt api ca atra bhavān svam eva mukha varṇam sva vāda anurāgāt nūnam vismṛtavān puruṣaḥ rāga ādibhiḥ upaplutaḥ anṛtam api brūyāt iti na asya vacanam pramāṇam iti tat iha api kim na pratyavekṣyate sambhavati na vā iti 
[168,09^3]	saḥ eva upadiśan upaplavāt vedam veda artham vā anyathā api upadiśet iti śrūyante hi kaiścid puruṣaiḥ utsanna uddhṛtāni śākhā antarāṇi idānīm api kānicid virala adhyetṛkāṇi tadvat pracura adhyetṛkāṇām api kasmiṃścid kāle kathaṃcid saṃhāra sambhavāt punar sambhāvita puruṣa pratyayāt pracurata upagamana sambhāvanā sambhavāt teṣām ca punar pratānayitṝṇām kadācid adhīta vismṛta adhyanānām anyeṣām vā sambhāvana abhraṃśa bhaya ādinā anyathā upadeśa sambhavāt tad pratyayāt ca tad bhaktānām avicāreṇa pratipatteḥ bahuṣu adhyetṛṣu sambhāvitāt puruṣāt bahulam pratipatti darśanāt tatas api kathaṃcid vipralambha sambhavāt kim ca 
[168,09^4]	parimita vyākhyātṛ puruṣa paraṃparām eva ca atra bhavatām api śṛṇumaḥ tatra kaścid dviṣṭa ājña dhūrtānām anyatamaḥ syāt api iti anāśvāsaḥ tasmāt na apauruṣeyāt vyākhyānāt na api sāmayikāt loka vyavahārāt veda artha siddhiḥ asāmayika tve api nānā arthānām śabdānām vyavahāre darśanāt kasyacid aprasiddhārthasya aprasiddhasya vā punar vyutpatti darśanena sarvatra tad āśaṅkā nivṛtteḥ sarveṣām yathārtha niyoge api avaiguṇyena yathāsamayam pratīti jananāt iṣṭa aniṣṭayoḥ aviśeṣāt aviśiṣṭānām sarva artheṣu ekam artham atyakṣa saṃyogam anatyakṣa darśini puruṣa sāmānye kaḥ vivecayet yatas lokāt pratītiḥ syāt api ca svayam api ayam na sarvatra prasiddhim anusarati yasmāt 
[169,25_169,26^1]	svarga uḥ vaśya ādi śabdaḥ ca dṛṣṭaḥ arūḍha artha vācakaḥ anena eva nirvarṇyamānaḥ manuṣya atiśāyi puruṣa viśeṣa niketaḥ ati mānuṣa sukha adhiṣṭhānaḥ nānā upakaraṇaḥ svargaḥ tat nivāsinī apsarāḥ urvaśī nāma iti loka vādaḥ tam anādṛtya anyām eva artha kalpanām ayam kurvāṇaḥ śabda antareṣu katham prasiddhim pramāṇayet tatra avirodhāt abhyupagamaḥ iti ced na atra api atīndriye virodha asiddheḥ anyatra api avirodhasya duranvayatvāt viruddhām api agnihotrāt svarga avāptim māndyāt ayam na lakṣayet api virodha avirodhau ca bādhaka sādhaka pramāṇa vṛttī te ca atyakṣe na abhimate tat katham tad vaśāt pratītiḥ na ca vacana vṛtteḥ eva avirodhaḥ anyatra api prasaṅgāt 
[169,26^2]	apauruṣeyaḥ āgamaḥ tasya pravādāt artha siddhiḥ tatra punar virodha cintāyām anāśvāsaḥ āgame syāt sati api tasmin atatha abhāvāt arthasya apramāṇa vṛtteḥ anyasya api śaṅkanīya tvāt yat uktam agnihotram juhuyāt svarga kāmaḥ iti atra śva māṃsa bhakṣaṇa deśanā vikalpaḥ bhavatu iti sa na bhavati pradeśa antareṣu tathā tasya carcanāt na tasya artha aparijñānāt pradeśa antareṣu api tathāvidha artha kalpanāyāḥ anivārya tvāt yadi hi kvacid vidita arthaḥ ayam apauruṣeyaḥ śabdarāśiḥ syāt tadā tatas artha pratītiḥ syāt te tu bāhulye api andhāḥ eva sarve iti yatheṣṭam praṇīyante tasmāt 
[170,12_170,17]	śabda antareṣu tādṛkṣu tādṛśī eva astu kalpanā yādṛśī agnihotram juhuyāt svarga kāmaḥ iti asya vākyasya api ca prasiddhiḥ ca nṛṇām vādaḥ pramāṇam sa ca naḥ iṣyate tatas ca bhūyas artha gatiḥ kim etat dviṣṭa kāmitam na prasiddhiḥ nāma anyāḥ anyatra jana pravādāt te ca sarve janāḥ rāga ādi avidyā parīta tvāt asambhāvanīya yāthātathya vacanāḥ tat eṣām pravādaḥ na pramāṇam na hi kasyacid api samyak pratipatteḥ abhāve bāhulyam arthavat bhavati pāraśīka mātṛ mithi ā ācāra vat teṣām eva puruṣāṇām vacanāt punar parokṣa artha sampratipattiḥ iti katham tat eva yugapad dveṣyam ca kāmyam ca 
[171,02_171,05]	atha prasiddhim ullaṅghya kalpane na nibandhanam prasiddheḥ apramāṇa tvāt tad grahe kim nibandhanam prāpta pratilomanena anyatra pravṛttiḥ guṇa doṣa sandarśanena yuktāḥ iti prasiddheḥ anvayaḥ iti ced na prāpteḥ pramāṇa vṛtti lakṣaṇa tvāt yat kiṃcana grahaṇam hi prasiddhim apramāṇayataḥ tad mukhena pratītiḥ nyāyāt prāpti pratiṣedhāt tulyā sva para vikalpayoḥ ubhayathā api vṛttiḥ iti kaḥ prasiddhau anurodhaḥ api ca iyam
[171,11_171,16]	utpāditā prasiddhyai eva śaṅkā śabda artha niścaye yasmāt nānā artha vṛtti tvam śabdānām tatra dṛśyate na prasiddheḥ eka artha niścayaḥ śabdānām tatas eva śaṅkā utpatteḥ nānā arthāḥ hi śabdāḥ loke dṛśyante lokavādaḥ ca pratītiḥ atas eva nānā arthāḥ iti tatas eka artha niyamaḥ na yuktaḥ anyathā asambhava abhāvāt nānā śakteḥ svayam dhvaneḥ avaśyam śaṅkayā bhāvyam niyāmakam apaśyatām 
[171,18]	iti antaraślokaḥ tasmāt avidita artha vibhāgeṣu śabdeṣu ekam artham atyakṣa saṃyogam anālambana samāropam viniścitya vyācakṣāṇaḥ jaiminiḥ tad vyājena svam eva matam āha iti na tīrthakara antarāt asya viśeṣam paśyāmaḥ tathā hi tad artha vacana vyāpāra śūnyasya tad samāropeṇa abhidhānam na sva vacanam atiśete tad kāriṇā kevalam mithyā vinīta tā eva ātmanaḥ samuddyotitā syāt tathā hi 
[171,25_172,09]	eṣa sthāṇuḥ ayam mārgaḥ iti vakti iti kaścana anyaḥ svayam bravīmi iti tayoḥ bhedaḥ parikṣyatām nirabhiprāya vyāpāra vacane sthāṇau samāropya upadiśataḥ svatantrasya vā svayam vacana upagame na kaścid viśeṣaḥ anyatra jaḍasya pratipatti māndyāt api ca eka artha niyame sati enam jaiminiḥ jānīyāt saḥ eva śabdasya sarvatra yogyasya eka artha dyotane niyamaḥ kutas na hi śabdasya kaścid arthaḥ svabhāva niyataḥ sarvatra yogya tvāt ayogya tve ca tat apracyuteḥ avidheyasya puruṣāṇām kvacid upanayana apanayanā sambhavāt jñātāḥ vai atīndriyāḥ kena vivakṣā vacanāt ṛte 
[172,10]	puruṣa praṇīte hi śabde kayācid vivakṣayā sa tām kadācid kvacid nivedayet api iti vivakṣā pūrvakānām śabdānām artha niyamaḥ pratīyeta api apauruṣeye tu vidyamānaḥ api artha niyamaḥ katham vijñeyaḥ svabhāva bhedasya abhāvāt sati vā pratyakṣasya svayam pratīti prasaṅgāt apratyakṣe api kenacid jñātum aśakya tvāt na ca asti kaścid viśeṣaḥ sarva śabdāḥ hi sarva artha pratyāsatti viprakarṣa rahitāḥ tatas teṣām
[172,17_172,19]	vivakṣā niyame hetuḥ saṃketaḥ tad prakāśanaḥ apauruṣeye sā na asti tasya sā ekārtha tā kutas vivakṣayā hi śabdaḥ arthe niyamyate na svabhāvataḥ tasya kvacid apratibandhena sarvatra tulya tvāt yatra api pratibandhaḥ tad abhidhāna niyama abhāvāt sarva śabdaiḥ karaṇānām abhidhāna prasaṅgāt tasmāt vivakṣā prakāśanāya abhiprāya nivedana lakṣaṇaḥ saṃketaḥ kriyate apauruṣeye tu na vivakṣā na saṃketaḥ kasyacid abhiprāya abhāvāt iti na niyamaḥ na tat jñānam 
[172,25_173,02]	svabhāva niyame anyatra na yojyeta tayā punar yadi saṃketa nirapekṣaḥ svabhāvataḥ eva artheṣu śabdaḥ nilīnaḥ syāt uktam atra apratibandhāt aniyamaḥ iti api ca svābhāvike vācya vācaka bhāve na punar vivakṣayā yatheṣṭam niyujyeta saṃketaḥ ca nirarthaḥ syāt na hi svabhāva bhedaḥ indriya gamyaḥ sva pratītau paribhāṣā ādikam apekṣate nīla ādi bheda vat tad apekṣa pratītayaḥ tu na vastu svabhāvāḥ kim tarhi sāmayikā rāja cihna ādi vat yaḥ ca sāmayikaḥ sa svabhāva niyataḥ ayuktaḥ tasya icchā vṛtteḥ atas eva saṃketāt svabhāva viśeṣasya
[173,07_173,13]	 vyaktau ca niyamaḥ kutas sva icchā vṛttiḥ saṃketaḥ saḥ iha eva kartum śakyate na anyatra iti naḥ uparodhaḥ asti sa ca puruṣaiḥ sva icchayā kriyamāṇaḥ tam eva svabhāvam vyanakti na anyam iti na niyamaḥ asti yatra svātantryam icchāyāḥ niyamaḥ nāma tatra kaḥ dyotayet tena saṃketaḥ naḥ iṣṭām eva asya yogyatām iti antaraślokaḥ 
[173,14_173,20]	yasmāt kila īdṛśam satyam yathā agniḥ śītanodanaḥ vākyam veda eka deśa tvāt anyat api aparaḥ abravīt anyaḥ tu apauruṣeyam āgama lakṣaṇam parityajya anyathā prāmāṇyam vedasya sādhayitu kāmaḥ prāha avitathāni veda vākyāni yatra apratipattiḥ veda eka deśa tvāt yathā agniḥ himasya bheṣajam iti ādi vākyam iti tasya idam rasavat tulya rūpa tvāt eka bhāṇḍe ca pāka vat śeṣavat vyabhicāri tvāt kṣiptam nyāya vidā īdṛśam 
[173,22]	svayam īdṛśam ācāryeṇa anumānam naiyāyi kaśeṣa vat anu māna vyabhicāram udbhāvayatā tulya rūpa tayā phalānām tulya rasa sādhana vat ekasthālī antargamāt dṛṣṭa vat adṛṣṭa taṇḍula pāka sādhana vat ca asādhanam uktam tat asādhana tva nyāyaḥ ca pūrvam eva uktaḥ uktam ca idam āgama lakṣaṇam asmābhiḥ tat tu sarvasya śakya vicārasya viṣayasya yathāsvam pramāṇena vidhi pratiṣedha viśuddhau na antarīyaka tva abhāve api śabdānām artheṣu varam saṃśayitasya vṛttiḥ tatra kadācid avisaṃvāda sambhavāt na tu anyatra dṛṣṭa pramāṇa uparodhasya puruṣasya pravṛttiḥ iti yaḥ punar prākṛta viṣayasya vahneḥ śīta pratighāta sāmarthyasya abhidhānam satya artham upadarśya sarvam satya artham āha śāstram śakya paricchede api viṣaye pramāṇa virodhāt bahutaram ayuktam api nityasya puṃsaḥ kartṛ tvam nityān bhāvān atīndriyān 
[174,08_174,14^1]	aindriyān viṣamam hetum bhāvānām viṣamām sthitim nivṛttim ca pramāṇābhyām anyat vā vyasta gocaram viruddham āgama apekṣeṇa anumānena vā vadat virodham asamādhāya śāstra artham ca apradarśya saḥ satya artham pratijānānaḥ jayet dhārṣṭyena bandhakīm apracyuta anutpanna pūrva apara rūpaḥ pumān kartā krameṇa karmaṇām karma phalānām ca bhoktā samavāyi kāraṇa adhiṣṭhāna bhāva ādinā iti āha vedaḥ tat ca ayuktam iti āvedita prāyam nitya tvam ca keṣāṃcid bhāvānām akṣaṇikasya vastu dharma atikramāt ayuktam apratyakṣāni eva hi sāmānya ādīni pratyakṣāni janma sthiti nivṛttīḥ ca viṣamāḥ padārthānām anādheya viśeṣasya prāk akartuḥ para apekṣayā janaka tvam niṣpatteḥ akārya rūpasya āśraya vaśena sthānam kāraṇāt ca vināśaḥ iti ādikam anyat api pratyakṣa anumānābhyām prasiddhi viparyayam āgama āśrayeṇa ca anumānena bādhitam agni hotra ādeḥ pāpa śodhana sāmarthya ādikam 
[174,14^2]	tasya evaṃvādinaḥ vedasya sarvatra śāstra śarīre pramāṇa virodham apratisamādhāya sambandha anuguṇa upāya puruṣa artha abhidhānāni ca śāstra dharmān apradarśya atyanta prasiddha viṣaya satya abhidhāna mātreṇa prajñā prakarṣa durava gaha gahane api niratyayatām sādhayitu kāmaḥ bandhakīm api prāgalbhyena vijayate kācid kila bandhakī svayam svāminā vipratipatti sthāne dṛṣṭvā upālabdhā sā tam pratyuvāca paśyata mātar puruṣasya vaiparītyam mayi dharmapatnyām pratyayam akṛtvā ātmīyayoḥ naḥ itara abhidhānayoḥ jala budbudayoḥ karoti tena jaratkāṇena grāmya kāṣṭha hārakeṇa prārthitā api na saṃgatā rūpa guṇa anurāgena kila mantri mukhya dārakam kāmaye aham iti evaṃjātīyakam etat api vahneḥ śīta pratīkāra vacanena dṛṣṭa pramāṇa virodhasya api atyanta parokṣe arthe avisaṃvāda anumānam 
[175,05_175,07]	sidhyet pramāṇam yadi evam apramāṇam atha iha kim na hi ekam na asti satya artham puruṣe bahu bhāṣiṇi yathā idam ati duṣkaram atyanta satya abhidhānam tathā atyanta asatya abhidhānam api tatra ekasya vacanasya kathaṃcid saṃvādena aviśiṣṭasya tad vacana rāśeḥ tathā abhāve na kaścid puruṣaḥ anāptaḥ syāt api ca 
[175,11_175,13]	na ayam svabhāvaḥ kāryam vā vastūnām vaktari dhvaniḥ na ca tad vyatiriktasya vidyate avyabhicāritā na tāvat etat vacanam vācyānām svabhāvaḥ na api eṣām kāryam tad abhāve api vaktuḥ vivakṣā mātreṇa bhāvāt na ca anyaḥ kaścid kasyacid avyabhicārī vyabhicāre ca tatas anyathā api tad sambhavāt tad bhāvāt tad pratītiḥ ayuktā 
[175,17_175,21]	pravṛttiḥ vācakānām ca vācya dṛṣṭi kṛtāḥ iti ced syāt etat kāryam eva vacanam vācakasya vācya darśana vṛtteḥ evam sati paraspara viruddha arthā katham ekatra sā bhavet yadi eṣa pratiniyamaḥ vācyam vastu antareṇa śabdaḥ na pravartate iti bhinneṣu pravādeṣu ekatra vastuni viruddha svabhāva upasaṃhāreṇa vacana vṛttiḥ na syāt na hi ayam sambhavaḥ asti ekaḥ śabdaḥ niṣparyāyam nityaḥ ca syāt anityaḥ ca iti 
[175,25_175,27]	vastubhiḥ naḥ āgamāḥ tena kathaṃcid na antarīyakāḥ pratipattuḥ prasidhyanti kutas tebhyaḥ artha niścayaḥ āgamam pramāṇam tad ādarśita artha pratipattaye ajñaḥ janaḥ samanveṣate samadhigata yāthātathyānām upadeśa anapekṣaṇāt ajñasya ca atīndriya guṇa puruṣa vivecane asāmarthyāt vacanānām samīhita artha sattām antareṇa api vṛttim paśyataḥ bhavitavyam eva adṛṣṭa vyabhicāra vacasām api puruṣāṇām vāci śaṅkayā kim yathārthāḥ na vā iti tena na yuktam anena kasyacid vacanena kiṃcid niścetum 
[176,05_176,06]	tasmāt na tad nivṛttyā api bhāva abhāvaḥ prasidhyati yat uktam sarva viṣaya tvāt āgamasya sati vastuni avisaṃvādena asya vṛtteḥ tad nivṛtti lakṣaṇa anupalabdhiḥ abhāvam sādhayati iti tat asya sarva viṣaya tve api vastu antareṇa āvṛttau syāt tat ca na asti tatas pratipattu kāmasya asiddhiḥ iti uktam 
[176,10_176,17]	tena asaṃniścaya phalāḥ anupalabdhiḥ na sidhyate tasmāt na pramāṇa traya nivṛttau api viprakṛṣṭeṣu abhāva niścayaḥ veda prāmāṇyam kasyacid kartṛ vādaḥ snāne dharma icchā jāti vāda avalepaḥ santāpa ārambhaḥ pāpa hānāya ca iti dhvasta prajñāne pañca liṅgāni jāḍye iti pramāṇa vārttike prathamaḥ paricchedaḥ
